# gr-qc [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [Inflation from Covariant Signature Change: A Geometric Mechanism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01274)
*Raghvendra Singh,Sergey Bondarenko*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出一种协变机制，通过度规符号（metric signature）从欧几里得（Euclidean）到洛伦兹（Lorentzian）区域的平滑变化，驱动一段有限持续时间的加速膨胀。该转变由沿类时迹（timelike congruence）的标量插值器（scalar interpolator）编码，产生于一个余维一（codimension-one）的超曲面上，该处度规退化但曲率不变量保持有限，因此该曲面是曲率正则的。利用这种协变延拓，可将延拓度规的爱因斯坦张量重写为局域化、依赖于插值器的有效源，从而得到一个在穿越附近支撑的纯几何应力张量。在洛伦兹区域，推导出一个与模型无关的局域加速判据：当插值器斜率超过由初始超曲面上的外曲率和空间里奇曲率（Ricci curvature）确定的临界值时，暴胀持续；当该不等式首次达到饱和时，暴胀结束。标准平滑剖面（tanh、广义逻辑函数和幂律/反正切函数）可得到加速时段的固有时长闭合表达式，表明在固定几何数据下，剖面形状控制该时长。该构造提供了一条从正则欧几里得起源到早期洛伦兹加速膨胀相的无奇点、无暴胀子（inflaton-free）路径，且与无边界（no-boundary）型边界条件兼容。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统宇宙学模型中，宇宙的早期加速膨胀通常需要引入暴胀子（inflaton）标量场或依赖于奇点（singularity）假设。本文旨在探索一种无需引入暴胀子、无奇点的替代机制，利用度规符号的平滑转变来自然产生有限时段的加速膨胀，同时与无边界型边界条件兼容。

Method: 采用协变形式，通过沿类时迹的标量插值器编码度规符号从欧几里得到洛伦兹的平滑过渡；将延拓后的爱因斯坦张量重写为依赖于插值器的局域化有效源；基于外曲率和空间里奇曲率推导出一个局域加速判据；对tanh、广义逻辑函数和幂律/反正切等标准平滑剖面进行解析求解，得到加速时段的固有时长。

Result: 推导出一个模型无关的局域加速判据：暴胀持续当插值器斜率超过由初始超曲面外曲率和空间里奇曲率确定的临界值。标准平滑剖面的闭合表达式表明，在固定几何数据下，剖面形状直接控制加速时段的固有时长。该构造在曲率正则的超曲面上产生一个纯几何的有效应力张量，支持从欧几里得到洛伦兹区域的平滑过渡。

Conclusion: 该构造提供了一种无奇点、无暴胀子的宇宙早期加速膨胀机制，其起源来自正则欧几里得区域，过渡到洛伦兹加速膨胀相，并与无边界型边界条件相容。这为理解宇宙暴胀的几何起源提供了一条新的理论路径。

Abstract: We present a covariant mechanism in which a smooth change of metric signature, from a Euclidean to a Lorentzian regime, drives a finite interval of accelerated expansion. The transition, encoded by a scalar interpolator along a timelike congruence, occurs on a codimension-one hypersurface where the continued metric is degenerate but curvature invariants remain finite, so the surface is curvature-regular. Using this covariant continuation, we rewrite the Einstein tensor of the continued metric as a localized, interpolator-dependent effective source for the post-transition Lorentzian branch, yielding a purely geometric stress tensor supported near the crossing. In the Lorentzian regime, we derive a model-independent, local criterion for acceleration: inflation persists while the interpolator's slope exceeds a critical value fixed by the extrinsic curvature and the spatial Ricci curvature on the initial hypersurface, and ends when this inequality is first saturated. Standard smooth profiles (tanh, generalized logistic, and power-law/arctan) admit closed-form expressions for the proper-time duration of the accelerated epoch, showing that, for fixed geometric data, the profile shape controls this duration. The construction provides a non-singular, inflaton-free route from a regular Euclidean origin to an early Lorentzian phase of accelerated expansion, in a manner compatible with no--boundary--type boundary conditions.

</details>


### [2] [Hypersurface Anchored Variational Principle for General Relativity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01285)
*Prasanta Sahoo*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种广义相对论（General Relativity）的变分推广，通过添加一个与嵌入类空超曲面（embedded spacelike hypersurface）锚定的微分同胚不变泛函（diffeomorphism invariant functional），导出了带有局域分布贡献的爱因斯坦方程以及确定允许嵌入的锚定方程（anchoring equation）。该构造不引入额外的传播体引力自由度，且在椭圆性和可逆性假设下，锚定超曲面具有局部持久性和线性稳定性。该锚定条件与局部切片规范条件（gauge conditions）一般不等价，因此定义了一个真正的变分约束而非坐标选择。在正则形式中，动量约束保持标准形式，而哈密顿约束则获得一项超曲面支持的贡献；相应的涂抹生成元在弱意义上闭合，仅在局域分布表面贡献处偏离狄拉克代数（Dirac algebra）。在均匀宇宙学中，该局域项在锚定面上诱导匹配条件，允许膨胀率的有限跃迁，同时保持跃迁超曲面外的标准演化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于变分法对广义相对论进行扩展，构造一个在嵌入类空超曲面上锚定的泛函，从而在经典解空间中定义一个受约束的扇区（constrained sector），该扇区包含至少一个满足锚定方程的嵌入超曲面，以探索新的引力动力学特征。

Method: 在爱因斯坦-希尔伯特作用量（Einstein-Hilbert action）中补充一个与时空度量独立变分的嵌入类空超曲面支持的微分同胚不变泛函，从而导出包含局域分布贡献的爱因斯坦方程以及决定允许嵌入的锚定方程。

Result: 体场方程在超曲面之外保持标准的二阶主结构，且未引入额外的传播体引力自由度；在椭圆性和可逆性假设下，锚定超曲面具有局部持久性和线性稳定性；锚定条件与局部切片规范条件一般不等价；正则形式中哈密顿约束获得超曲面支持项，涂抹生成元在弱意义下仅在局域分布表面贡献处偏离狄拉克代数；均匀宇宙学中，锚定面诱导匹配条件，允许膨胀率的有限跃迁。

Conclusion: 该构造定义了广义相对论经典解空间的一个受约束扇区，其中超曲面的锚定条件代表一种真正的变分约束，而非坐标选择；在均匀宇宙学中，该方案允许在锚定面上实现有限膨胀率跃迁，为标准演化之外提供了新的物理可能性。

Abstract: A hypersurface anchored variational extension of General Relativity is formulated in which the Einstein-Hilbert action is supplemented by a diffeomorphism invariant functional supported on an embedded spacelike hypersurface whose embedding is varied independently of the spacetime metric. The resulting Euler-Lagrange system consists of the Einstein equations with a localized distributional contribution together with an anchoring equation determining admissible embeddings. For the admissible class of hypersurface functionals considered here, the bulk field equations retain the standard second order principal structure away from the hypersurface and no additional propagating bulk gravitational degrees of freedom are introduced. Under ellipticity and invertibility assumptions, local persistence and linear stability of anchoring hypersurfaces follow from standard implicit function and elliptic estimates. The anchoring condition is generically inequivalent to local slicing gauge conditions and therefore defines a genuine variational restriction rather than a coordinate choice. In the canonical formulation, the momentum constraints retain their standard form, whereas the Hamiltonian constraint acquires a hypersurface supported term. The corresponding smeared generators close in the weak sense: the Dirac algebra is recovered in the bulk, with deviations confined to localized distributional surface contributions. The construction therefore defines a constrained sector of the classical solution space of General Relativity consisting of spacetimes that admit at least one embedded hypersurface satisfying the anchoring equation. In homogeneous cosmology, the localized term induces matching conditions across the anchoring surface, allowing finite transitions in the expansion rate while preserving standard evolution away from the transition hypersurface.

</details>


### [3] [Impact of Spacecraft Orbit Uncertainties and Velocity Mismodeling on the LISA Gravitational-Wave Response](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01318)
*Lorenzo Speri,Olaf Hartwig,Waldemar Martens,Oliver Jennrich,Eric Joffre,Michele Armano,Martin Hewitson,Nora Lützgendorf*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文首次系统研究了激光干涉空间天线（LISA）轨道确定不确定性对引力波响应的影响，发现航天器轨道不确定性在高频段最差失配度低于10⁻⁷，而忽略航天器速度在约10⁻⁴ Hz频段造成约10⁻⁴量级的失配度，对银河系双星系统参数估计偏差小于1-σ。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LISA数据分析研究通常假设航天器轨道完全已知，但实际轨道确定过程会引入航天器位置和速度的不确定性，需量化这些不确定性如何传播到探测器输出并影响引力波数据分析。

Method: 利用失配度（mismatch）量化LISA响应知识中的误差，分析航天器轨道不确定性及忽略航天器速度对响应的影响，并通过银河系双星系统参数估计验证偏差程度。

Result: 航天器轨道不确定性在高频段对LISA响应知识影响最大，最差失配度低于10⁻⁷；忽略航天器速度在约10⁻⁴ Hz频段影响最大，失配度约10⁻⁴量级；对于信噪比（SNR）=200、频率10⁻⁴ Hz、观测一年的银河系双星，忽略速度导致参数估计偏差小于1-σ。

Conclusion: 该工作首次完整刻画了从引力波应变（gravitational wave strain）经探测器输出到参数估计的误差传播路径，为LISA实际数据分析中轨道不确定性的处理提供了定量依据。

Abstract: The Laser Interferometer Space Antenna (LISA) is a space-based gravitational wave observatory that consists of three spacecraft in a near-equilateral triangular formation. The spacecraft orbits are typically assumed to be perfectly known in LISA data analysis studies, but in reality, the orbit determination process introduces uncertainties in the spacecraft positions and velocities. In this work, we investigate how these uncertainties propagate into the LISA detector output and the impact of neglecting the spacecraft velocities. We quantify these errors in the knowledge of the LISA response using mismatches and discuss the implications for gravitational wave data analysis. We find that spacecraft orbit uncertainties impact the LISA response knowledge at high frequencies with worst mismatch below $10^{-7}$. The effect of neglecting the spacecraft velocities is largest at frequencies around $10^{-4}$ Hz with mismatches of order $10^{-4}$. For a galactic binary with frequency $10^{-4}$ Hz and SNR=200 observed for one year, we find that neglecting the spacecraft velocities in the response leads to less than 1-$σ$ biases in the parameter estimates. This work provides the first characterization of how errors in the LISA gravitational wave response propagate from gravitational wave strain through detector output to estimated parameters.

</details>


### [4] [Vacuum Cherenkov radiation in supercritical magnetic fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01419)
*Daniel Gálvez-García,Nora Bretón*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文比较了欧拉-海森伯理论（Euler-Heisenberg theory）在临界与超临界磁场下产生的切连科夫辐射（Cherenkov radiation），并将该辐射与带电粒子产生的同步辐射（synchrotron radiation）进行了对比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在极强电磁场下，真空折射率发生变化，光速降至低于c，导致超相对论带电粒子可能超过光速并诱发切连科夫辐射。本研究旨在比较不同磁场强度下该辐射的特性，并将其与同步辐射进行对比。

Method: 基于欧拉-海森伯理论（Euler-Heisenberg theory），分别对临界磁场（critical magnetic fields）和超临界磁场（supercritical magnetic fields）条件下的切连科夫辐射进行理论计算与比较，同时将其与同步辐射（synchrotron radiation）做对比分析。

Result: 给出了临界与超临界磁场下切连科夫辐射的对比结果，以及切连科夫辐射与同步辐射之间的比较结果。

Conclusion: 在极强电磁场下，真空折射率改变可使带电粒子产生切连科夫辐射，且该辐射特性随磁场强度（临界与超临界）而变化，并与同步辐射存在差异。

Abstract: In the presence of very intense electromagnetic fields, the refractive index of vacuum is modified such that light velocity is less than $c$ and ultrarelativistic charged particles can be faster than light and can induce Cherenkov radiation. We present the comparison of the Cherenkov radiation produced by the Euler-Heisenberg theory for critical and supercritical magnetic fields. We also make the comparison between the Cherenkov and the synchrotron radiation produced by the charged particles.

</details>


### [5] [Stability regions of glued wormholes with massless Kim-Lee backreacted spacetimes as interior](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01687)
*G. F. Akhtaryanova,R. Kh. Karimov,R. N. Izmailov,A. Bhattacharya*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了一种通过薄壳（thin shell）将零ADM质量（zero ADM mass）的内部Kim-Lee虫洞与外部分别为Schwarzschild真空和Reissner-Nordström时空粘合而成的“粘合虫洞”（glued wormhole）的稳定性，发现两种情况下稳定性区域几乎相似，尽管内部时空物理性质不同（一个带标量电荷，另一个带电电荷）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 零ADM质量的渐近虫洞（如Ellis-Bronnikov虫洞）在天体物理应用（如星系微引力透镜，galactic microlensing）中具有重要价值，但单独存在时对小扰动不稳定。因此，需要探索通过粘合构造使其稳定存在的可能性。

Method: 采用Garcia、Lobo和Visser提出的薄壳“质量”（mass）与“外力”（external force）约束的新概念，通过薄壳动力学界定粘合虫洞的稳定性区域。研究两类情况：零ADM质量内部为Kim-Lee虫洞，分别粘合到外部Schwarzschild真空时空和外部Reissner-Nordström时空。

Result: 两类粘合虫洞的稳定性区域几乎相似，尽管两种内部Kim-Lee时空物理性质截然不同（一种带标量电荷，另一种带电电荷）。详细分析了实现粘合虫洞稳定性的条件。

Conclusion: 零ADM质量的内部虫洞可以作为粘合虫洞的内部伴侣而保持质量为零，并共享粘合虫洞的整体稳定性。通过薄壳动力学分析，两类不同内部时空的粘合虫洞展现出相似的稳定性区域。

Abstract: Asymptotic zero Arnowitt-Deser-Misner (ADM) mass wormholes, such as the zero-mass traversable Ellis-Bronnikov wormhole, are of great interest for astrophysical applications such as in the galactic microlensing. However, when considered individually, they are unstable to small perturbations. On the other hand, there is a possibility that they can be stable as an interior partner of a traversable glued wormhole obtained by suitably gluing the interior to the observationally relevant massive exterior spacetimes across spherically symmetric thin shells. Although the exterior spacetime has non-zero ADM mass, massless interior partner remains massless sharing the stability of the glued wormhole. The dynamics of the thin-shell then demarcates the stability regions of the glued wormhole that we wish to study here by employing the novel concepts of thin-shell "mass" and of "external force" constraints discovered by Garcia, Lobo and Visser. We shall consider two classes, where the zero ADM mass interior are Kim-Lee wormholes glued to the exterior Schwarzschild vacuum and Reissner-Nordström spacetime respectively. It turns out that the stability regions in both cases are almost similar although the two interior Kim-Lee spacetimes are physically very different, one scalar charged and the other electrically charged. The conditions under which the stability of glued wormholes could be achieved are analyzed in detail.

</details>


### [6] [Particle dynamics and quasi-periodic oscillations of a Reissner--Nordström-like black hole in Kalb--Ramond gravity under an external magnetic test field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01723)
*Faizuddin Ahmed,Ahmad Al-Badawi,Sardor Murodov,Bekzod Rahmatov,Javlon Rayimbaev*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了Kalb–Ramond引力中Reissner–Nordström型黑洞周围带电测试粒子在外部磁场下的动力学与准周期振荡（QPO），并利用GRO J1655–40、XTE J1550–564和M82 X-1的观测数据通过MCMC分析对模型参数进行约束，证实该带电KR黑洞模型能一致地再现观测到的双峰QPO对。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索Lorentz破缺效应和外部磁场对强引力环境下带电粒子运动与QPO特征的影响，并检验这类修正引力模型能否与天文观测数据（特别是QPO）自洽对应。

Method: 在Kalb–Ramond（KR）引力框架下，引入Lorentz破缺参数ℓ，构造带电Reissner–Nordström型黑洞时空；从无源Maxwell方程出发，在修正背景下构建外部磁场分布。推导运动方程、有效势、圆轨道条件以及轨道频率和径向epicycle频率；应用相对论进动模型（relativistic precession model）将上峰QPO对应轨道频率、下峰对应近星点进动频率；利用三颗天体（GRO J1655–40、XTE J1550–564、M82 X-1）的观测双峰QPO数据，通过马尔可夫链蒙特卡罗（Markov chain Monte Carlo）方法约束模型参数。

Result: 黑洞电荷Q/M、KR参数ℓ、带电粒子比电荷ε和磁耦合参数β=bM共同影响最内稳定圆轨道（ISCO）位置和QPO频率。后验约束表明，给定参数范围内，带外部磁场的带电KR黑洞模型能够一致地再现观测双峰QPO对。

Conclusion: QPO观测可以作为探测Lorentz破缺黑洞几何和强引力电磁效应的有效现象学工具。

Abstract: We investigate the dynamics of charged test particles and quasi-periodic oscillations around a Reissner--Nordström-like black hole in Kalb--Ramond (KR) gravity in the presence of an external magnetic test field. The KR background introduces a Lorentz-violating parameter $\ell$, which modifies the spacetime geometry, horizon structure, circular orbits, and characteristic frequencies of particle motion. In contrast to the standard Wald-type prescription, the magnetic-field configuration is constructed from the source-free Maxwell equation on the charged KR background, allowing the magnetic profile to be consistently adapted to the modified geometry. We derive the equations of motion, the effective potential, the conditions for circular orbits, and the orbital and radial epicyclic frequencies of charged particles. The results show that the black-hole charge $Q/M$, the KR parameter $\ell$, the specific particle charge $ε$, and the magnetic coupling $β=bM$ jointly affect the innermost stable circular orbit (ISCO) and the quasi-periodic oscillation (QPO) frequencies. We then apply the obtained frequencies to the relativistic precession model, where the upper QPO frequency is identified with the orbital frequency and the lower one with the periastron-precession frequency. Using the observed twin-peak QPO data of GRO J1655--40, XTE J1550--564, and M82 X-1, we perform a Markov chain Monte Carlo analysis to constrain the model parameters. The obtained posterior constraints indicate that the charged KR black-hole model with an external magnetic field can consistently reproduce the observed QPO pairs within the adopted parameter ranges. These findings suggest that QPO observations may serve as a useful phenomenological tool for probing Lorentz-violating black-hole geometries and electromagnetic effects in strong-gravity environments.

</details>


### [7] [Classical and Loop Quantum Cosmology of Interacting Dark Energy: A Dynamical System Analysis with Superfluid Dark Matter and Dust Matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01724)
*Mohd Shahalam,K. Yerzhanov,G. Bauyrzhan,P. K. Dhankar*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在经典爱因斯坦引力与圈量子宇宙学框架下，研究相互作用的暗能量（dark energy）与暗物质（dark matter）的宇宙学动力学，发现暗物质性质与量子引力效应显著改变了相空间的渐近演化行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解暗物质属性与量子引力修正如何影响相互作用暗区（interacting dark-sectors）的宇宙学动力学，特别是相空间中的临界点性质与渐近演化行为。

Method: 在经典爱因斯坦引力（Classical Einstein Gravity）与圈量子宇宙学（Loop Quantum Cosmology, LQC）中，分别引入超流暗物质（superfluid dark matter）与标准无压流体两种暗物质模型，以及广义非线性态方程与常态方程两种暗能量模型，并采用两个唯象相互作用项Q=α\dotρ_m和Q=β\dotρ_d描述暗区能流转移，通过相空间稳定性分析研究动力学行为。

Result: 经典引力下，无压物质模型存在稳定的晚期吸引子（attractor），而超流暗物质模型仅存在鞍点（saddle）与非双曲临界点（non-hyperbolic critical point）。在LQC中，量子几何修正以非奇异量子反弹（quantum bounce）替代大爆炸奇点，且经典无压物质模型的稳定吸引子消失，所有相互作用模型仅剩鞍点与非双曲临界点。

Conclusion: 暗物质态方程性质与圈量子宇宙学中的量子几何修正均对相互作用暗区的渐近演化有显著影响，二者共同决定了相空间临界点的稳定性特征。

Abstract: We study the cosmological dynamics of interacting dark energy and dark matter in Classical Einstein Gravity and Loop Quantum Cosmology. Two dark matter scenarios are considered: superfluid dark matter described by a generalized cubic equation of state and the standard pressureless fluid. The dark energy component is modeled using both a generalized nonlinear equation of state and a constant equation of state. We examine two phenomenological interaction terms, $Q=α\dotρ_m$ and $Q=β\dotρ_d$, which govern the energy transfer between the dark sectors. In classical gravity, the pressureless matter model exhibits stable late-time attractors, whereas the superfluid dark matter model admits only saddle and non-hyperbolic critical points. Extending the analysis to Loop Quantum Cosmology, quantum geometric corrections replace the Big Bang singularity with a nonsingular quantum bounce, and significantly modify the phase-space dynamics. As a result, the stable attractors of the classical pressureless matter model disappear, and all interacting models possess only saddle and non-hyperbolic critical points. These findings highlight the significant influence of both dark matter properties and quantum gravitational effects on the asymptotic evolution of interacting dark-sectors.

</details>


### [8] [Rotating Black Holes and the Kerr/CFT Correspondence in Einstein-Bumblebee Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01884)
*Yu-Qi Chen,Jin-Yang Shen,Hai-Shan Liu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在五维爱因斯坦-大黄蜂引力（Einstein-Bumblebee gravity）中构造了具有等角动量的旋转黑洞（带和不带宇宙学常数），并通过Wald形式论（Wald formalism）和Komar积分（Komar integral）两种方法研究其热力学性质。结果表明两种方法计算的守恒荷（质量、角动量、熵）相差一个仅由大黄蜂耦合（Bumblebee coupling）决定的常数前因子。进一步应用Kerr/CFT对应（Kerr/CFT correspondence）导出微观熵，发现其精确复现了Komar积分版本的熵，而非Wald熵。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在五维爱因斯坦-大黄蜂引力框架下构造具有等角动量的旋转黑洞，并系统比较Wald形式论与Komar积分两种热力学方法在该理论中的一致性，进而通过Kerr/CFT对应检验微观熵的相容性。

Method: 采用Wald形式论和Komar积分两种方法分别计算旋转黑洞的守恒荷与熵，并引入Kerr/CFT对应从微观视角导出熵。

Result: 两种热力学方法给出的守恒荷（质量、角动量、熵）相差一个仅由大黄蜂耦合决定的常数前因子；Kerr/CFT对应导出的微观熵与Komar积分版本的熵一致，而非Wald熵。

Conclusion: 在五维爱因斯坦-大黄蜂引力中，Komar积分与Kerr/CFT对应在熵的计算上一致，暗示该理论中Komar积分可能是更合适的热力学方法；Wald熵与微观熵的差异源于大黄蜂耦合的修正效应。

Abstract: We constructed rotating black holes with equal angular momentum in five dimensional Einstein-Bumblebee gravity with and without cosmological constant. Their thermodynamic properties are examined via two distinct methods: the Wald formalism and the Komar integral. Notably, the conserved charges, including mass, angular momentum, and entropy, computed from these two approaches differ by a constant prefactor that is solely determined by the Bumblebee coupling. Subsequently, we apply the Kerr/CFT correspondence to derive the microscopic entropy of these black holes and find that it precisely reproduces the entropy in Komar-integral version, rather than the Wald entropy.

</details>


### [9] [Chaotic behaviors of particles around the black hole with an anisotropic matter immersed in a magnetic field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01910)
*Khusan Alibekov,Hocheol Lee,Yovqochev Pahlavon,Bobomurat Ahmedov,Bum-Hoon Lee,Ahmadjon Abdujabbarov,Wonwoo Lee*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过Harrison变换（Harrison transformation）获得了爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦方程（Einstein-Maxwell equations）的一个精确解，描述了一个与各向异性物质共存并浸没在外磁场中的静态黑洞。研究发现，各向异性物质参数增大抑制局部混沌行为（由李雅普诺夫指数表征），而外磁场变化则通过庞加莱截面（Poincaré sections）呈现出引力-磁非线性相互作用导致的全局混沌行为定性转变。该研究为磁化黑洞时空中的不可积粒子运动提供了新理论框架，并可用于探测星系中心黑洞周围的等离子体磁场效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究对磁化黑洞时空中粒子混沌动力学的理解尚不充分，特别是各向异性物质与外磁场对混沌行为各自的贡献及其相互作用机制缺乏系统理论框架。

Method: 采用Harrison变换求解爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦方程，得到描述静态黑洞与各向异性物质共存于外磁场中的精确解；通过计算李雅普诺夫指数（Lyapunov exponent）量化局部混沌行为，并利用庞加莱截面分析全局混沌动力学特征。

Result: 各向异性物质参数增大会系统性地抑制局部混沌行为，表现为李雅普诺夫指数降低；外磁场变化则引发全局混沌行为的定性变化，庞加莱截面显示规则轨迹与混沌轨迹之间在非线性引力-磁相互作用下发生转变。

Conclusion: 各向异性物质与外磁场在塑造黑洞周围粒子混沌动力学中扮演不同但互补的角色；该结果为探索磁化黑洞时空中的不可积粒子运动及探测星系中心黑洞周围由等离子体效应产生的磁场提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: We present an exact solution to the Einstein-Maxwell equations that describes a static black hole coexisting with anisotropic matter immersed in an external magnetic field, obtained via the Harrison transformation. Our findings reveal that an increase in the anisotropic matter parameter systematically suppresses the local chaotic behavior, as indicated by a reduction in the Lyapunov exponent. Conversely, variations in the external magnetic field lead to qualitative changes in global chaotic behavior. This is analyzed through Poincaré sections, which demonstrate transitions between regular and chaotic trajectories resulting from the nonlinear gravitational-magnetic interactions. These factors play distinct yet complementary roles in shaping chaotic particle dynamics around black holes. This study would offer a new theoretical framework for exploring non-integrable particle motion within magnetized black hole spacetimes and for probing a black hole at the galactic center, where magnetic fields may arise from plasma effects surrounding astrophysical black holes.

### [10] [Phase Transitions with Lyapunov Exponents under Einstein and String Frames in Dilatonic Reissner--Nordström--AdS Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01912)
*Hocheol Lee,Bogeun Gwak*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了膨胀Reissner–Nordström–AdS黑洞中Lyapunov指数作为黑洞相变动力学探针的有效性。结果表明，尽管Lyapunov指数本身在共形框架变换下具有非平凡依赖性，但其捕获的相结构特征（如尖点行为和转变点）在爱因斯坦和弦框架下保持一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨Lyapunov指数是否能够作为黑洞相变（black hole phase transitions）的动力学探针，特别是在考虑共形框架（conformal frame）依赖性的情况下。

Method: 在爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-膨胀理论（Einstein–Maxwell–dilaton theory）框架下，分析了膨胀Reissner–Nordström–AdS黑洞的热力学量及带电试探粒子的Lyapunov指数，并在爱因斯坦框架（Einstein frame）和弦框架（string frame）下进行对比研究。

Result: Hawking温度和Wald熵在共形框架变换下保持不变，因此两框架下相结构相同。Lyapunov指数对大量粒子表现出非平凡框架依赖性，但在无质量极限下无框架依赖性。尽管Lyapunov指数本身依赖框架，其捕获的相结构特征（包括尖点行为和转变点）在两种框架下一致。

Conclusion: Lyapunov指数在共形框架下取值具有依赖性，但其揭示的临界结构在不同框架间保持不变，因此仍可作为黑洞相变的有效动力学探针。

Abstract: We investigate Lyapunov exponents as dynamical probes of black hole phase transitions in dilatonic Reissner--Nordström--AdS black holes within Einstein--Maxwell--dilaton theory. The thermodynamic quantities and the Lyapunov exponent of charged probe particles were analyzed in both the Einstein and string frames, thus providing a direct comparison between the thermodynamic phase structure of the black hole and that captured by the Lyapunov exponent. Thermodynamic quantities, including the Hawking temperature and Wald entropy, remained constant under conformal frame transformations, yielding identical phase structures in the two frames. In contrast, the Lyapunov exponent exhibited non-trivial frame dependence for massive probe particles due to dilaton coupling, while no frame dependence was found in the massless limit. Numerical analysis revealed that the phase structure features captured by the Lyapunov exponent, including characteristic cusp behavior and transition points, were independent of the choice of frame, despite the Lyapunov exponent itself being frame-dependent. Therefore, the Lyapunov exponent exhibited frame-dependent values, while the critical structure it captures remained constant across conformal frames.

### [11] [Neutron stars with primary scalar hair](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01937)
*Hamza Boumaza,Christos Charmousis,David Langlois,Etienne Ligout*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索退化高阶标量-张量（DHOST）引力理论中中子星解的性质，特别是原生标量毛（primary scalar hair）对星体结构的影响，并评估其与广义相对论（GR）预测的偏离程度。

Method: 求解修改后的托尔曼-奥本海默-沃尔科夫（TOV）方程组，采用多方物态方程（polytropic equation of state）和真实物态方程构建平衡位形，分析标量毛对度规、标量场轮廓及质量-半径关系的影响。

Result: 正标量电荷（positive scalar charges）导致中子星比广义相对论（GR）预测的更致密；超过某一临界阈值时，星体出现奇点（singularities）。标量毛的存在使质量-半径关系偏离GR的预测。

Conclusion: 观测结果可对DHOST理论中超出广义相对论（GR）效应的参数以及潜在标量毛（scalar hair）施加严格约束，从而为检验修改引力理论提供途径。

Abstract: We investigate static and spherically symmetric neutron star solutions endowed with primary scalar hair in a subfamily of Degenerate-Higher-Order-Scalar-Tensor (DHOST) theories of gravity. By solving the modified Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkoff (TOV) equations, we construct equilibrium configurations for polytropic and realistic equations of state and analyse the impact of the scalar hair on the stellar structure. We examine the resulting metric and scalar field profiles as well as the mass-radius relation, showing deviations from the predictions of General Relativity (GR). Positive scalar charges lead to more compact stars than in GR and, above a critical threshold, to singularities. Observations could therefore put stringent constraints on the parameters characterising the beyond-GR effects in these theories and their potential scalar hair.

</details>


### [12] [Boson Stars in Teleparallel Gravity with a Nonminimally Coupled Field: The Violation of Energy Conditions and Gravitational Waveforms from EMRIs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02017)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在teleparallel引力框架中引入非最小耦合，通过求解场方程获得玻色子星的基态与激发态静态球对称解；随后分析解的能条件（energy conditions）；并针对由该类玻色子星组成的极端质量比旋近（Extreme-Mass-Ratio Inspiral, EMRI）系统，计算其引力波信号的频域特征应变（frequency-domain characteristic strain）。

Result: 激发态解的能量密度可能出现负值，四种常用能条件不再满足；而所有研究的基态解能量密度为正，四种能条件均满足。EMRI系统的引力波频域特征应变位于LISA探测灵敏度范围内。

Conclusion: 基态玻色子星在非最小耦合teleparallel引力中满足所有能条件，具有物理可行性；其产生的EMRI引力波信号可被LISA探测，有望作为区分不同致密天体类型的观测线索。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate boson star models within the framework of teleparallel gravity with non-minimal coupling, and obtain static, spherically symmetric solutions for both the ground state and excited states. The results indicate that the energy density of the excited-state solutions can become negative. For these solutions, the four commonly used energy conditions are no longer satisfied. In contrast, for all the ground-state solutions we have studied, the energy density remains positive and all four energy conditions are consistently satisfied. Moreover, considering the importance of astrophysical observations, the gravitational-wave signals from Extreme-Mass-Ratio Inspirals (EMRIs) composed of these boson stars are investigated. Our results reveal that the frequency-domain characteristic strain of these waveforms falls within the detectability range of LISA, which can provide potential evidence for distinguishing compact astrophysical objects.

### [13] [Nonlocal correlations of fermionic entanglement in the spacetime of Einstein-Gauss-Bonnet black hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02039)
*Yifei Xu,Yanjun Chen,Qi Xiao,Xiaolong Gong*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 在爱因斯坦-高斯-博内特（EGB）黑洞时空中，研究了量子相干非局域优势（NAQC）和贝尔非局域性（BN）两种非经典关联度量，发现两者均随霍金温度升高而单调退化，且NAQC与BN的层级关系在EGB时空中仍然保持。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索弯曲时空（curved spacetimes）中的非经典关联，为量子信息理论与引力物理的交叉提供关键见解。

Method: 考虑两个观察者（Alice和Rob）初始共享最大纠缠贝尔态（Bell state），分别处于惯性克鲁斯卡尔坐标系（Kruskal frame）和非惯性类史瓦西坐标系（Schwarzschild-like frame），通过玻戈留波夫变换（Bogoliubov transformation）关联两坐标系下的场模式，推导费米子场的混合二分密度矩阵（mixed bipartite density matrix），得到NAQC和BN的解析表达式。

Result: NAQC和BN均随霍金温度（Hawking temperature）升高而单调退化；NAQC与BN之间的层级关系（hierarchical relationship）在EGB时空中仍然保持；高阶曲率修正（high curvature corrections）对量子资源存在显著影响。

Conclusion: 在EGB黑洞时空中，非经典关联（NAQC和BN）强烈依赖于霍金温度，且NAQC-BN的层级关系具有鲁棒性，这为理解弯曲时空量子资源退化机制提供了新视角。

Abstract: The investigation of nonclassical correlations in curved spacetimes offers key insights into the intersection of quantum information theory and gravitational physics. This paper studies two nonlocal correlation measures, non local advantage of quantum coherence (NAQC) and Bell nonlocality (BN) in a $d$-dimensional spherically symmetric Einstein-Gauss-Bonnet (EGB) black hole spacetime. We consider two observers (Alice and Rob) initially sharing a maximally entangled Bell state: Alice freely falls into the black hole (inertial Kruskal frame), while Rob accelerates outside the horizon (non-inertial Schwarzschild-like frame). The Unruh-Hawking effect modifies Rob's field modes, requiring Bogoliubov transformations to relate the two frames. We derive the mixed bipartite density matrix for fermionic fields and analytical expressions for NAQC and BN, which depend on Hawking temperature (itself governed by $α$, $d$, and $r_h$). Our results show both correlations degrade monotonically with increasing Hawking temperature, confirm the NAQC-BN hierarchical relationship persists in EGB spacetime, and highlighting the impact of high curvature corrections on quantum resources.

### [14] [The Direct Wave is Not a Meaningful Test of Horizon Properties](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02380)
*Anuj Kankani,Sean T. McWilliams*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过数值相对论应变数据证明，黑洞并合辐射中的“直接波（direct wave）”成分的频率与残余视界频率或表面引力无关（仅在χ_f≈0.7附近偶然交叉），其阻尼时间存在显著演化，因此基于直接波分析残余视界性质（包括检验霍金面积定律）的方法不可靠。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期研究发现黑洞并合辐射中存在一种非准正则模（non-quasinormal mode）成分，即直接波，其频率和阻尼时间被认为与残余视界（remnant horizon）性质相关，并已被用于分析GW250114事件及检验霍金面积定律（Hawking's area law）。本文旨在检验直接波与视界性质之间是否存在真实的物理关联。

Method: 采用数值相对论（numerical relativity）应变数据，分析直接波的瞬时频率与阻尼时间，并将其与视界频率（horizon frequency）及表面引力（surface gravity）进行对比；同时评估基于固定阻尼时间的单阻尼正弦模型（single damped sinusoid model）和基于视界性质的演化频率模型对直接波成分的适用性。

Result: 直接波频率与视界频率或表面引力不存在相关性，仅在残余自旋χ_f≈0.7附近（对应GW250114的自旋）存在偶然交叉；直接波的瞬时频率呈准稳定（quasi-stable）状态，但阻尼时间存在显著演化，因此固定阻尼时间的单阻尼正弦模型不适用；对于大残余自旋系统，基于视界性质的演化频率模型也无法描述直接波成分；若基于直接波解释的视界频率检验霍金面积定律，将导致错误的违反该定律的结论。

Conclusion: 直接波并非残余视界性质的可靠探针（reliable probe），基于直接波对霍金面积定律的检验结果不成立。

Abstract: Recently, a distinct non--quasinormal mode component of black hole binary merger radiation, named the direct wave, has been identified. The frequency and damping time of the direct wave have been associated with properties of the remnant horizon. This has led to direct-wave based analysis of GW250114, including a test of Hawking's area law. However, as we demonstrate here using numerical relativity strain data, the direct wave frequency is not correlated with the horizon frequency or surface gravity, other than an incidental crossing around $χ_f \approx 0.7$ corresponding closely to the remnant spin of GW250114. We show that while the instantaneous frequency of the direct wave is quasi-stable, the damping time shows significant evolution and therefore a single damped sinusoid model, containing a fixed damping time, is not appropriate. We further show that an evolving frequency model based on horizon properties also does not model the direct wave component for systems with large remnant spins. We demonstrate that testing Hawking's area law with a horizon frequency based on the direct wave interpretation will lead to apparent violations of Hawking's area law when no violation actually occurs. Our results therefore indicate that the direct wave is not a reliable probe of the remnant horizon's properties.

</details>


### [15] [Black Hole Persistence in Scalar Tensor Theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02409)
*Balkar Yildirim,Alan Albert Coley*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过构建微扰标量-张量解（scalar-tensor solution），研究位于非奇异反弹宇宙中的中心不均匀性（central inhomogeneity）所对应的黑洞能否持续存在。采用微扰展开方案，在辐射完美流体主导的反弹FLRW背景上引入广义McVittie几何描述的局部不均匀性，求解场方程至反弹点附近$η^4$阶，发现存在一个随反弹演化的小视界$r_h\sim d_0$，其持续通过反弹支持黑洞穿越宇宙反弹的解读。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将黑洞嵌入反弹宇宙学（bouncing cosmology）中，检验黑洞能否在宇宙经历非奇异反弹（nonsingular bounce）后仍然存活，从而探讨黑洞在反弹宇宙中的演化与存续问题。

Method: 采用微扰方案（perturbative scheme），设小参数$ε$，零阶由辐射完美流体驱动的空间平坦反弹FLRW时空求解；一阶通过广义McVittie几何引入中心不均匀性，将微扰编码于一阶度规和标量场函数中，允许各向异性流体（径向与切向压力），将场方程在反弹点$η=0$附近展开至$\mathcal{O}(η^4)$求解。

Result: 所得完美流体解包含三个任意函数，通过渐近FLRW条件约束；在保持反弹抛物线结构的初始条件下，积分常数$d_0$成为真正微扰参数（$d_0\to0$时所有微扰消失）。发现一个随反弹演化的小视界$r_h\sim d_0$，其在反弹前后演化不对称（non-symmetric about $η=0$）。

Conclusion: 该小视界持续通过反弹，支持黑洞可能经历宇宙反弹而存续的解读；视界尺度与$d_0$同量级，演化不对称表明反弹过程对黑洞结构有非对称影响。

Abstract: We construct a perturbative scalar-tensor solution describing a central inhomogeneity embedded in an evolving cosmological background, with the aim of studying black hole persistence through a nonsingular bounce. Scalar-tensor gravity provides a natural framework for realizing bouncing cosmologies, while the inclusion of a localized inhomogeneity makes the field equations substantially more difficult to solve. We therefore adopt a perturbative scheme, with perturbative parameter $ε$, in which the leading-order equations are solved by a spatially flat bouncing FLRW spacetime sourced by a radiation perfect fluid. At next order, a central inhomogeneity is introduced through a generalized McVittie geometry, with the perturbations encoded in the corresponding first-order metric and scalar-field functions. We first allow an anisotropic fluid with radial and tangential pressures, whose diagonal components solve the diagonal field equations. The field equations are solved as a series expansion up to $\mathcal{O}(η^4)$ near the bounce at $η=0$. The resulting perfect fluid solution contains three arbitrary functions which are constrained by requiring the spacetime to asymptote to FLRW as $r\to\infty$. With suitable initial conditions preserving the parabolic structure of the bounce, the integration constant $d_0$ emerges as the true perturbative parameter: all perturbations vanish as $d_0\to0$. Finally, we find a small evolving horizon, $r_h\sim d_0$, which we interpret as the horizon of the central inhomogeneity. Its persistence through the bounce supports the interpretation of a black hole surviving the cosmological transition, and its evolution is not symmetric about $η=0$.

</details>

# physics.atom-ph [[Back]](#toc)

### [16] [Identical-Particle Symmetry-Enabled Complete Coherent Control of Ultracold Atomic and Molecular Collisions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01620)
*Jing-Chen Zhang,Adrien Devolder,Timur V. Tscherbul,Paul Brumer,Yu Liu*

Main category: physics.atom-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明，全同粒子（identical particles）碰撞中的交换对称性（exchange symmetry）能够实现总散射截面（total scattering cross section）的对称性保护相干控制（symmetry-protected coherent control）。对于全同费米子，反对称化迫使所有散射通道完全相位同步（phase synchronization），达到最大控制可见度；全同玻色子虽仍有同步效应，但因交换卫星贡献导致可见度下降；可区分粒子则缺乏对称性强制锁相，可控性最低。作者以锂-锂碰撞体系为例，通过耦合通道量子散射计算加以验证，并指出该机制在全同粒子碰撞中具有广泛适用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前的相干控制方法（如直流电场或微波屏蔽）对同核分子（homonuclear molecules）等全同粒子体系失效或难以应用，亟需一种不依赖外场、基于内禀对称性的全新控制机制。

Method: 通过理论分析揭示交换对称性对散射通道相位的锁定机制，并利用耦合通道量子散射计算（coupled-channel quantum-scattering calculations）对$^{6}\mathrm{Li}$-$^{6}\mathrm{Li}$（全同费米子）、$^{7}\mathrm{Li}$-$^{7}\mathrm{Li}$（全同玻色子）和$^{6}\mathrm{Li}$-$^{7}\mathrm{Li}$（可区分粒子）三种体系进行对比验证。

Result: 全同费米子体系中，反对称化实现所有散射通道的完全相位同步，获得最大控制可见度（maximal control visibility）；全同玻色子因额外交换卫星贡献（exchange satellite contributions）致可见度降低；可区分粒子缺乏对称性锁相，可控性与可见度最低。全同粒子情形下，对称性强迫同步能在任意碰撞能量下实现对未态宇称（parity of the final state）的完全控制。

Conclusion: 交换对称性赋予全同粒子碰撞一种普适的相干控制机制，尤其适用于同核分子等现有外场方法无法操控的体系，为对称性保护的量子控制提供了新途径。

Abstract: We show that exchange symmetry in collisions of identical particles enables symmetry-protected coherent control of the total scattering cross section. For identical fermions, antisymmetrization enforces complete phase synchronization of the contributing scattering channels, yielding maximal control visibility. For identical bosons, synchronization persists but with reduced visibility due to additional exchange (satellite) contributions. Collisions of distinguishable particles lack this symmetry-imposed phase locking, leading to lower controllability and visibility. We elucidate these principles through coupled-channel quantum-scattering calculations for lithium-lithium collisions, comparing the $^{6}\mathrm{Li}$-$^{6}\mathrm{Li}$ (identical fermions), $^{7}\mathrm{Li}$-$^{7}\mathrm{Li}$ (identical bosons), and $^{6}\mathrm{Li}$-$^{7}\mathrm{Li}$ (distinguishable) systems. Furthermore, in the identical particle cases, symmetry-enforced synchronization enables full control over the parity of the final state at any collisional energy. This mechanism is broadly applicable to identical-particle collisions, including homonuclear molecules for which established approaches -- DC electric fields, or microwave shielding -- are ineffective or unavailable.

</details>

# cs.LG [[Back]](#toc)

### [17] [One More Time: Revisiting Neural Quantum States from a Reinforcement Learning Perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02292)
*Juan Agustín Duque,Sergio García Heredia,Vinicius Hernandes,Eliška Greplová,Thomas Spriggs,Aaron Courville,Anna Dawid*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出近端波函数优化（Proximal Wavefunction Optimization, PWO），一种用于神经量子态（NQS）训练的信任域算法。PWO将变分能量最小化建模为优势策略梯度问题，分别对振幅通道和相位通道进行裁剪约束，避免了矩阵求逆，在Ising和受阻J1-J2自旋系统中相比Adam、minSR和SPRING提升了稳定性和收敛速度，并成功微调了15亿参数的RWKV-7模型，将NQS优化规模推至此前工作的千倍以上。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 神经量子态（Neural Quantum States, NQS）中的自回归模型虽能从Born分布精确独立采样，但其优化方法仍存在不足：Adam可扩展但忽略函数空间几何，随机重配置（stochastic reconfiguration）虽具理论原则性但计算昂贵且在大模型中数值不稳定。本文旨在弥合这一差距，提出兼具可扩展性与理论保障的优化算法。

Method: 将变分能量最小化重新解释为Born分布上的优势策略梯度（advantage policy-gradient）问题，从而引入信任域优化。提出近端波函数优化（PWO），在振幅通道裁剪概率比变化、在相位通道限制相位增量，避免显式矩阵求逆，并允许多次更新复用一个样本批次。

Result: 在Ising和受阻J1-J2一维和二维自旋系统中，PWO在稳定性和实际时间收敛速度上优于Adam、minSR和SPRING。进一步将15亿参数的RWKV-7模型微调用于NQS优化，规模超过此前工作的三个数量级。

Conclusion: PWO有机结合了一阶优化的可扩展性与信任域算法的理论保证，为大规模NQS训练提供了一种高效且稳定的替代方案，并证明了NQS优化可以扩展到此前难以达到的模型规模。

Abstract: Neural quantum states (NQS) provide a flexible and scalable framework for approximating quantum many-body wavefunctions. Among NQS parameterizations, autoregressive models are especially attractive because they enable exact, independent sampling from the Born distribution, avoiding the autocorrelation and mixing issues of Markov chain methods. Yet their optimization remains comparatively underexplored: Adam is a scalable method but ignores function space geometry, while stochastic reconfiguration is principled but costly and numerically fragile in large models. To address this gap, we show that variational energy minimization can be viewed as an advantage policy-gradient problem over the Born distribution, motivating trust-region optimization for NQS training. We introduce Proximal Wavefunction Optimization (PWO), a principled trust-region algorithm that clips probability-ratio changes in the amplitude channel and phase increments in the phase channel. PWO avoids explicit matrix inversion, reuses samples across multiple updates, and combines the scalability of first-order optimization with theoretical guarantees. Across Ising and frustrated $J_1$-$J_2$ one- and two-dimensional spin systems, PWO improves stability and wall-clock convergence over Adam, minSR, and SPRING. Finally, we fine-tune a $1.5$B-parameter RWKV-7 model, demonstrating NQS optimization at a scale over three orders of magnitude beyond prior work.

</details>

### [18] [Towards triggerless four-dimensional detectors for High Energy Physics collider experiments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01496)
*Vladimir V. Gligorov*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本文综述了高能物理（HEP）旗舰对撞机实验（如LHC的CMS、ATLAS、LHCb）中数据量指数增长与皮秒级时间精度（picosecond timing）技术引入的趋势，探讨了时间测量与网络技术相结合如何可能推动未来探测器从头设计为无触发模式（triggerless），并反思了这种范式转换（paradigm shift）对物理研究的潜在益处。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前高能物理实验产生的数据量呈指数级增长（例如LHC实验每秒产生的数据占全球互联网总流量的十分之一以上），且增长趋势不减；同时皮秒级时间精度技术在HEP探测器中的应用日益普及，催生了实时处理与选择的新方法。因此，需系统审视时间测量与网络技术的融合如何推动下一代探测器架构的变革。

Method: 作者回顾了计划在CMS、ATLAS和LHCb实验未来升级中引入精密时间信息（precision timing information）的方案，并分析了时间技术与网络技术结合后，如何可能使未来探测器从底层设计为无触发模式（triggerless）。

Result: 论文指出，将皮秒级时间精度引入CMS、ATLAS和LHCb的升级中，是当前高能物理实验发展的重要方向；时间与网络技术的结合为未来从底层设计无触发（triggerless）探测器提供了可行性基础。

Conclusion: 时间测量与网络技术的协同发展有望推动高能物理探测器架构的根本性范式转换（paradigm shift），即从传统的触发系统转向无触发（triggerless）设计，从而带来显著的物理收益。

Abstract: High Energy Physics experiments at flagship colliders produce and process some of the biggest datasets on Earth, with the current generation of flagship experiments at the Large Hadron Collider producing more than a tenth of the world's total internet traffic every second. Moreover the quantities of data produced have increased exponentially over the past decades and this trend shows no sign of slowing down. In parallel, the use of picosecond timing is becoming more common in HEP detectors, enabling qualitatively new approaches to real-time processing and selections. I review the planned introduction of precision timing information into the upcoming upgrades of the CMS, ATLAS, and LHCb experiments. I discuss the ways in which the combination of timing and networking technology may enable future detectors to be designed as triggereless from the ground up, and reflect on the physics benefits of such a paradigm shift for the field.

</details>

Thwaites,S. Tilav,K. Tollefson,J. A. Torres,S. Toscano,D. Tosi,K. Upshaw,A. Vaidyanathan,N. Valtonen-Mattila,J. Valverde,J. Vandenbroucke,T. Van Eeden,N. van Eijndhoven,L. Van Rootselaar,J. van Santen,J. Vara,F. Varsi,M. Velazquez,M. Venugopal,M. Vereecken,S. Vergara Carrasco,S. Verpoest,D. Veske,A. Vijai,J. Villarreal,C. Walck,A. Wang,E. H. S. Warrick,C. Weaver,P. Weigel,A. Weindl,J. Weldert,A. Y. Wen,C. Wendt,J. Werthebach,M. Weyrauch,N. Whitehorn,C. H. Wiebusch,D. R. Williams,L. Witthaus,G. Wrede,X. W. Xu,J. P. Yanez,Y. Yao,E. Yildizci,S. Yoshida,F. Yu,S. Yu,T. Yuan,S. Yun-Cŕcamo,A. Zander Jurowitzki,A. Zegarelli,S. Zhang,Z. Zhang,P. Zhelnin,P. Zilberman,C. Zilleruelo Cañas*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本文提出WavePID，一种基于模板的对数似然比分类器，利用纳秒级脉冲时序信息提升IceCube中微子天文台在5–100 GeV能段的风味识别性能，展示了时序信息与形态学分类器的互补性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: IceCube中微子天文台（IceCube Neutrino Observatory）通过事件形态学（event morphology）识别中微子风味，但在5–100 GeV能区，稀疏的光子探测使得风味分类极具挑战性，而该能区对于振荡测量和标准模型外新物理（physics beyond the Standard Model）的搜索至关重要。

Method: 提出WavePID，一个基于模板的对数似然比分类器（template-based log-likelihood-ratio classifier），利用单个探测器模块上的纳秒级时序信息（nanosecond-scale timing），提取三个观测量：到重建顶点的距离（distance to the reconstructed vertex）、早期电荷分数（early-charge fraction）、以及模块间时间差（module-to-module time difference）。

Result: 在经先进图神经网络（graph neural network）筛选的级联富集样本（cascade-enriched sample）上评估，WavePID在级联纯度（cascade purity）和分类性能上均优于仅使用神经网络的方案。Geant4模拟将这一信号归因于μ子径迹（muon tracks）与电磁级联（electromagnetic showers）之间切伦科夫辐射几何（Cherenkov emission geometry）的差异。

Conclusion: 表明每个模块的脉冲时序（per-module pulse timing）携带与形态学分类器互补的风味识别信息，为低能中微子重建开辟了新的物理动机观测量（physics-motivated observable）。未来低能分类器和下一代中微子望远镜的探测器设计应充分利用纳秒级脉冲时序。

Abstract: The IceCube Neutrino Observatory, a cubic-kilometer detector at the South Pole, identifies neutrino flavor through event morphology. Sparse photon detection makes this classification particularly challenging in the 5--100~GeV regime, the energy range relevant for oscillation measurements and searches for physics beyond the Standard Model. We introduce WavePID, a template-based log-likelihood-ratio classifier that exploits nanosecond-scale timing on individual detector modules through three observables: the distance to the reconstructed vertex, the early-charge fraction, and the module-to-module time difference. Evaluated on a cascade-enriched sample selected by a state-of-the-art graph neural network, WavePID improves both cascade purity and classification performance over the neural network alone. This demonstrates that per-module pulse timing carries flavor-identification information complementary to morphology-based classifiers, opening a new physics-motivated observable for low-energy neutrino reconstruction. Geant4 simulations associate this signal with differences in Cherenkov emission geometry between muon tracks and electromagnetic showers. These results motivate exploiting nanosecond-scale pulse timing in future low-energy classifiers and in detector designs with improved per-module timing in next-generation neutrino telescopes.

</details>

# astro-ph.EP [[Back]](#toc)

### [20] [The influence of lunar tidal potential on clock frequencies at different positions on Earth](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01758)
*Hongbin Zhang,Yanyue Gao,Baocheng Zhang*

Main category: astro-ph.EP

TL;DR: 本文基于一种新方法，在地心费米坐标系（geocentric Fermi frame）中系统研究了月球潮汐势（lunar tidal potential）对位于地球不同位置时钟的分数频移（fractional frequency shift）的影响。结果表明，时钟间的经度差和纬度差均会改变频移，而月球经度和纬度的变化则分别影响频移的相位/幅度以及仅幅度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着时钟计时技术的进步，越来越小的时间差可以被区分，因此有必要研究地球不同位置时钟之间的分数频移。

Method: 提出一种新方法，在地心费米坐标系（geocentric Fermi frame）下，系统计算了微弱月球潮汐势（lunar tidal potential）对时钟分数频移的影响。

Result: 位于同一纬度的两个时钟，经度差会改变它们之间的分数频移；同一经度下纬度差也会产生类似现象。月球经度变化同时改变频移的相位和幅度，而月球纬度变化仅影响幅度。

Conclusion: 研究结果可为地球时钟的校准与同步（calibration and synchronization）提供有用参考信息。

Abstract: With the advancements in clock timing technology, increasingly smaller time differences can be distinguished. Therefore, it is critical to investigate the fractional frequency shift of clocks at different locations on Earth. In this paper, we study it systematically under the influence of a subtle lunar tidal potential based on a new method. Our calculations in the geocentric Fermi frame show that when two clocks are located at the same latitude, the longitude difference changes the fractional frequency shift between them. A similar phenomenon occurs when there is a difference in latitude between two clocks on the ground at the same longitude. Interestingly, when the Moon's longitude changes, the phase and amplitude of the lunar tidal fractional frequency shift between two clocks with the same longitude difference will change, while the change in the Moon's latitude only affects the amplitude of the fractional frequency shift of these two clocks. Our results provide useful information for the calibration and synchronization of clocks on Earth.

</details>

### [21] [On perturbations that preserve the connectivity properties in tree percolations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01291)
*Mirmukhsin Makhmudov,Ville Suomala*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文研究了无限局部有限树上的键逾渗（bond percolation）模型，在边保留概率受到依赖于边到根距离的扰动因子序列 {q_n} 扰动后，原模型是否仍保持（或不保持）无限连通性。在最小假设下证明了逾渗行为的定量稳定性，并将结果应用于 Erdős 相似性猜想（Erdős similarity conjecture）中关于康托集（Cantor sets）的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在无限局部有限树上的键逾渗模型中，当原始模型存在无限簇时，需要探究在何种扰动（0<q_n≤1）下该连通性得以保留；当原始模型不存在无限簇时，则研究在 q_n≥1 的扰动下该性质是否稳定。本文旨在回答这些稳定性问题，并将其应用于 Erdős 相似性猜想。

Method: 以无限局部有限树为图结构，将原边保留概率 p_e 替换为 min{1, q_{|e|} p_e}，其中 |e| 为边到根的距离，{q_n} 为正值扰动因子序列。分别对原始模型存在无限簇和不存在无限簇两种情形，在最小假设下分析逾渗行为的稳定性。

Result: 在仅对原始模型施加最小假设的条件下，无论原始模型是否允许无限簇，逾渗行为在面对满足相应条件的定量非平凡扰动（quantitative non-trivial perturbations）时均保持稳定。

Conclusion: 本文建立的稳定性结果适用于 Erdős 相似性猜想中关于康托集的问题，展示了逾渗模型中的扰动分析在经典猜想中的应用价值。

Abstract: We consider a general bond percolation on an infinite locally finite tree, where the edge retention probabilities $p_e$ are replaced by $\min\{1,q_{|e|}p_e\}$, where $\{q_n\}_{n\ge 1}$ is a sequence of positive perturbation factors and $|e|$ denotes the distance between the edge $e$ and the root. If the original percolation model admits infinite clusters, it is of interest to investigate under which perturbations $0<q_n\le 1$ this connectivity property is preserved. Conversely, if the original percolation does not admit infinite clusters, we are led to study the stability of such a property under perturbations satisfying $q_n\ge 1$.
  In both cases, under minimal assumptions on the original model, we show that the percolative behaviour is stable against certain quantitative non-trivial perturbations. We also discuss an application of our results to the Erdős similarity conjecture for Cantor sets.

</details>


### [22] [Fluctuations of the Sherrington--Kirkpatrick free energy at critical temperature](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02172)
*Hang Du,Brice Huang*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文在临界逆温度 β=1 且外场为零的设定下，证明 Sherrington–Kirkpatrick (SK) 自旋玻璃模型自由能的方差为 (1/6) log N + O(1)，并建立了高斯中心极限定理 (CLT)。同时，证实了临界二副本重叠 (two-replica overlap) 的标度行为 E⟨R₁₂²⟩ ≍ N^{-2/3} 以及均匀指数矩上界。关键方法是将 Ising 型与球型 SK 配分函数进行比较，证明二者在 L² 意义下相差 o(1)，从而可利用球型模型处理临界涨落。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 物理学家 Aspelmeier 等人曾预测 SK 模型在临界温度下自由能的方差为 (1/6) log N，Talagrand 也猜想临界二副本重叠的标度律 E⟨R₁₂²⟩ ≍ N^{-2/3}。本文旨在对这些物理与数学猜想给出严格数学证明。

Method: 建立 Ising 型 SK 配分函数 Z_N 与球型 SK 配分函数 Z_N^{sp} 之间的精确比较：定义比率 X_N = Z_N / Z_N^{sp}，证明 X_N = 1 + o(1) 在 L² 范数下成立。Z_N^{sp} 作为可处理的重新权重 (reweighting) 变量，用于捕捉 Z_N 的发散临界涨落并估计重叠矩。

Result: 1) 自由能方差 Var(F_N) = (1/6) log N + O(1)；2) 中心化与缩放后的 F_N 满足高斯 CLT；3) 临界二副本重叠满足 E⟨R₁₂²⟩ ≍ N^{-2/3}；4) 存在 N^{1/3}|R₁₂| 的一致指数矩上界。

Conclusion: 本文严格证明了 SK 模型在临界温度下的自由能方差与标度律，确认了物理与数学领域的重要猜想。将 Ising SK 与球型 SK 配分函数进行比较的技术框架，为处理复杂自旋玻璃模型的临界行为提供了一种有效的新途径。

Abstract: We consider the Sherrington--Kirkpatrick spin glass model at the critical inverse temperature $β= 1$ with zero external field. We prove that the free energy $F_N = F_{N,β=1}$ of this model has variance
  \[
  \mathrm{Var}(F_N) = \frac16 \log N + O(1)\,,
  \] confirming a physics prediction of Aspelmeier \cite{aspelmeier2008free}, and that the centered and scaled $F_N$ satisfies a Gaussian CLT. We also identify the critical two-replica overlap scale, proving
  \[
  \mathbb{E} \langle R_{1,2}^2\rangle \asymp N^{-2/3}\,,
  \] as conjectured by Talagrand \cite{talagrand2011mean2}, together with a uniform exponential moment bound for $N^{1/3} |R_{1,2}|$. The key input is a comparison between the Ising and spherical SK partition functions $Z_N$ and $Z^{\mathrm{sp}}_N$: if $X_N = Z_N / Z^{\mathrm{sp}}_N$, then $X_N = 1 + o(1)$ in $L^2$. Thus $Z^{\mathrm{sp}}_N$ captures the diverging critical fluctuations of $Z_N$ and serves as a tractable reweighting variable for estimating overlap moments.

</details>


### [23] [Flux solutions for stochastic chemical systems with sources and sinks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02367)
*E. Franco,J. J. L. Velázquez*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文研究一类既不满足细致平衡（detailed balance）也不满足复平衡（complex balance）的随机化学系统（stochastic chemical systems），通过向保守化学系统添加源和汇来构建与储库接触的随机化学系统。证明这些系统是非爆炸马尔可夫链（non-explosive Markov chains），且随时间趋于稳态，稳态解为非平衡解。最后将结果应用于描述分子通过膜通道的输运通量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 许多真实的随机化学系统不满足细致平衡或复平衡条件，但现有理论主要针对满足这些性质的系统。本文旨在为处于非平衡状态的随机化学系统提供严格的数学框架，特别是通过引入源和汇来模拟系统与外部储库（reservoirs）的接触。

Method: 通过对保守化学系统（conservative chemical systems）添加源（sources）和汇（sinks），构建一类新的随机化学系统。利用马尔可夫链（Markov chain）理论对该类系统的动力学性质进行严格分析。

Result: 证明了所构造的随机化学系统是非爆炸的马尔可夫链，且当时间趋于无穷时系统收敛到一个稳态。该稳态解是远离平衡（out of equilibrium）的稳态解。

Conclusion: 将理论结果应用于描述分子通过某些膜通道（membrane channels）的通量（fluxes），验证了模型在非平衡输运问题中的实用性。

Abstract: In this paper we study a class of stochastic chemical systems that, in general, do not satisfy the property of detailed balance nor the property of complex balance. These systems are obtained by adding sources and sinks to conservative chemical systems. This procedure is a way to define rigorously stochastic chemical systems in contact with reservoirs. We prove that these systems are non-explosive Markov chains and we prove that they converge to a steady state as time tends to infinity. The stationary solution are out of equilibrium solutions. We conclude the paper by applying our results in order to describe fluxes of molecules through some membrane channels.

</details>

Motivation: 建立Wilson环变量关联与plaquette随机团簇模型中拓扑量之间的显式关系式，以利用该对应研究晶格规范理论的关联性质。（Motivation）

Method: 通过推导Potts晶格规范理论中Wilson环变量关联与plaquette随机团簇模型拓扑量之间的数学关系式，并借助对偶性、自由/常边界条件设置等技巧进行分析。（Method）

Result: 在$\mathbb{Z}^4$上证明了自由边界条件下的关联长度等于对偶模型常边界条件下的关联长度；在$\mathbb{Z}^3$上证明了除临界温度外，缓慢增长Wilson环变量的关联呈指数衰减；在任意维度下证明了足够高或足够低温度时关联长度有限。（Result）

Conclusion: 该关联公式为理解晶格规范理论中的关联行为提供了新工具，并揭示了其在多个维度和边界条件下的普适性质。（Conclusion）

Abstract: We exhibit a formula relating the correlation between Wilson loop variables in Potts lattice gauge theory to a topological quantity in the plaquette random cluster model. As applications we show that the correlation length of the model on $\mathbb{Z}^4$ with free boundary conditions equals that of the dual model with constant boundary conditions, we prove exponential decay of correlations between slowly growing Wilson loop variables for Ising lattice gauge theory on $\mathbb{Z}^3$ at all but the critical temperature, and we demonstrate that the correlation length is finite at sufficiently high or low temperatures in any dimension.

### [25] [Mixing times of spin systems on dynamical percolation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02477)
*Alexandre Stauffer,Oskar Vavtar*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文研究了动态渗流（dynamical percolation）上最近邻格劳伯动力学（nearest-neighbour Glauber dynamics）的混合时间（mixing time），证明当渗流概率低于临界阈值且环境更新速率足够小时，混合时间具有对数阶标度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解动态随机环境中自旋系统的弛豫行为是统计力学（statistical mechanics）与非平衡态物理的核心问题之一。本文旨在刻画动态渗流背景下自旋系统混合时间的标度行为，特别是环境动力学与自旋动力学的相互影响。

Method: 采用耦合方法（coupling method），构建一种特殊的耦合机制，在环境行为良好的局部区域将不同初始条件的局部构型耦合在一起。该方法不依赖马尔可夫链的可逆性（reversibility），适用于更广泛的非可逆系统。

Result: 对于一类相对广泛的最近邻自旋系统，当渗流概率低于临界阈值（$p<p_c(d)$）且环境更新速率$λ$足够小时，对于任意温度，混合时间（mixing time）为$O(\log N / λ)$量级。

Conclusion: 该结果表明，在动态渗流环境中，若环境变化足够慢，自旋系统的弛豫时间主要由环境演化主导，混合时间反比于环境更新速率，且仅随系统尺度对数增长。

Abstract: We study the mixing times of stochastic spin systems corresponding to nearest-neighbour Glauber dynamics on dynamical percolation, defined on $d$-dimensional torus of side-length $N$. In this model, the status of each edge (open or closed) updates independently at rate $λ>0$, according to $\mathrm{Ber}(p)$ samples. Simultaneously, the spin of each site updates at rate $1$ according to Glauber dynamics on the environment restricted to open edges. We show that for a relatively general class of nearest-neighbour systems, as long as $p<p_c(d)$, for any temperature, if $λ$ is sufficiently small, the mixing time is of order $\frac{\log N}λ$. This Markov chain is non-reversible, and the proof is obtained by developing a particular coupling that couples together local configurations whenever the environment behaves well.

</details>

### [26] [The ring wants to be broken](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01967)
*Alexei Vazquez*

Main category: physics.soc-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过解析计算循环环格点（circulant ring lattice）$C_n(1,\dots,c)$ 的拉姆齐社区数（Ramsey community number）$r_κ$，证明了在没有节点异质性的网络中，仅靠局部连接规则即可涌现出社区结构，并发现最近邻环（$c=1$）永远不会被分区（$r_κ=\infty$），而次近邻环（$c=2$）在约35个节点以上就会偏好二分社区结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此前通过数值模拟发现，由局部规则生长的网络中可以涌现社区结构，无需节点异质性。但该现象缺乏严格的解析证明，因此本文旨在为最简单的同质局部连接图——循环环格点——提供拉姆齐社区数 $r_κ$ 的精确解析计算，从而严格刻画社区涌现的相变条件。

Method: 采用对称 $\mathrm{Beta}$ 先验的伯努利随机块模型（Bernoulli stochastic block model）作为社区检测规则；分别推导了平衡二分社区划分与无划分两种假设下的贝叶斯证据（Bayesian evidence）的闭式表达式；通过比较两者的对数证据，精确定位相变点，得到 $r_κ$ 的解析结果。

Result: 对于最近邻环（$c=1$），二分社区的后验概率随 $n$ 以 $n^{-(2α+3)}$ 衰减，因此 $r_κ=\infty$，网络永远不会被分区。对于次近邻环（$c=2$），$r_κ\simeq 35$ 个节点，当网络规模超过此阈值时，二分社区划分的对数证据以 $(\ln 2)\,n$ 增长，分区被偏好。

Conclusion: 该工作提供了一个社区涌现的精确可解实例，严格证明即使在无内置社区的网络中，只要局部连接范围（interaction range）足够大（$c\ge 2$），社区结构即可自发产生；表明最少的局部连接增量即可打破环的对称性。

Abstract: The Ramsey community number $r_κ$ is the minimum network size at which a graph's connectivity is better described by a partition into communities than by no partition, under a prescribed community-detection rule. It was introduced through numerical simulations of networks grown by local rules, which suggested that community structure can emerge without any node heterogeneity. Here I compute $r_κ$ analytically for the simplest homogeneous, locally wired graph: the circulant ring lattice $C_n(1,\dots,c)$. Using a Bernoulli stochastic block model with symmetric $\mathrm{Beta}$ priors as the detection rule, the Bayesian evidence for a balanced two-community partition and for the unpartitioned network are both obtained in closed form, so the transition between them can be located exactly. The result is a sharp dependence on the interaction range: the plain cycle ($c=1$) is never partitioned, its two-community posterior decaying as $n^{-(2α+3)}$, so $r_κ=\infty$; but the next-nearest-neighbour ring ($c=2$) acquires a finite $r_κ\simeq 35$ nodes, above which the partition is preferred with a log-evidence growing as $(\ln 2)\,n$. This provides an exactly solvable instance of community emergence in a network with no built-in communities, and shows that a minimal amount of local connectivity is enough to break the ring.

</details>

### [27] [Molecular interpretability of the bulk electrochemical impedance of concentrated electrolytes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02316)
*Connie J. Fairchild,Stephen J. Cox,Benjamin Rotenberg,Thomas Sayer*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本论文提出了一种基于频率依赖电导率矩（moments of frequency-dependent conductivity）和广义朗之万方程（generalized Langevin equation）驱动的“游走振子”（itinerant oscillator, IO）模型，用以替代传统等效电路拟合方法，解析电解质体相对电化学阻抗谱（EIS）的贡献。通过分析室温离子液体的分子动力学模拟，模型揭示记忆函数中时间尺度分离对温度依赖的β弛豫过程的重要性，并在保持常用工作流简便性的同时，直接报告时间尺度的分布。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电化学阻抗谱（EIS）被广泛用于研究施加电压下的时间依赖响应与弛豫现象，但现有理解仍存在重大空白，阻碍了从微观化学机制层面对EIS谱进行解释。传统经验拟合方法在物理解释力上存在局限，亟需一种能同时提供分子可解释性且不依赖电解质浓度假设的新分析框架。

Method: 提出基于频率依赖电导率矩（moments）的方法，并采用广义朗之万方程（generalized Langevin equation）描述有效单粒子动力学，即“游走振子”（itinerant oscillator, IO）模型。与Debye-Falkenhagen模型不同，IO模型不预先假定电解质浓度，通过对室温离子液体的分子动力学（molecular dynamics）模拟数据进行记忆函数（memory function）分析，验证该方法的有效性。

Result: IO模型成功解析了模拟中的记忆函数，揭示了捕捉记忆函数内时间尺度分离（separation of timescales）对于描述温度依赖的β弛豫（β-relaxation）过程的关键作用。该阻抗模型能够直接报告时间尺度的分布信息，同时保持与常用工作流相当的简便性。

Conclusion: 所提出的基于IO模型和电导率矩的EIS分析新方法，在无需电解质浓度假设的前提下，提供了具有分子可解释性的阻抗谱描述框架，能够有效揭示弛豫过程背后的时间尺度特征，有望改进对EIS谱的微观机制理解。

Abstract: Electrochemical impedance spectroscopy (EIS) is a widely used technique to understand time-dependent response and relaxation under applied voltage. While these spectra contain a wealth of information, major gaps in our understanding can hinder our ability to interpret EIS spectra in terms of microscopic chemical mechanisms. We propose an alternative approach to common empirical fitting procedures for describing the contribution of the bulk electrolyte to the EIS spectrum. This new approach is rooted in determining the moments of the frequency-dependent conductivity, with molecular interpretability provided by a generalized Langevin equation description of an effective single particle dynamics; the `itinerant oscillator' (IO) model. In contrast to a Debye--Falkenhagen description, the IO model makes no assumptions regarding the concentration of the electrolyte, a fact we demonstrate by analysing molecular dynamics simulations of a room-temperature ionic liquid. By analysing the memory function from simulation within the framework provided by the IO model, we reveal the importance of capturing the separation of timescales within the memory function for describing the temperature dependent $β$-relaxation process. We go on to show how our impedance model directly reports on this distribution of timescales while retaining the simplicity of commonly employed workflows.

</details>

### [28] [Elastic Modulus in One-Dimensional Quantum Droplets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01863)
*Rui Zhang,Tianmiao Zhang,Huan-Bo Luo,Zibin Zhao*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文基于超高斯变分拟设（super Gaussian variational ansatz），系统研究了一维量子液滴（quantum droplet）的弹性模量（elastic modulus），推导了其与相互作用强度和粒子数的依赖关系，建立了与呼吸模式频率的定量联系，并发现一维系统中孤子-液滴交叉（soliton-to-droplet crossover）导致弹性模量比 η 呈现比三维情形更复杂的依赖行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 三维量子液滴中已引入体积模量（bulk modulus）概念并揭示了其与呼吸模式频率（breathing-mode frequency）的联系，受此启发，本文旨在探究一维量子液滴的弹性模量（elastic modulus）及其物理行为。

Method: 采用超高斯变分拟设（super Gaussian variational ansatz）系统推导弹性模量 B；通过虚时演化（imaginary time evolution）和空间标度方法（spatial scaling method）进行数值模拟验证；引入超越Thomas-Fermi近似的液滴宽度修正。

Result: 建立了弹性模量与呼吸模式本征频率的定量关系；获得了参数 η = B/2 对控制参数 g 和 N 的依赖关系；发现一维系统中孤子-液滴交叉（soliton-to-droplet crossover）导致 η 的依赖行为比三维情形的简单幂律标度更复杂；高粒子数区域弹性模量渐近趋近于主要由相互作用强度决定的极限值，低粒子数区域则同时依赖于粒子数和相互作用强度。

Conclusion: 一维量子液滴的弹性模量行为与三维情形存在显著差异，其核心源于孤子-液滴交叉效应，这一发现丰富了对低维量子液滴弹性响应和集体动力学的理解。

Abstract: Quantum droplets (QDs) are self-bound states of ultradilute quantum fluids stabilized by the interplay between the Lee Huang-Yang (LHY) quantum-fluctuation correction and the mean-field interaction, providing a useful platform for exploring macroscopic quantum phenomena. Recent studies on three-dimensional QDs have introduced the concept of bulk modulus and revealed its connection with the breathing-mode frequency, thereby linking the elastic response of QDs to their collective dynamics. Motivated by this progress, we investigate the elastic modulus of one-dimensional QDs. Based on a super Gaussian variational ansatz, we systematically derive the elastic modulus B and analyze its dependence on the interaction strength and particle number. The analytical predictions are further validated by numerical simulations based on imaginary time evolution and the spatial scaling method. We also establish a quantitative relation between the elastic modulus and the eigenfrequency of the breathing mode. In addition, by incorporating corrections to the droplet width beyond the Thomas Fermi approximation, we obtain the dependence of the ratio η = B/2 on the control parameters g and N. Unlike the three-dimensional case, where the corresponding ratio follows a simple power-law scaling, the one-dimensional system is affected by the soliton-to-droplet crossover, leading to a more intricate dependence of η on g and N. Our results show that, in the high-particle-number regime, the elastic modulus asymptotically approaches a limiting value determined mainly by the interaction strength, whereas in the low-particle-number regime it depends on both the particle number and the interaction strength.

</details>


### [29] [Interaction-rotation driven localization-delocalization of eigenstate in Fock space: An exact diagonalization study on trapped Bose gas](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01888)
*Mohd Talib,M. A. H. Ahsan*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该论文通过精确对角化方法研究了有限系统中相互作用玻色子在非旋转和旋转情况下的局域-退局域转变（localization-delocalization transition）与纠缠结构，利用逆参与率（IPR）、香农熵（Shannon entropy）和冯·诺依曼纠缠熵（von Neumann entanglement entropy）表征基态结构，发现相互作用强度、旋转和玻色子数共同驱动系统向退局域态转变，且局域态与弱纠缠、退局域态与强纠缠相关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在理解有限系统中相互作用玻色子的局域-退局域转变机制及其纠缠结构，特别关注旋转效应与系统尺寸对这一转变的调节作用。

Method: 采用精确对角化（exact diagonalization）方法在固定总角动量子空间中获得多体能谱，并通过逆参与率（IPR）、香农熵（信息熵）和冯·诺依曼纠缠熵分析基态结构。

Result: 非旋转情况下，随相互作用增强出现从局域到退局域的转变，IPR下降而熵增加；旋转进一步推动退局域化，中等角动量展现部分扩展，高角动量出现饱和行为但随系统尺寸增大而减弱；IPR、信息熵和纠缠熵行为一致，提供统一表征。

Conclusion: 相互作用强度、旋转和玻色子数共同推动系统向退局域态转变，局域态与弱纠缠相关，退局域态与强纠缠相关，验证了多种熵度量在表征该转变中的一致性与有效性。

Abstract: We investigate the localization-delocalization transition and entanglement structure in a finite system of interacting bosons in non-rotating and rotating cases. The many-body eigenspectrum is obtained via exact diagonalization within subspaces of fixed total angular momentum, and the structure of the ground state is analyzed using the inverse participation ratio (IPR), the Shannon entropy (information entropy) and the von Neumann entanglement entropy. In the non-rotating case, a transition from localized to delocalized behavior is observed with increasing interaction strength. The transition is characterized by a decrease in IPR and a corresponding increase in entropy measures, indicating spread of eigenstate weight over all the basis states in the Hilbert space. The effect becomes more pronounced with increasing number of bosons due to the increase of the Hilbert space dimension. In the presence of rotation, the system is driven further toward delocalization. For moderate angular momentum, the eigenstates exhibit partial spreading, while at higher angular momenta a saturation behavior emerges, where further increase in rotation has a limited effect on the localization properties. However, the saturation weakens with increasing system size, indicating a nontrivial interplay between rotation and number of bosons. The consistent behavior of IPR, information entropy and von Neumann entanglement entropy demonstrates that these measures provide a unified characterization of the localization-delocalization transition. The results highlight the combined role of interaction strength, rotation and number of bosons in driving the system towards delocalized state. We observe a connection between localization-delocalization and entanglement, with localized states exhibiting weaker entanglement and delocalized states showing stronger entanglement.

### [30] [Localization and Topological Properties of SU(3) Fermions in non-Abelian Gauge Fields: Color-Orbit Coupling and Color-Flip Fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02274)
*Bar Alluf,C. A. R. Sá de Melo*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文研究了SU(3)彩色费米子在含非阿贝尔规范场的一维双色光学晶格中的局域化与拓扑性质。通过构建广义三色Aubry-André模型，发现非阿贝尔场破坏了常规自对偶性，产生迁移率区域，并利用精确对角化等方法绘制了扩展/局域体态的相图。此外，通过将一维无序模型映射为二维彩色Harper模型，计算拓扑不变量揭示了边缘态的拓扑绝缘体性质，并发现拓扑彩色绝缘体相可邻接扩展、局域或混合相，与传统拓扑绝缘体不同。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实验上已实现SU(3)彩色费米子的人工非阿贝尔规范场，但非阿贝尔规范场、无序与内部自由度之间的相互作用如何影响量子多体系统的局域化与拓扑性质尚不清楚，亟需理论探索。

Method: 采用色-轨道耦合和色翻转（Rabi）场描述非阿贝尔规范场，建立广义三色Aubry-André模型。使用精确对角化（exact diagonalization）、态密度评估（density-of-states evaluations）和逆参与率（inverse participation ratio）的有限尺寸标度（finite-size scaling）进行分析。进一步将一维无序模型映射为二维彩色Harper模型，并计算电荷-电荷陈数（charge-charge Chern number）等拓扑不变量。

Result: 非阿贝尔场破坏了常规三色Aubry-André系统的自对偶性，在能谱中产生迁移率区域。得到了扩展/局域体态的相图。边缘态具有拓扑性质，多个带隙相被揭示为拓扑绝缘体。拓扑彩色绝缘体相可邻接三种构型：两个扩展相、两个局域相，或各一个，与传统拓扑绝缘体始终邻接两个扩展相形成鲜明对比。

Conclusion: 非阿贝尔规范场能增强或阻碍色局域化（color localization），且拓扑绝缘体相与邻近相的配置关系比传统情形更丰富，为理解无序系统中非阿贝尔场的物理效应提供了新视角。

Abstract: The interplay between disorder, gauge fields, and internal degrees of freedom fundamentally affects localization and topological properties of quantum many-body systems. Motivated by recent experimental realizations of synthetic non-Abelian gauge fields for SU(3) colored fermions, we investigate their localization and topological properties in 1D bichromatic optical lattices consisting of strong and weak laser beams. Describing the non-Abelian gauge field via color-orbit coupling and color-flip (Rabi) fields, we obtain a tight-binding description of trapped SU(3) colored fermions corresponding to a generalized three-color Aubry-André model. We show that these fields explicitly break the conventional self-duality of a simple three-color Aubry-André system. This duality breaking generates mobility regions across the energy spectrum, demonstrating that non-Abelian fields can either enhance or hinder color localization. Using exact diagonalization, density-of-states evaluations, and finite-size scaling of the inverse participation ratio, we obtain phase diagrams that identify regions of extended or localized bulk states. Furthermore, the color-orbit and Rabi fields induce edge states with topological properties. We develop an exact mapping from our 1D disorder model into a 2D color Harper model with a fictitious magnetic flux ratio and dimension controlled by the weak laser beam's phase. Using this mapping, we evaluate topological invariants, such as the charge-charge Chern number, for edge states emerging in energy gaps, revealing the topological insulating nature of several gapped phases. Lastly, we identify that these topological color-insulator phases can energetically neighbor three configurations: two extended, two localized, or one of each. This sharply contrasts with conventional topological insulators, which always neighbor two extended phases.

Out of the box, Q-GAIN implements classification, object detection, and physics-informed metrics for feature detection in images of atomic Bose-Einstein condensates (BECs). Q-GAIN encourages a natural, module-based workflow: starting with data loading and preprocessing, followed by ML-based feature identification, and ending with conventional analysis techniques. We demonstrate this modularity by configuring Q-GAIN for three ML tasks. First, we demonstrate the basic workflow of the Q-GAIN framework by implementing the standard task of classifying handwritten digits from the MNIST dataset. Then, we re-implement our earlier soliton detection (SolDet) package in the Q-GAIN framework, enabling the detection and analysis of solitonic excitations in time-of-flight data. Finally, we develop an object-detection tool that identifies quantized vortices in images of ring-shaped BECs.

### [32] [Understanding Non-Gaussian Chorus Wave Statistics via the Benjamin-Feir Index](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01475)
*D. J. Ratliff,O. Allanson,D. Rasinskaite,J. Stawarz,C. E. J. Watt,S. Chakraborty*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前对赤道合声波的非高斯统计特性（non-Gaussian statistics）缺乏基于第一性原理的定量刻画指标，亟需建立一种能够从理论层面区分高斯与非高斯合声波场景的波活动指数，以服务于空间天气建模（space weather modelling）中的阈值量化需求。

Method: 推导了赤道合声波的扩展波作用量模型（extended wave action model），从中识别出一个波活动指数——Benjamin-Feir指数（Benjamin-Feir index, BFI）的变体，并基于该指数构建了全球分布图，以识别非高斯波统计特性出现的关键区域。通过与范艾伦探测器A的实际测量事件进行定性比对，验证模型并识别改进方向。

Result: 波活动指数阈值确定为BFI > 0.5时出现非高斯频率谱（non-Gaussian frequency spectra）。全球分布图显示，磁层（magnetosphere）的夜侧和晨侧区域（0 < MLT < 9）是非高斯波统计特性的主要出现区域。模型能够解释非高斯合声波特有的不对称频率谱（asymmetric frequency spectra），且与实测数据具有良好定性一致性。

Conclusion: 该研究首次从第一性原理建立了区分高斯与非高斯合声波场景的波活动指数，为空间天气建模中的阈值量化提供了理论基础。模型的关键优势在于能够刻画非高斯合声波的不对称频率谱特征，但后续仍需根据实测数据进一步改进模型细节。

Abstract: We derive an extended wave action model for equatorial chorus waves, identifying a wave activity index (a version of the Benjamin-Feir index, BFI) which indicates non-Gaussian frequency spectra emerge when BFI$>$0.5. Global maps of this index indicate the night and dawn sectors ($0<{\rm MLT}<9)$ of the magnetosphere as the primary region for non-Gaussian wave statistics to emerge. Comparisons with events measured by the Van Allen probe A demonstrate good qualitative agreement whilst identifying key aspects for model refinement. A key strength of our model that our work highlights is its ability to account for the asymmetric frequency spectra characteristic of non-Gaussian chorus. This work ultimately establishes the first wave activity index that distinguishes Gaussian and non-Gaussian wave scenarios from first principles, providing the groundwork for a threshold-based quantification for use in space weather modelling.

### [33] [On the limits of the energetic coupling between field dislocation mechanics and phase field crystal](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01284)
*Aymane Graini,Jorge Viñals,Manas V. Upadhyay*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文分析了场位错力学（FDM）与相场晶体模型（PFC）之间的一种能量耦合方案，发现该耦合仅作用于位错场中的兼容（无旋）部分，对携带位错拓扑信息的不兼容（无散）部分不敏感，且无法阻止FDM中位错核的非自然扩展，无法有效将位错力学与晶体学整合到统一的连续介质框架中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前研究提出了将场位错力学（FDM）与相场晶体模型（PFC）进行能量耦合的方案，旨在将位错力学与晶体学统一在同一连续介质框架中。本文旨在对该耦合方案进行变分分析与数值验证，评估其能否有效实现这一整合目标。

Method: 采用变分分析法（variational analysis）考察耦合项对相场演化的影响，并结合数值模拟对耦合方案的效果进行验证。此外，还考虑了最一般情形下的能量耦合推广。

Result: 耦合项仅作为散度驱动的力作用于相场演化，仅匹配位错场中兼容（无旋）部分；对携带位错拓扑信息的不兼容（无散）弹性畸变不敏感。构型畸变（configurational distortion）的性质导致力学边界条件从FDM到PFC呈扩散性而非弹性传递。数值模拟表明该耦合无法阻止FDM中的位错核非自然扩展（core spreading）。

Conclusion: 即使在最一般情形下，这种能量耦合方案也存在同样的缺陷，限制了其将位错力学与晶体学整合的能力。

Abstract: This paper investigates the energetic coupling between Field Dislocation Mechanics (FDM) and the Phase Field Crystal (PFC) model proposed in Phys. Rev. B 102, 064109, 2020. While FDM correctly solves the initial boundary value problem of a continuum body with dislocation fields, PFC captures the underlying crystallographic structure. The coupling, which penalizes the $L^2$ distance between elastic distortion from FDM and configurational distortion from PFC in the $L^2$ sense, had been proposed to reconcile dislocation mechanics with crystallography in a single continuum framework. Variational analysis reveals that the coupling term acts as a divergence-driven forcing in the phase-field evolution that matches only the compatible (curl-free) parts of the distortion fields. Consequently, its contributions are insensitive to the incompatible (divergence-free) elastic distortion carrying all the information on dislocation topology. Furthermore, the nature of the configurational distortion causes mechanical boundary conditions to be transmitted diffusively from FDM to PFC rather than elastically. Numerical simulations demonstrate that this coupling cannot prevent the unnatural core spreading in FDM. Finally, it is shown that even in the most general case, an energetic coupling suffers from the same drawbacks, which limits its ability to integrate dislocation mechanics with crystallography.

### [34] [Microscopic origins of inertial magnetization dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01398)
*Caleb Webb,Ling Gan,Shufeng Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过非马尔可夫量子主方程（non-Markovian quantum master equation）证明，铁磁体中的惯性磁化动力学（inertial magnetization dynamics）源于磁子与光学声子（optical phonons）的相干耦合，为超快自旋动力学的微观机制提供了理论解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超快实验已观察到铁磁体中的惯性磁化动力学现象，但其微观起源尚不明确，亟需理论解释。

Method: 采用非马尔可夫量子主方程对惯性动力学进行建模，将磁子-声子耦合（magnon-phonon coupling）作为微观机制进行分析。

Result: 惯性动力学来源于磁子与晶格中光学声子的相干相互作用；光学声子的快速频率解释了皮秒时间尺度上的章动（nutation）现象；不同实验间的差异可通过衬底依赖的声子阻尼（phonon damping）加以解释。

Conclusion: 该研究确立了磁子-声子耦合作为惯性磁化的微观基础，为在太赫兹频率下调控超快自旋动力学和磁态开辟了新途径。

Abstract: Ultrafast experiments have uncovered inertial magnetization dynamics in ferromagnets, but their microscopic origin remains elusive. Using a non-Markovian quantum master equation we show that inertial dynamics arise from coherent interactions with optical phonons in the lattice. The fast optical frequency explains the nutation observed on picosecond timescales and accounts for variations between experiments through substrate-dependent phonon damping. By establishing magnon{phonon coupling as the microscopic basis of inertial magnetization, our results open new pathways for tailoring ultrafast spin dynamics and controlling magnetic states at terahertz frequencies.

### [35] [Vitriflow: calibrated amorphous structure ensembles from melt-quench simulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01407)
*Jonathon Cottom,Robin Delhomme,Emilia Olsson*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出 vitriflow 框架，将熔融-淬火分子动力学（melt-quench molecular dynamics）中通常隐含的参数选择（如数值设置、熔融温度、保温时间、淬火速率、系统尺寸及后处理筛选）转化为显式决策链，通过耦合数值稳定性、描述符校准、人工缺陷筛选与统计收敛，为无定形材料（amorphous materials）建模提供可复现的生成路径，并在 a-SiO₂、a-Si₃N₄ 和 a-Sm₂O₃ 三个体系中验证了其区分缺陷、量化密度泛函理论（DFT）精炼响应及排除再结晶结构的能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 熔融-淬火分子动力学被广泛用于构建无定形材料模型，但生成的系综（ensemble）隐性地依赖于数值设置、熔融温度、保温时间、淬火速率、系统尺寸及后处理筛选等一系列参数选择，缺乏显式、可复现的决策流程。

Method: vitriflow 框架将隐含参数选择转化为显式决策链，耦合数值稳定性（numerical stability）、基于描述符（descriptor）的协议校准、用户定义的人工缺陷筛选（artefact screening）以及生成分析系综在材料特定描述符空间中的统计收敛（statistical convergence）。

Result: 在 a-SiO₂ 中成功区分无缺陷结构与氧桥缺陷结构；在 a-Si₃N₄ 中量化了从 MG2 到 PBE 再到 HSE06 的密度泛函理论（DFT）精炼响应于共同结构种群中的变化；在 a-Sm₂O₃ 中无需固定配位数即可排除再结晶结构。

Conclusion: vitriflow 提供了一条可复现的无定形系综生成路径，其数值设置、热协议、筛选操作与统计精度均依据材料问题本身选择，而非先验假设（assumed a priori）。

Abstract: Melt--quench molecular dynamics is widely used to construct amorphous materials models, but the resulting ensemble is defined by choices that are often made implicitly: numerical settings, melt temperature, liquid-hold time, quench rate, system size, and post-generation screening. We introduce vitriflow, a computational materials methodology that turns these choices into an explicit decision chain. The framework couples numerical stability, descriptor-based protocol calibration, user-defined artefact screening, and statistical convergence of the generated analysis ensemble in a material-specific descriptor space. We demonstrate the approach for a-SiO$_2$, a-Si$_3$N$_4$, and a-Sm$_2$O$_3$, which respectively test tetrahedral network fidelity, MG2 $\rightarrow$ PBE $\rightarrow$ HSE06 DFT refinement of a heteropolar nitride, and amorphous/crystal discrimination in a mixed-coordination rare-earth oxide. vitriflow separates defect-free from oxygen-bridge-defective silica, quantifies DFT-refinement response in a common a-Si$_3$N$_4$ structural population, and removes recrystallised Sm$_2$O$_3$ structures without imposing fixed coordination. The result is a reproducible route for generating amorphous ensembles whose numerical settings, thermal protocol, screening actions, and statistical precision are selected from the materials question rather than assumed a priori.

</details>


### [36] [Phase-selective orbital-charge conversion in $\mathrm{MoTe_2}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01623)
*J. L. Costa,E. Santos,G. R. Gallo,G. Rodrigues-Junior,R. O. Cunha,E. L. T. França,R. Cardias,T. G. Rappoport,J. B. S. Mendes,A. Azevedo*

Conclusion: $\mathrm{MoTe_2}$ 中的轨道 Rashba–Edelstein 响应（orbital Rashba–Edelstein response）是观测到的横向电荷转换信号的主导机制；该工作表明厚度驱动的结构相变可调控二维 TMDs 的轨道电子学（orbitronic）响应。

Abstract: Two-dimensional transition metal dichalcogenides (TMDs) have emerged as promising materials for spin--orbitronics owing to their strong spin--orbit coupling and rich electronic phases. However, their orbital transport properties remain largely unexplored. Here, we demonstrate that the orbitronic response of $\mathrm{MoTe_2}$ is governed by a thickness-driven structural phase transition. RF-sputtered $\mathrm{MoTe_2}$ thin films exhibit a crossover at a critical thickness of approximately $4.5\,\mathrm{nm}$, stabilizing in the metallic $1T^\prime$ phase below this threshold and in the semiconducting $2H$ phase above it. Raman spectroscopy and scanning tunneling spectroscopy (STS) confirm the structural and electronic transition, revealing gapless behavior in ultrathin films and a finite band gap in thicker samples. Spin-pumping measurements detect an additional transverse charge-conversion signal exclusively in metallic $1T^\prime$-$\mathrm{MoTe_2}$, in agreement with first-principles calculations that identify a dominant orbital Rashba--Edelstein response as the underlying conversion mechanism.

### [37] [Intrinsically low thermal conductivity of stoichiometric lithium niobate:Experimental measurement and microscopic origin](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01673)
*Wenjiang Zhou,Fuwei Yang,Yuxi Wang,Weiheng Li,Wujuan Yan,Kexin Zhang,Bai Song*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文结合频域热反射（FDTR）实验与机器学习原子模拟，系统研究了化学计量比铌酸锂（sLN）的热传输特性，揭示了其极低热导率的微观机制主要源于强非简谐性与大散射相空间，而非简谐特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着基于铌酸锂（LiNbO₃, LN）的电光和非线性光学器件快速发展，热管理成为关键问题，但化学计量比铌酸锂（sLN）的热传输实验测量稀缺，微观机制尚不明确。

Method: 采用频域热反射（frequency-domain thermoreflectance, FDTR）激光泵浦-探测技术，结合先进的机器学习原子模拟（machine-learned atomistic simulations），对sLN的热传输进行实验与计算综合研究。

Result: 室温热导率（κ）远低于硅等经典半导体；温度依赖κ呈T⁻α标度（α接近1），表明热传输受本征声子-声子散射主导；与超高κ基准立方砷化硼（cBAs）对比发现，sLN的低κ并非源于简谐特性（声子热容和群速度相当或更高），而是源于更强的非简谐性（anharmonicity）和更大的散射相空间（scattering phase space），使声子寿命降低1-2个数量级，最大声子平均自由程约140 nm；薄膜厚度低于1 μm时出现显著尺寸效应，10 nm厚时κ降至体材料的一半。

Conclusion: 建立了sLN热传输的基础理解，为先进铌酸锂技术的热管理提供了原子尺度的见解。

Abstract: With the rapid development of integrated electro-optic and nonlinear optical devices based on lithium niobate (LiNbO$_3$, LN), thermal management is becoming a critical area of focus. However, experimental measurement of thermal transport in stoichiometric LiNbO$_3$ (sLN) remains scarce, and the intrinsic microscopic mechanisms remain to be established. Here, we combine the laser pump-probe technique of frequency-domain thermoreflectance (FDTR) with state-of-the-art machine-learned atomistic simulations to comprehensively investigate thermal transport in sLN. The measured and simulated room-temperature thermal conductivity ($κ$) values of sLN agree well, which are orders-of-magnitude lower than that of many classic and emerging semiconductors such as silicon. Furthermore, the temperature-dependent $κ$ exhibits a $T^{-α}$ scaling with $α$ near unity, suggesting that thermal transport is dominated by intrinsic phonon-phonon scattering. By comparing sLN with cubic boron arsenide (cBAs) which serves as an ultrahigh-$κ$ benchmark, we reveal that harmonic properties are not responsible for the low $κ$ of sLN, which feature phonon heat capacity and group velocities that are either higher than or comparable to those in cBAs. Instead, the low $κ$ originates from substantially stronger anharmonicity and larger scattering phase space. These two factors collectively suppress phonon lifetimes by 1-2 orders of magnitude, leading to a maximum phonon mean free path of approximately 140 nm. As a result, notable size effects emerge in thin-film sLN below 1 $μ$m, with $κ$ dropping to half the bulk value at 10 nm. Altogether, our findings establish a fundamental understanding of thermal transport in sLN and provide atomistic insights for thermal management in advanced lithium niobate technologies.

Method: 采用扩散量子蒙特卡洛（DMC）方法对双层InSe的局部堆叠构型（local-registry landscape）进行基准计算，并与密度泛函理论（DFT）结果进行对比分析。
