Conclusion: DFT-based莫尔模型可能显著低估局部堆叠能量起伏（local stacking-energy corrugation），这一偏差将直接影响对扭曲层状材料中结构弛豫（structural relaxation）、畴形成（domain formation）和电子重构（electronic reconstruction）的预测。

Abstract: Density functional theory (DFT) is widely used to model twisted bilayers, but the accuracy of the local stacking energetics underlying such models remains uncertain. Here, we benchmark the local-registry landscape of bilayer InSe using diffusion quantum Monte Carlo (DMC). DFT predicts that AB, AAr, and ABr stackings, which share the same interfacial Se registry, are nearly degenerate within 1.5 meV/f.u. and exhibit nearly indistinguishable DFT charge-density responses. DMC instead separates these stackings by 8(5) and 41(4) meV/f.u., while the energy difference between the most stable and least stable registries reaches 60(7) meV/f.u.. These large energy separations show that the stacking energetics are not determined by the interfacial atomic motif alone but depend on the full registry and its associated many-body electronic response. More broadly, these results show that DFT-based moiré models can substantially underestimate local stacking-energy corrugation, with direct consequences for predicted structural relaxation, domain formation, and electronic reconstruction in twisted layered materials.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用分层筛选框架：第一步基于PBE相图进行热力学稳定性筛选；第二步利用通用机器学习原子间势进行动力学稳定性筛选，涵盖谐波声子（harmonic-phonon）和有限温度分子动力学（finite-temperature molecular dynamics）双重判据；第三步采用SCAN泛函进行热力学相图精化；最后结合分解焓（decomposition enthalpy）与化学空间完整性（chemical-space completeness）进行优先级排序。

Result: 从Sci. Data 9, 302 (2022)报道的894个稳定材料中，经结构去重得到603个独特结构；PBE完整相图筛选后仅298个保持热力学稳定；动力学筛选确认166个材料在双重判据下稳定；SCAN相图进一步缩减至109个；最终优先选出25个高置信度实验合成候选物。

Conclusion: 该工作提供了一个将稳定性预测转化为实验可操作的合成目标的实用协议，有效弥合了机器学习驱动的材料发现中预测与合成之间的关键差距。

Abstract: Machine-learning-accelerated materials discovery has yielded large numbers of computationally stable compounds, yet many remain experimentally unrealized, underscoring a persistent gap between prediction and synthesis. Here, we introduce a hierarchical screening framework that combines PBE-based thermodynamic stability, efficient dynamical-stability screening enabled by universal machine-learning interatomic potentials, and SCAN-based thermodynamic refinement. Applying this protocol to the 894 stable materials previously reported in Sci. Data 9, 302 (2022), we first curate 603 unique structures, of which only 298 remain thermodynamically stable on the complete PBE phase diagrams, demonstrating the critical role of competing phases in stability assessment. Dynamical screening then identifies 166 materials stable under both harmonic-phonon and finite-temperature molecular dynamics criteria, and SCAN phase diagrams further narrow this set to 109. Finally, by combining decomposition enthalpy with chemical-space completeness, we prioritize 25 candidates as high-confidence targets for experimental synthesis. This work provides a practical protocol for translating stability predictions into experimentally actionable synthesis targets, closing a key gap in machine-learning-driven materials discovery.

Abstract: We investigate the structural, electronic, and optical properties of native point defects in CaO using first-principles density-functional calculations. Oxygen vacancies are favored under O-poor conditions, whereas calcium vacancies dominate under O-rich conditions. Calculated migration barriers and binding energies indicate that vacancy complexes are thermodynamically stable and can survive high-temperature annealing. ### [41] [Quantifying angular momentum of coherently driven circular phonons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01841)
*Roman Mankowsky,Serhane Zerdane,Shih-Wen Huang,Mathias Sander,Xin Liu,Danylo Babich,Martina Basini,Puneet Kaur,Jan-Chi Yang,Michael Fechner,Urs Staub,Henrik Lemke*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实验已在非磁性SrTiO₃中观测到太赫兹（terahertz）脉冲诱导的内部磁场，但其起源仍存在争议。本文旨在解决这一争议，明确THz驱动下离子运动如何产生磁性的微观机制。

Method: 采用超快X射线衍射（ultrafast x-ray diffraction）技术，实时追踪圆偏振太赫兹脉冲激发后STO中离子的时间依赖性轨迹，并定量分析声子角动量（phonon angular momentum）在各离子组分中的分布。

Result: 氧离子（oxygen ions）虽质量较轻，却贡献了约90%的声子角动量。负离子与正离子之间的角动量不平衡为STO中诱导磁性（induced magnetism）提供了清晰的物理解释。

Conclusion: 该工作首次实现了对圆形离子运动及其角动量的定量测量，建立了一套研究固体中角动量转移（angular momentum transfer）的通用方法论，为控制拓扑声子输运（topological phonon transport）及声子驱动磁性（phonon-driven magnetism）开辟了新途径。

Abstract: The use of intense terahertz (THz) pulses to manipulate low-energy excitations offers a powerful approach for ultrafast control of electronic and magnetic properties in materials. Theory suggests that circular ionic motions driven by THz fields carry angular momentum, potentially generating internal magnetic fields. Recent experiments in nonmagnetic SrTiO3 (STO) have hinted at such THz-induced fields, but their origin remains debated. Here, we employ ultrafast x-ray diffraction to resolve the time-dependent ionic trajectories in STO following excitation by circularly polarized THz pulses. Our analysis reveals that oxygen ions, despite their lower mass, contribute around 90% of the phonon angular momentum. The resulting imbalance between the negatively and positively charged ions provides a clear explanation for the mechanism behind induced magnetism in STO. This work further provides the first quantitative measurement of circular ionic motions and their angular momentum and establishes a general methodology for the investigation of angular momentum transfer in solids, paving the way for new strategies to control topological phonon transport and phonon-driven magnetism in quantum materials.

### [42] [HVAF Spraying of NiTi Coatings: Microstructure, Phase Transformation and Shape Memory Behavior](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01997)

Method: 研究采用高速空气燃料热喷涂法（high velocity air fuel thermal spray method），在低碳钢基体上使用四组不同工艺参数沉积NiTi涂层，随后对涂层的化学成分、孔隙率、微观结构、相变行为及功能性热力学性能进行评估。

Result: 成功制备出厚度为100-300微米的厚NiTi涂层，涂层虽存在微观结构不均匀、孔隙、氧化物颗粒、高密度位错缺陷（dislocation defects）和内应力，但仍能在冷却或机械加载时发生马氏体相变（martensitic transformation）。退火后涂层展现出三点弯曲测试中的热驱动效应（thermal actuation），以及纳米压痕和划痕测试中的形状记忆效应（shape memory effects），但拉伸强度有限。

Conclusion: 高速空气燃料热喷涂法可成功制备具有功能性热力学性能和良好附着力的厚NiTi涂层，尽管存在微观缺陷，退火处理是涂层展现功能性热力学性能的必要条件。该涂层在热驱动和形状记忆方面具有潜在应用价值。

Abstract: Depositing various coatings on surface of engineering components with the aim to improve their performance concerning wear, corrosion, friction and thermal protection is already a standard practice. Depositing metallic NiTi shape memory alloy coatings may be a viable alternative for hard ceramic coatings. NiTi coatings offer additional benefits originating from unique functional thermomechanical properties. However, fabrication of thick NiTi coatings turned out to be difficult. Standard electroplating and laser cladding methods are not suitable for NiTi the most widely used plasma spray methods tend to produce chemically inhomogeneous coatings that do not transform martensitically, cold sprayed NiTi coatings suffer from poor adhesion to the substrates. In this work we report on first ever successful fabrication of thick NiTi coatings (100-300 um) that display functional thermomechanical properties and simultaneously show very good adherence to the substrate. We used high velocity air fuel thermal spray method to fabricate NiTi coatings deposited on mild steel using four different sets of processing parameters. Chemical composition, porosity, microstructure, phase transformation and functional thermomechanical properties of the NiTi coatings were evaluated. Although the coatings contain inhomogeneous microstructure, voids, oxide particles, high density of dislocation defects and internal stress, they undergo martensitic transformation upon cooling and or mechanical loading. As sprayed NiTi coatings need to be annealed to display functional thermomechanical properties. Despite their limited tensile strength, the coatings displayed thermal actuation in 3 point bending tests and shape memory effects in nanoindentation and scratch tests.

Further analysis reveals that Pd- and Ag-substituted monolayers remain selective for $NO$, while Zn substitution favors $NO_2$ detection even in ambient atmospheric conditions. Abstract: Hydrogen chemisorption on graphitic carbon modifies the carbon orbital hybridization from sp2 to sp3, altering both structural and electronic properties. To this end, we investigate here the evolution of the C 1s core-level lineshape in nanoporous graphene (NPG) and vertically aligned carbon nanotubes (CNTs) upon hydrogenation, exploiting soft-to-hard X-ray photoemission spectroscopy to achieve a depth-resolved analysis. Abstract: In a combined experimental and theoretical study, we demonstrate anisotropic polariton transport on the nanoscale in the van der Waals antiferromagnet CrSBr. ### [47] [Differentiable inverse design of short-range order in high-entropy alloys: from target sro to target property](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02219)
*Tiancheng Ding,Conrard Giresse Tetsassi Feugmo*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于梯度下降（gradient descent）的短程有序（SRO）结构构建方法，替代传统的随机交换搜索（reverse Monte Carlo），将原子占据视为连续变量，实现了更快速、更准确的多主元合金（multi-principal-element alloys）结构设计，并结合小神经网络闭环预测力学性能，最终以开源Python包（anisro）发布。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多主元合金的力学性能受短程有序（short-range order, SRO）控制，但传统设计流程将结构构建与性能验证割裂为两个独立问题，缺乏统一优化路径，导致设计效率低下。

Method: 采用梯度下降（gradient descent）方法，将原子占据率处理为连续变量而非固定离散值，替代传统随机交换搜索（reverse Monte Carlo）；引入源自双元素体系并推广至多元素的物理校正项，确保设计结构在热力学上的合理性；训练一个小型神经网络，直接从成分和SRO统计量预测力学性能。

Result: 在小体系中精度与随机交换方法相当；在4000原子大体系中速度提升6倍、精度提升8倍；在9种面心立方（face-centered-cubic, FCC）和体心立方（body-centered-cubic, BCC）合金上，成功捕捉了-20%至+57%的SRO驱动刚度变化；在钴铬镍合金上，四个目标刚度中三个的偏差在6%以内；证实至少需要864个原子才能正确捕捉SRO方向与幅度。

Conclusion: 该方法提供了一条基于梯度、由性能驱动的合金设计实用路径，并已以开源Python包（anisro）形式发布，克服了传统方法在大体系与多元素场景下的效率瓶颈。

Abstract: Short-range order (SRO) governs the mechanical response of multi-principal-element alloys, but designing an alloy for a target property usually means solving two disconnected problems: building a structure matching a desired SRO pattern, then separately checking its property, with no shared optimization. This work replaces the standard random-swap search (reverse Monte Carlo) with a gradient-based approach: atom occupancy is treated as continuous rather than fixed, so the whole process can be tuned using gradient descent, the same method used to train neural networks. This builder matches random-swap accuracy on small systems, but is six times faster and eight times more accurate on large 4000-atom systems, and scales smoothly to alloys with many elements without extra bookkeeping. A physics-based correction term, adapted from prior two-element work and extended here to many elements, keeps designed structures thermodynamically realistic rather than just numerically matching the target SRO pattern. A small neural network then predicts mechanical properties directly from composition and SRO statistics, closing the loop from target property back to structure. Tested on nine face-centered-cubic and body-centered-cubic alloys, the pipeline captured SRO-driven stiffness changes from -20% to +57%, and cell-size checks showed at least 864 atoms are needed to get the direction and size of these changes right, since the commonly used 108-atom cells can mislead. Against real simulations for a cobalt-chromium-nickel alloy, the method matched three of four target stiffness values within 6%. The method is released as an open-source Python package, anisro, offering a practical route to gradient-based, property-driven alloy design.

</details>


### [48] [Ultrafast Demagnetization Governed by Spin Fluctuations in CaRuO$_{3}$/SrTiO$_{3}$ Superlattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02224)
*Yu-Han Gao,Wen-Xiao Shi,Yuan-Sha Chen,Ji-Rong Sun,Qing-Lin Yang,Xu Yang,Zhuo Deng,Peng-Tao Yang,Zheng Chang,Hong-Mei Feng,Wei He,Xiang-Qun Zhang,Zhao-Hua Cheng*

Method: 实验上，作者在CaRuO₃/SrTiO₃超晶格中测量退磁速率随温度、泵浦注量（pump fluence）和外加磁场的依赖关系。理论上，将三温度模型（three-temperature model）与自洽重整化理论（self-consistent renormalization theory）整合，建立唯象模型来解释反常的退磁加速行为。

Result: 实验发现退磁速率随温度、泵浦注量和外加磁场的升高而增加（即反常加速），与传统铁磁体在临界点附近的行为相反。模型揭示，超晶格的内禀梯度磁性（intrinsic gradient magnetism）抑制了比热（specific heat）的典型发散，从而解除了热力学瓶颈，使超快动力学主要由自旋涨落驱动的电子-自旋散射顶点增强所主导。

Conclusion: 空间不均匀性可以解除宏观热力学奇点与微观散射过程之间的耦合，为在关联量子材料（correlated quantum materials）中操控超快自旋动力学提供了新范式。退磁速率对外部参数的显著敏感性进一步表明，可利用磁不稳定性附近的增强涨落来设计高度可调谐的超快自旋电子器件（ultrafast spintronic devices）。

Abstract: For ultrafast magnetization switching devices, critical slowing down in conventional ferromagnets near their Curie temperature constitutes a key challenge that must be overcome. In contrast to this typical behavior, we observe an anomalous acceleration of demagnetization in CaRuO$_{3}$/SrTiO$_{3}$ superlattices, a moderately correlated weak itinerant ferromagnet. The demagnetization rate increases with rising temperature, pump fluence, and applied magnetic field. To explain these anomalous phenomena, we develop a phenomenological model integrating the three-temperature model with self-consistent renormalization theory. Because the intrinsic gradient magnetism of the superlattice suppresses the typical divergence of specific heat, the conventional thermodynamic bottleneck is bypassed. Our model reveals that this decoupling enables the ultrafast dynamics to be predominantly governed by the spin-fluctuation-driven enhancement of the electron-spin scattering vertex. Our work demonstrates how spatial inhomogeneity can decouple macroscopic thermodynamic singularities from microscopic scattering processes, offering a new paradigm for manipulating ultrafast spin dynamics in correlated quantum materials. The pronounced sensitivity of the demagnetization rate to external parameters further suggests the potential for designing highly tunable ultrafast spintronic devices that leverage enhanced fluctuations near the magnetic instability.

Abstract: The time auto-correlation of auxiliary wave functions (TACAW) method enables efficient simulations of ultra-low-loss electron energy loss spectra (EELS) arising from vibrational and magnon excitations. In practical applications to realistic materials systems, however, TACAW calculations become challenging due to the large system sizes required for models containing defects, interfaces, impurities, or grain boundaries, as well as the substantial computational cost and data throughput associated with molecular dynamics and multislice calculations. Here we discuss a practical methodology for large-scale TACAW simulations and present torched-TACAW, a freely available implementation of the TACAW part of the described workflow for efficient STEM-EELS simulations. The overall approach combines molecular dynamics based on foundational machine-learned interatomic potentials, partitioning of elongated supercells, and on-the-fly processing of multislice outputs in order to enable near ab initio quality simulations with tractable memory use and data flow. Using rutile TiO2 as a model system, we analyze important numerical aspects of the method, including windowing and supercell partitioning, and demonstrate atomic-resolution STEM-EELS simulations for thick samples.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 钽（Tantalum, Ta）是实现超导量子比特（superconducting qubit）长退相干时间（coherence time）的候选材料，但其微观结构与宏观性能之间的构效关系（structure-property relationship）尚不清楚，亟需系统研究。

Method: 在温度为20°C至600°C范围内、以及在不同种子层（seed layers）——铌（Nb）、氮化钛（TiN）和氮化钽（TaN）——上，通过溅射沉积（sputter-deposition）制备200 nm厚的Ta薄膜；利用表面形貌、残余电阻比（residual-resistance ratio）、晶体相组成、超导转变温度（superconducting transition temperature）以及共面波导谐振器（coplanar waveguide resonator）射频性能（RF-performance）进行表征；对X射线衍射（XRD）数据进行Williamson-Hall分析，并结合截面高分辨透射电子显微镜（cross-sectional HR-TEM）直接观察界面无序程度。

Result: 在温度高于500°C及所有种子层上均可获得α-Ta薄膜；在单光子区域（single-photon regime）、100 mK温度下测量到高达150万的内禀品质因子（internal quality factor）；不同种子层上的α-Ta薄膜尽管体材料性质相似，但射频性能差异显著；Williamson-Hall分析显示微应变（microstrain）减小与品质因子提高之间存在明确相关性；截面HR-TEM直接解析了界面无序（interfacial disorder），进一步支持该结论。

Conclusion: 结果强调界面工程（interface engineering）在优化用于低损耗量子计算电路（low-loss quantum computing circuitry）的超导薄膜（superconducting thin films）中发挥关键作用。

Abstract: Tantalum (Ta) is a promising material for reaching long coherence times in superconducting qubits. A detailed understanding of the underlying structure-property relationship remains elusive though. In the present study, we sputter-deposited 200 nm thick Ta films on high-resistivity silicon (100) substrates at temperatures ranging from T = 20°C to 600°C, as well as on different seed layers (Nb, TiN and TaN). Alpha-Ta thin films were readily obtained at temperatures above 500°C and on all seed layers. The films were characterized in terms of surface morphology, residual-resistance ratio, crystal phase composition and superconducting transition temperature, as well as RF-performance using coplanar waveguide resonators. Internal quality factors of up to 1.5 million were measured at 100 mK in the single-photon regime. Despite similar bulk material properties, alpha-Ta films on different seed layers exhibit markedly different RF-performance, which we attribute to dissimilar strain and structural defects at the substrate-metal interfaces. Williamson-Hall analysis of XRD data reveals a clear correlation between decreasing microstrain and increasing quality factor. Cross-sectional HR-TEM further supports this interpretation by directly resolving interfacial disorder. Our results highlight the critical role of interface engineering in optimizing superconducting thin films for low-loss quantum computing circuitry.

</details>


### [51] [From Bloch to Néel: Anisotropy-dependent Domain-Wall Character in FePd Thin Films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02256)
*Annika Stellhorn,Alicia Backs,Ekaterina Klyushina,Connie Bednarski-Meinke,Steffen Tober,Denis Vasiukov,Oskar Stepancic,Vítor Alexandre de Oliveira Lima,Lukas Aniansson,Paul Steadman,Manuel Valvidares,Jörg Schwenke,Claudiu Bulbucan,Elizabeth Blackburn*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本实验利用圆二色X射线共振磁散射（CD-XRMS）等技术，研究了具有高垂直磁各向异性（perpendicular magnetic anisotropy）的L1₀-FePd薄膜中依赖于深度的畴壁形成机制，发现长程有序度对手性自旋结构（chiral spin textures）的深度演变起关键作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究具有高垂直磁各向异性的L1₀-FePd薄膜中畴壁形成（domain wall formation）的深度依赖特性，并阐明磁晶各向异性强度与长程有序度对手性自旋结构的影响。

Method: 采用圆二色X射线共振磁散射（circular dichroism X-ray resonant magnetic scattering, CD-XRMS）随入射X射线角度的变化，结合CD-STXM、CD-ptychography以及结构有序度、磁性质和表面形貌的宏观表征，对不同磁晶各向异性强度的两个FePd样品进行深度演变分析。

Result: 高磁晶各向异性样品（Q_{PMA}=1.8）表现出出乎意料大的Néel贡献，角度依赖的CD-XRMS直接揭示了从上层FePd区域的混合Bloch-Néel手性向下界面的纯Néel型结构的平滑转变。第二样品（Q_{PMA}=1.45）的畴壁则为纯Néel型。

Conclusion: 长程结构有序度（long-range structural order）在确定L1₀-FePd薄膜中磁结构的形成过程中起着至关重要的作用。

Abstract: We report an experimental investigation of the depth-dependent domain wall formation in L1$_0$-FePd thin films with high perpendicular magnetic anisotropy. Using circular dichroism X-ray resonant magnetic scattering (CD-XRMS) as a function of the incident X-ray angle, we explore the depth evolution of chiral spin textures in two samples with different strengths of magnetocrystalline anisotropy. Combined with CD-STXM, CD-ptychography, and macroscopic characterization of the structural order, magnetic properties, and surface morphology, we relate these observations to differences in the long-range order of the L1$_0$ phase of FePd. One FePd thin film with very high magnetocrystalline anisotropy, characterized by $Q_{PMA}=1.8$, exhibits an unexpectedly large Néel contribution. Angular-dependent CD-XRMS directly reveals a smooth transition from a hybrid Bloch-Néel chirality within the upper FePd layer towards a purely Néel-type structure at the lower FePd interface. In the second FePd sample, despite a still relatively large $Q_{PMA}=1.45$, the domain walls were found to be purely Néel type. These results indicate a crucial role of the long-range structural order in determining the formation of the magnetic structure.

### [52] [Bottlenecks in Hamiltonian-Adaptive Resolution Simulation Method for Modeling Interfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02415)
*Hari Haran Sudhakar,Alessandra Serva,Rocio Semino*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文深入分析了哈密顿自适应分辨率模拟（H-AdResS）方法在界面体系应用中的关键参数选择问题，发现Langevin恒温器比Nosé-Hoover更可靠，而短程静电力模型（如Damped Shifted Force）可能导致非物理结果，并讨论了力与能量不连续性的截断策略及键合自由度渐近插值的局限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: H-AdResS方法能在一个模拟盒子中结合原子尺度与粗粒化（coarse-grained）模型，非常适合包含界面或反应区域的体系。然而，前序工作发现该方法在界面体系（如MOF/CO₂界面）中的正确使用并不简单，因此需要深入分析恒温器方案和长程静电力模型的选择对其结果的影响。

Method: 采用H-AdResS方法，在LAMMPS 2023平台上开展界面模拟，系统比较不同恒温器（Langevin与Nosé-Hoover）以及不同静电力模型（包括短程Damped Shifted Force方法）的表现，并讨论截断策略（capping strategies）及键合自由度插值的可行性。

Result: Langevin恒温器是H-AdResS的可靠选择，而Nosé-Hoover会产生伪影；短程静电力模型（Damped Shifted Force）在界面建模中可能导致非物理结果；无法通过修改H-AdResS哈密顿量来实现键合自由度的渐近插值。

Conclusion: 该研究为H-AdResS模拟的正确设置提供了指导，帮助研究人员判断该方法是否适用于准确建模其目标体系。

Abstract: The Hamiltonian-Adaptive Resolution Simulation (H-AdResS) method allows to combine atomistic and particle-based coarse-grained models in a single simulation box, which makes it very attractive to model systems containing interfaces or reactive regions surrounded by an interacting environment. In our previous work [arXiv:2604.21867], we implemented H-AdResS in LAMMPS 2023 and extended its use to interfaces, focusing on MOF/CO$_2$ interfaces as an example. We found that, despite its advantages, using this method properly for this kind of systems is not trivial. In this work, an in-depth analysis of the impact of the choice of thermostatting schemes and long-range electrostatics models is presented. Even though its Hamiltonian formulation enables performing H-AdResS simulations within constant temperatures ensembles, not every thermostat is appropriate. We demonstrate that Langevin thermostat is a reliable choice for this method, while Nosé-Hoover results in artifacts. In addition, we show that using short-range models such as the Damped Shifted Force method for electrostatics, a popular choice for H-AdResS simulations, can lead to non-physical results when modeling interfaces. The need of capping strategies to deal with discontinuities in forces and energies arising from abrupt changes in resolution is also discussed. Finally, the impossibility of changing the definition of the H-AdResS Hamiltonian to include a gradual interpolation of the bonded degrees of freedom is discussed. We hope that this contribution helps the reader to appropriately set up H-AdResS simulations and to assess if this method can be used to accurately model their system of interest.

</details>

# cs.AI [[Back]](#toc)

### [53] [Grounded autonomous research: a fault-tolerant LLM pipeline from corpus to manuscript in frontier computational physics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02329)
*Haonan Huang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出一个从 arXiv 论文语料到发表级稿件的端到端自主科研流水线（pipeline），在凝聚态物理领域（11,083 篇论文）实现了从研究方向构思、方法校准、第一性原理计算到论文撰写全流程的自主操作，通过冗余设计（新鲜上下文隔离、分布式锚定、对抗性审查）实现容错，并识别出数值性面对（numerical confrontation）作为核心锚定机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 前沿物理科学研究与机器学习沙盒有本质差异：物理推理贯穿所有方法选择、工具链文档不足、校准必须依赖外部文献锚点（external literature anchors），而无框架（unscaffolded）的智能体会信口编造看似合理但不可验证的结果。现有自主科研智能体无法有效应对物理科学中的方法学校准与文献验证需求。

Method: 构建一个端到端流水线，从包含 11,083 篇凝聚态物理 arXiv 论文的语料出发，经过六个阶段、47 个新鲜上下文（fresh-context）会话，共享仅磁盘状态（on-disk state），累计 2,162 次文献咨询事件。采用冗余容错机制：新鲜上下文隔离、分布式锚定（distributed grounding）、对抗性审查（adversarial review），并设置前架构基线（pre-architecture baseline）和无导引消融（no-pilot ablation）作为对照。

Result: 该流水线自主产出一篇包含三项实质性物理发现（关于交变磁性压电效应，altermagnetic piezomagnetism）的发表级稿件。前导和导引后阶段（pre- and post-pilot stages）完全自主，导引阶段（pilot）仅在复现失败时需要有限的人类介入（操作性知识整理，非科学方向指导）。对比实验表明，在校准检查点进行结构性数值性面对是有效的锚定机制。

Conclusion: 该研究识别了自主科研智能体的基本操作原语（primitives）、特征化失效模式（characterized failure modes）以及量化的介入模式（quantified intervention pattern），为计算物理之外的高风险科学领域中的自主研究奠定了方法论基础。

Abstract: Autonomous-research agents have demonstrated end-to-end LLM automation in machine-learning sandboxes where execution provides calibration. Frontier physical science differs categorically: physical reasoning underlies every methodology choice, toolchains are often underdocumented, and calibration must come from external literature anchors - which unscaffolded agents cite but do not confront, hallucinating plausible, unverifiable results from internal priors. We present a pipeline that runs end-to-end from a corpus of 11,083 recent condensed-matter physics arXiv papers to a publication-grade manuscript with three substantive physics findings (here on altermagnetic piezomagnetism): the agent autonomously conceives a research direction by mapping the corpus, calibrates methodology by reproducing published references, conducts novel first-principles computations, and writes the manuscript - grounded in literature throughout, across 47 fresh-context sessions in six phases sharing only on-disk state, with 2,162 literature-consultation events. Fault tolerance emerges from redundancy: fresh-context isolation, distributed grounding, and adversarial review catch what any single session misses; pre- and post-pilot stages are fully autonomous, and pilot requires bounded human intervention only at reproduction failures - operational knowledge curation, not scientific direction. Two paired failure modes - a pre-architecture baseline and a no-pilot ablation - isolate structurally enforced numerical confrontation at calibration checkpoints as the operative grounding mechanism. The primitives, characterized failure modes, and quantified intervention pattern lay a foundation for autonomous research in high-stakes scientific domains beyond computational physics.

</details>

### [54] [Nomic Structure and Reduction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01289)
*Sean Gryb,Karim P. Y. Thébault*

Main category: physics.hist-ph

TL;DR: 本文针对具有不规则法则结构（irregular nomic structure）的物理理论的正则形式化表述展开分析，指出其运动方程的不适定性（ill-posedness）与一种有害的过剩表征能力（surplus representational capacity）相关。通过辛约化（symplectic reduction）可将此类理论转化为具有规则法则结构与适定初值问题的理论。论文综合并对比了多种约束哈密顿理论（constrained Hamiltonian theories）的表述与分析路径，提出不规则法则结构的情形最适合采用范畴论（category theory）表述，其中态空间（state spaces）被视作箭头（arrows），辛约化被视作箭头的复合（arrow composition），并由此得出态空间同构的理论等价、约化态空间同构的理论在规则法则结构表征层面等价的自然结论。该分析为后续处理不规则法则结构理论的量子化（quantization）奠定了基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 具有不规则法则结构的物理理论在正则表述中面临运动方程不适定与过剩表征能力带来的困难，亟待建立统一且严密的形式化框架来分析与转化这类理论，并为其后续量子化提供理论准备。

Method: 综合并对比多种约束哈密顿理论的表述与分析方法，借鉴Gryb与Thébault（2024）关于模型空间法则结构形式化的近期工作，以及Bradley与Weatherall（2020）和Bradley（2025b）运用范畴论比较理论结构与表征能力的方法，提出以态空间为箭头、辛约化为箭头复合的范畴论表述方案。

Result: 在该范畴论框架下自然得出两个结论：态空间同构的理论是等价的；约化态空间（reduced state spaces）同构的理论在规则法则结构表征层面是等价的。

Conclusion: 该分析为不规则法则结构理论的量子化提供了合适的形式基础，量子化问题将在后续论文中处理。

Abstract: The canonical formulation of physical theories with irregular nomic structure is as constrained Hamiltonian theories within which ill-posedness of the equations of motion is connected to a pernicious form of surplus representational capacity. Such theories can be converted into theories with regular nomic structure and a well-posed initial value problem via the process of symplectic reduction. We analyse, synthesise, and contrast different approaches to the presentation and analysis of constrained Hamiltonian theories, drawing upon recent work on formalisation of nomic structure on model spaces (Gryb and Thébault 2024) and comparisons of theoretical structure and representational capacity via category theory (Bradley and Weatherall 2020; Bradley 2025b). We suggest that the case of irregular nomic structure is most naturally suited to a category theoretic presentation in which state spaces are arrows and symplectic reduction is arrow composition (Landsman 2005). Under this approach one obtains the natural results that theories with isomorphic state spaces are equivalent and theories whose reduced state spaces are isomorphic are equivalent at the level of the regular representations of their nomic structure. This analysis provides a suitable foundation for the case of quantization of theories with irregular nomic structure, which will be in a companion paper.

</details>


### [55] [Black Boxes in Black Hole Imaging](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02110)
*Juliusz Doboszewski,Jamee Elder*

Main category: physics.hist-ph

TL;DR: 探讨黑洞成像中计算机模拟与机器学习方法的认知不透明性（epistemic opacity），区分了不影响推理可靠性的不透明性与当前制约理解的模型不透明性（GRMHD模型）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究黑洞成像中计算机模拟和机器学习方法的认知不透明性问题，特别是评估这种不透明性是否以及如何影响科学推理的可靠性。

Method: 采用哲学分析与案例研究相结合的方式，基于（下一代）事件视界望远镜（Event Horizon Telescope, EHT）的情境，论证了某些形式的不透明性（包括机器学习带来的不透明性）在更广泛的推理框架中不一定损害推理的可靠性。

Result: 识别出两类不透明性：一类是可以通过嵌入更广泛推理框架而维持可靠性的不透明性；另一类是当前存在于人马座A*（Sagittarius A*）的广义相对论磁流体动力学（GRMHD）模型中的问题性不透明性，后者限制了当前对该源模型的理解以及机器学习模型在未来观测中的潜在用途。

Conclusion: 部分认知不透明性（包括机器学习带来的）不影响推理可靠性；但GRMHD模型的不透明性揭示了当前对黑洞源模型理解的局限性，并对未来ML模型的应用构成约束。

Abstract: We investigate the epistemic opacity of computer simulations and machine learning methods in the context of black hole imaging. We argue that there are forms of opacity-including opacity resulting from the use of machine learning-which do not need to affect the reliability of an inference when it is seen as a part of a broader inferential framework. We propose conditions under which that can plausibly be the case, and discuss how opaque methods can be useful in the context of the (next generation) Event Horizon Telescope. However, we also argue that at least one problematic form of opacity is currently present in black hole imaging: GRMHD models of Sagittarius A* are opaque. This form of opacity signals the limitations of current understanding of the models of this source, and constrains the potential uses of ML models in future observations.

### [56] [Efficient high-order explicit symplectic splitting methods for post-Newtonian Hamiltonian systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01596)
*Yujie Jiang,Lijie Mei*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文针对后牛顿（post-Newtonian, PN）哈密顿系统提出了一种新的加倍相空间（doubled phase space）扩展与分裂方法，构造出无阶数降阶（order reduction）的高阶显式辛积分器（explicit symplectic integrator），在2PN自旋双星模拟中验证了其优越的长时间守恒性与计算效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 后牛顿哈密顿系统（post-Newtonian Hamiltonian system）的非可分离性（nonseparability）通常需要计算昂贵的隐式积分器（implicit integrator）。近期虽通过加倍相空间（doubled phase space）实现了显式辛方法（explicit symplectic method），但现有高阶显式积分器在时间步长较小时会出现阶数降阶（order reduction）问题，影响收敛精度。

Method: 提出一种新的加倍哈密顿量（doubled Hamiltonian）扩展与分裂（splitting）方法，在此基础上构造经过特别设计的显式辛积分器（explicit symplectic integrator）。该方法利用小PN参数（small PN parameter）的优势，避免了高阶方法的阶数降阶现象。

Result: 在2PN自旋双星（2PN spinning binaries）模拟中，所提出积分器在长时间守恒性（long-term conservation of invariants）方面优于隐式方法及现有显式分裂技术（explicit splitting technique），同时计算效率显著更高。

Conclusion: 本文方法实现了真正的高阶收敛（genuine high-order convergence），且不存在阶数降阶问题，为后牛顿哈密顿系统的高效、高精度数值模拟提供了可行的显式辛方案。

Abstract: The nonseparability of post-Newtonian (PN) Hamiltonian systems typically necessitates the use of computationally expensive implicit integrators. Recent research overcomes this limitation by embedding the dynamics into a doubled phase space, which enables the development of explicit symplectic methods. However, existing specially designed explicit integrators suffer from order reduction for high-order methods when the time stepsize is small, i.e., $h <\varepsilon^3$. In this paper, we propose a novel extension and splitting approach for the doubled Hamiltonian, under which specially designed explicit symplectic integrators can be constructed. It is shown that the proposed integrators achieve genuine high-order convergence without order reduction and take advantage of the small PN parameter $\varepsilon$. Numerical results from simulations with 2PN spinning binaries demonstrate superior long-term conservation of invariants and significantly higher computational efficiency compared to both implicit methods and existing explicit splitting techniques.

</details>

### [57] [Study of ZZ and ZH production in the bb$ττ$ final state and search for high-mass spin-0 and spin-1 resonances in proton-proton collisions at $\sqrt{s}$ = 13 TeV](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01589)
*CMS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文基于CMS实验在质心能量13 TeV、积分亮度138 fb⁻¹的质子-质子对撞数据，首次对ZZ和ZH过程在bbττ末态中的产生进行了研究。非共振分析针对标准模型ZZ和ZH过程，共振分析则探测超出标准模型的重粒子（自旋0的X→ZZ和自旋1的Z'→ZH），设定质量在0.2–6 TeV范围内的产生截面上限，未观测到偏离标准模型的信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在测量Z玻色子对（ZZ）以及Z玻色子与希格斯玻色子（ZH）的联合产生，聚焦于bbττ末态。非共振分析因该道在非共振希格斯玻色子对产生（nonresonant Higgs boson pair production）搜索中的关键作用而受到激励；共振分析则用于搜索超出标准模型（beyond the standard model）的新物理信号。

Method: 利用CMS探测器在大型强子对撞机（LHC）上收集的质子-质子对撞数据（质心能量√s=13 TeV，积分亮度138 fb⁻¹），对bbττ末态进行非共振与共振两类分析。非共振分析针对标准模型ZZ和ZH过程；共振分析搜索衰变为ZZ的自旋-0共振态X（质量范围0.2–5 TeV）和衰变为ZH的自旋-1共振态Z'（质量范围0.5–6 TeV）。

Result: 在95%置信水平上，给出产生率与分支比乘积的上限：σ(X)B(X→ZZ)的范围为300 pb到24 fb，σ(Z')B(Z'→ZH)的范围为0.4 pb到12 fb。这是首次对ZZ/ZH→bbττ过程的实验测量。未观测到标准模型预期的偏离。

Conclusion: 这是首次对ZZ/ZH→bbττ过程的直接测量，所得上限结果在多个TeV质量区间内排除了超出标准模型信号的存在，确认当前数据与标准模型预言一致。

Abstract: A study of the production of pairs of Z bosons (ZZ) and of the associated production of a Z boson and a Higgs boson (ZH) in final states containing two b quarks and two tau leptons (bb$ττ$) is presented. The analysis is based on proton-proton collisions collected at $\sqrt{s}$ = 13 TeV by the CMS experiment at the LHC, corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 138 fb$^{-1}$. The nonresonant analysis targets the standard model ZZ and ZH processes in the bb$ττ$ final state, motivated by the prominent role of this channel in searches for nonresonant Higgs boson pair production. The resonant searches target physics beyond the standard model, probing heavy spin-0 resonances X that decay into ZZ and spin-1 resonances Z' that decay into ZH, with masses in the 0.2$-$5 and 0.5$-$6 TeV ranges, respectively. Upper limits at 95% confidence level are set on the product of production rate and branching fraction $σ$(X)$\mathcal{B}$(X $\to$ ZZ), ranging from 300 pb to 24 fb, and $σ$(Z')$\mathcal{B}$(Z' $\to$ ZH), ranging from 0.4 pb to 12 fb. These are the first measurements to probe the ZZ/ZH $\to$ bb$ττ$ processes. No deviation from standard model expectations is observed.

</details>


### [58] [Heavy-Flavor Electron Classification Using Hadronic Environment as Point Cloud](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02225)
*Jingyu Zhang,Wanbing He,Long Ma*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本研究利用点云（point cloud）表示强子环境，采用多种基于集合的机器学习架构（包括Transformer模型）来分离来自粲（charm）和底（bottom）强子的半轻子衰变电子。在约40%效率的工作点下，分类器纯度接近80%，且显著优于人工构建的可观测量基准。分析表明，模型主要依赖强子环境的几何与拓扑（topological）特征进行判别，并捕获了超出少量手动构造变量的有效区分信息。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 来自粲（charm）和底（bottom）强子半轻子衰变的电子是高能碰撞中的重要探针，但由于两者衰变拓扑结构的高度相似性，有效区分它们仍然是一个挑战性问题。

Method: 将强子环境表示为点云（point cloud），采用多种基于集合的机器学习架构（包括Transformer模型）进行粲/底起源电子的分类。通过模型响应与物理可观测量之间的关系分析以及特征扰动测试（feature perturbation tests）来理解模型所学表征。

Result: 不同架构间性能可比，表明主要限制来自粲与底强子结构的内在相似性而非模型表达能力。在约40%效率的实验相关工作点下，测试数据集上的纯度接近80%，显著优于基于手动构建可观测量的BDT基线。学习到的表征主要对强子环境的几何与拓扑（topological）属性敏感，并捕获了超出少量手动构造变量的非平凡区分信息。

Conclusion: 基于点云的机器学习方法能有效分离粲和底起源的电子，但性能瓶颈在于衰变结构的内在相似性。模型成功提取了超越传统手动构造变量的有效几何与拓扑判别特征。

Abstract: Electrons from semi-leptonic decays of charm (D) and bottom (B) hadrons are important probes in high-energy collisions, while their separation remains challenging due to the similarity of the underlying decay topologies. In this work, we represent the hadronic environment as a point cloud and investigate a hadron-based approach for distinguishing charm- and bottom-origin electrons using several set-based machine learning architectures, including Transformer models. Comparable performance is observed across different architectures, indicating that the dominant limitation originates from the intrinsic similarity between charm- and bottom-related hadronic structures rather than model expressivity. At an experimentally relevant working point corresponding to approximately 40% efficiency, the classifier achieves a purity close to 80% on the test dataset and significantly improves the classification performance relative to a hand-crafted observable BDT baseline. By studying the relation between the model response and physics-motivated observables, together with feature perturbation tests, we find that the learned representation is primarily sensitive to geometric and topological properties of the hadronic environment. Comparisons with high-level observables further suggest that the learned representation captures nontrivial discriminating information beyond a small set of manually constructed variables.

### [59] [Measurement of solar $pp$ neutrino flux with the new PandaX-4T data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02405)
*PandaX Collaboration,Peiyuan Chen,Wei Chen,Xiaohua Chen,Xun Chen,Yunhua Chen,Chen Cheng,Xiangyi Cui,Yuxin Cui,Manna Deng,Roni Dey,Yingjie Fan,Deqing Fang,Xuanye Fu,Zhixing Gao,Yujie Ge,Lisheng Geng,Xunan Guo,Xuyuan Guo,Zichao Guo,Chencheng Han,Ke Han,Changda He,Jinrong He,Ruquan Hou,Houqi Huang,Junting Huang,Yule Huang,Xiangdong Ji,Yonglin Ju,Xiaorun Lan,Chenxiang Li,Mingchuan Li,Peiyuan Li,Shuaijie Li,Tao Li,Yangdong Li,Yuan Li,Zhiyuan Li,Qing Lin,Jianglai Liu,Yuanchun Liu,Yunyang Luo,Yugang Ma,Yajun Mao,Yue Meng,Binyu Pang,Ningchun Qi,Xiangxiang Ren,Dong Shan,Xiyuan Shao,Manbin Shen,Wenliang Sun,Xuyan Sun,Yi Tao,Yueqiang Tian,Yuxin Tian,Anqing Wang,Guanbo Wang,Hao Wang,Haoyu Wang,Jiamin Wang,Lei Wang,Meng Wang,Qiuhong Wang,Shaobo Wang,Shibo Wang,Siguang Wang,Wei Wang,Xu Wang,Zhou Wang,Yuehuan Wei,Weihao Wu,Yuan Wu,Mengjiao Xiao,Xiang Xiao,Yuhan Xie,Kaizhi Xiong,Jianqin Xu,Yifan Xu,Binbin Yan,Xiyu Yan,Yong Yang,Shunyu Yao,Peihua Ye,Chunxu Yu,Zhe Yuan,Youhui Yun,Minzhen Zhang,Peng Zhang,Shibo Zhang,Shu Zhang,Siyuan Zhang,Tao Zhang,Wei Zhang,Yang Zhang,Yingxin Zhang,Yuanyuan Zhang,Kangkang Zhao,Li Zhao,Jiaxu Zhou,Jiayi Zhou,Jifang Zhou,Ning Zhou,Xiaopeng Zhou,Zhizhen Zhou,Chenhui Zhu*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用PandaX-4T探测器的Run 2数据（曝光量1.9吨·年），探测器在Run 2前经过升级以改善响应和本底条件；利用物理数据自身及气体分析系统约束放射性惰性气体杂质的时间变化；改进数据处理链、探测器响应表征和本底模型；对20–1000 keV范围内的电子反冲数据进行盲法谱分析（blind spectral analysis）。

Result: 结合此前Run 0数据，拟合得到pp中微子通量为(8.5 ± 3.5)×10¹⁰ cm⁻²s⁻¹，与标准太阳模型预言一致；在电子反冲能量低于165 keV的能区，信号统计显著性为2.2σ，首次给出该低能区太阳pp中微子-电子弹性散射的正指示。

Abstract: We report a new measurement of the solar proton--proton ($pp$) neutrino flux via neutrino--electron elastic scattering using the PandaX-4T Run 2 data set collected between 2024 and 2026, corresponding to an exposure of 1.9 tonne$\cdot$yr. Before Run 2 data taking, the detector underwent a series of upgrades to improve its response and background conditions. Time variations of radioactive noble-gas impurities are constrained using the physics data themselves, complemented by measurements from the gas-assay system. The analysis introduced improvements in the data processing chain, detector response characterization, and background models. A blind spectral analysis was then performed on the electronic-recoil data across a wide energy range from 20 to 1000 keV. In combination with the Run 0 data published earlier, the fitted $pp$ flux is $(8.5 \pm 3.5)\times 10^{10}$ $\mathrm{cm^{-2}s^{-1}}$, consistent with the prediction of the Standard Solar Model. With a statistical significance of $2.2σ$ above background, this marks the first positive indication of solar $pp$ neutrino--electron scattering below an electronic-recoil energy of 165 keV.

### [60] [From Dirac Cones to Semions: An Exact Finite-Size Theory of Parity-Anomaly Transport in Chiral Spin Liquids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01341)
*Kumar Ghosh*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过严格推导柱面上带隙狄拉克锥（gapped Dirac cone）的奇宇称行列式，解决了手性自旋液体（chiral spin liquids）中陈数、陈-西蒙斯规范场能级与自旋霍尔电导之间的混淆问题，证明有限周长修正是严格指数的，并在笼目晶格（kagome lattice）上通过三个独立层次验证了从微观自旋子陈数到物理自旋霍尔电导的精确映射。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手性自旋液体中存在一个隐藏的“记账”问题：分数化自旋子的整型陈数（Chern number）、涌现陈-西蒙斯规范场（Chern–Simons gauge field）的能级，以及实验或模拟中实际测量的分数化自旋响应，这三者是相关但截然不同的量，而文献中经常将它们混为一谈。本文旨在理清这些概念并建立严格的定量映射。

Method: 在空间柱面上严格推导了带隙狄拉克锥的奇宇称行列式（parity-odd determinant），对紧致和乐（compact holonomy）进行全阶求和而非仅截断至领头阶。随后在笼目晶格上通过三个独立层次进行验证：精确的部分子能带结构计算、以及相互作用的密度矩阵重整化群（density-matrix renormalization group, DMRG）通量泵浦模拟。

Result: 证明了有限周长对拓扑响应的修正是严格指数的，不存在普适的1/L项；建立了从微观自旋子陈数到物理自旋霍尔电导（spin Hall conductance）的精确映射。数值验证结果：部分子能带计算给出陈数C=-1，在4到12格点宽的柱面上呈指数收敛；DMRG通量泵浦得到自旋响应ν_s=-0.500±0.011，与无任何可调参数的分析预测一致。

Conclusion: 这些结果将单圈反常计算（one-loop anomaly calculation）转化为一个经过定量验证的桥梁，连接了微观拓扑与可观测的分数化响应，为手性自旋液体中拓扑响应与微观陈数之间的精确对应关系提供了严格的理论基础。

Abstract: Chiral spin liquids carry a hidden bookkeeping problem: the integer Chern number of their fractionalized spinons, the level of the emergent Chern--Simons gauge field, and the fractional spin response actually measured in experiment or simulation are related but distinct quantities, and the literature routinely conflates them. Here we resolve this by deriving the exact parity-odd determinant of a gapped Dirac cone on a spatial cylinder, resummed to all orders in the compact holonomy rather than truncated at leading order. The result proves that finite-circumference corrections to the topological response are strictly exponential, with no universal $1/L$ term, and fixes the precise map from microscopic spinon Chern number to physical spin Hall conductance. We validate this chain of reasoning on the kagome lattice at three independent levels: an exact parton band-structure calculation ($C=-1$, converging exponentially over cylinders four to twelve sites wide), and an interacting density-matrix renormalization group flux pump ($ν_s=-0.500\pm0.011$) that agrees with the analytic prediction without any adjustable parameter. Together, these results turn a one-loop anomaly calculation into a quantitatively verified bridge between microscopic topology and observable fractional response.

</details>


### [61] [Quantum Tunneling-induced Hybridization and Coherent Dynamics of Jackiw-Rebbi Zero Modes in a Modified Su-Schrieffer-Heeger Chain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01344)
*Surajit Mandal*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过解析与数值方法研究了一种改进SSH模型中Jackiw-Rebbi零模的隧穿诱导杂化与相干动力学，揭示了有限重叠导致的零能简并解除、双井系统类型的相干振荡现象，并建立了统一的理论框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索改进SSH模型中JR零模的隧穿效应与相干动力学，建立连接拓扑零模、量子隧穿与相干演化的统一框架。

Method: 采用解析分析与数值模拟相结合的方法，包括低能狄拉克理论（Dirac theory）推导有效质量反转、量子隧穿的两能级有效描述。

Result: 发现：1) 二阶JR零模通过量子隧穿解除零能简并，产生对称-反对称杂化态；2) 出现两个JR模之间的相干占据概率振荡及子晶格极化周期性转移；3) 振荡周期由杂化能隙（hybridization gap）调控。

Conclusion: 建立了改进SSH系统中JR零模、量子隧穿与相干动力学的统一框架，为可调控拓扑量子态转移提供了潜在的实验平台。

Abstract: We investigate analytically and numerically the tunneling-induced hybridization and coherent dynamics of Jackiw-Rebbi (JR) zero modes in a modified Su-Schrieffer-Heeger (SSH) model. Unlike the conventional SSH model, this modified system possess two bulk gap closing points, namely, the quadratic-type gap closing point at $k=0$ and the Dirac-type gap closing point at $k=\pmπ/4a$. While the quadratic point does not support a topological domain wall due to the absence of mass inversion, the low-energy Dirac theory around $k=\pmπ/4a$ predicts an effective mass that changes sign at two spatially separated interfaces under a kink profile, generating a pair of JR bound states localized at those interfaces. We show that finite overlap between the JR zero modes lifts the zero-energy degeneracy through quantum tunneling, producing symmetric-antisymmetric hybridized states analogous to a quantum mechanical double-well system. An effective two-level description reveals coherent oscillations of the occupation probability between the two JR modes, accompanied by periodic transfer of sublattice polarization between the (A,C) and (B,D) sectors. The oscillation period is governed by the hybridization gap, providing a tunable route for controlling topological bound states. Our results establish a unified framework connecting JR zero modes, quantum tunneling, and coherent dynamics in modified SSH systems, offering a promising platform for controllable topological quantum-state transfer in engineered lattice structures.

### [62] [Generalized quantum geometry formulated through interacting vertex correlations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01434)
*Alejandro S. Miñarro,Gervasi Herranz*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出将量子几何（quantum geometry）从传统的布洛赫能带几何（Bloch-band geometry）扩展到更一般的流形（manifold）上，其中绝热参数代表基态的形变，包括集体玻色子涨落、外场或结构畸变。广义量子几何张量（quantum geometric tensor）由相互作用顶点的关联编码，从而将量子几何推广到结构、集体和相互作用多体系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统量子几何仅将晶体动量（crystal momentum）作为参数空间，局限于布洛赫能带体系。然而，波函数演化的参数空间不止于此，因此需要将量子几何推广至更一般的流形，以描述包含集体激发、外场和结构畸变在内的多体系统中的几何性质。

Method: 通过将量子几何张量推广到由基态形变参数定义的流形上，证明了广义量子几何张量可由形变参数共轭的相互作用顶点关联函数（correlations of interacting vertices）编码。以Hubbard-Stratonovich玻色子场和Jahn-Teller构型空间为例进行说明。

Result: 表明量子几何可以扩展到布洛赫能带几何之外，适用于更一般的流形；广义量子几何张量与相互作用顶点的关联函数直接相关。

Conclusion: 所提出的形式体系以一般流形为框架，将量子几何推广到结构、集体和相互作用的多体系统中，拓展了量子几何的应用范围。

Abstract: Quantum geometry characterizes the variation of electron wavefunctions in solids along a parameter space. Conventionally, crystal momentum is chosen as the parameter, since it couples to electromagnetic fields, offering an interpretation of quantum geometry in terms of dipole matrix elements, polarization fluctuations, and optical responses. However, Bloch momentum is not the only possible parameter space in which a wavefunction can evolve. In this work, we show that quantum geometry can be extended beyond the bare Bloch-band geometry to manifolds whose adiabatic parameters represent deformations of the ground state, including collective bosonic fluctuations, external fields, or structural distortions. We show that the generalized quantum geometric tensor is encoded by correlations of interacting vertices, conjugate to the deformation parameters. By way of illustration, we briefly discuss the application of these extended geometric concepts to manifolds generated by Hubbard-Stratonovich bosonic fields, or Jahn-Teller configurational spaces. The formulation presented here is framed by general manifolds, which extend quantum geometry to generic structural, collective, and interactive many-body systems.

### [63] [Nonperturbative Nonlinear Hall Effect in Nonequilibrium Steady States](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01519)
*Lei Geng,Martin Eckstein,Lei Chen,Shouvik Sur,Silke Paschen,Qimiao Si,Philipp Werner*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于非平衡稳态格林函数（nonequilibrium steady-state Green's functions）的非微扰方法，用于研究直流电场驱动的晶格系统中的非线性霍尔效应（nonlinear Hall effect），超越了传统常数弛豫时间近似和微扰框架的局限，并揭示了相互作用和电子-声子自能对强场霍尔信号的显著影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管非线性霍尔效应在量子材料中受到广泛关注，但现有研究大多局限于弱场微扰（perturbative）区域。因此需要发展一种能够处理强场非微扰（nonperturbative）区域的通用理论框架。

Method: 采用非平衡稳态格林函数方法，通过自能（self-energies）引入耗散和相互作用，超越了常数弛豫时间近似（constant relaxation-time approximation），并同时处理带间跃迁（interband transitions）和带内跃迁（intraband transitions）。

Result: 将方法应用于两带半金属模型，成功获取了非微扰交叉区域（Berry曲率热点）之外的强场霍尔响应，并发现常数弛豫时间估计和Berry曲率偶极子（Berry curvature dipole）计算在该区域不可靠。进一步表明，基于动力学平均场理论（dynamical mean-field theory）的相互作用和电子-声子自能可以显著改变霍尔信号。

Conclusion: 该框架能够对非平衡非线性霍尔现象进行定量模拟，并为强场输运实验提供理论指导。

Abstract: The nonlinear Hall effect in quantum materials has attracted broad interest, yet most existing studies focus on the weak-field, perturbative regime. Here we develop a nonperturbative approach based on nonequilibrium steady-state Green's functions for dc-field-driven lattice systems, with dissipation and interactions incorporated through self-energies beyond the constant relaxation-time approximation and interband transitions treated alongside their intraband counterparts. Applied to a two-band semimetal model, our approach provides direct access to the strong-field Hall response beyond the nonperturbative crossover where the edge of the nonequilibrium distribution reaches Berry-curvature hot spots, a regime in which constant relaxation-time estimates and Berry curvature dipole calculations become unreliable. We further demonstrate that interaction and electron-phonon self-energies within dynamical mean-field theory can substantially change the Hall signal. Our framework enables quantitative simulations of nonequilibrium nonlinear Hall phenomena and provides guidance for strong-field transport experiments.

### [64] [Ultrasonic Observation of Slowing Down of Multipole Fluctuations in Sr$_2$RuO$_4$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01720)
*Ryosuke Kurihara,Mitsuhiro Akatsu,Shunsuke Yaoita,Keisuke Mitsumoto,Yuichi Nemoto,Yoshiyuki Yoshida,Hiroshi Yaguchi,Terutaka Goto*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过超声测量研究了非常规超导体 Sr₂RuO₄ 在超导转变温度 (T_c = 1.4 K) 附近电子态的动力学性质，观测到面内横向超声衰减系数的增大，并基于群论提出电十六极 (electric hexadecapole) 自由度在涨落减缓中起关键作用，进而讨论了多分量超导序参量与多极自由度之间的关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究非常规超导体 Sr₂RuO₄ 中超导转变温度附近电子态的动力学性质（dynamical properties），揭示其超导机制背后的微观自由度。

Method: 对 Sr₂RuO₄ 进行超声测量 (ultrasonic measurements)，测量面内横向超声衰减系数 (in-plane transverse ultrasonic attenuation coefficient)；施加 10 T 磁场抑制超导转变以区分超导与多极效应；结合群论分析 (group-theoretical considerations) 进行对称性解释。

Result: 超声衰减系数在接近 T_c 时增大，呈现 Landau-Khalatnikov 型频率依赖关系，典型弛豫时间 (relaxation time) 约为 10⁻¹⁰ s；10 T 磁场下超导转变被抑制，但衰减系数在低温下仍持续增大，表明与多极自由度 (multipole degrees of freedom) 相关的涨落减缓 (slowing down of fluctuations) 仍然存在。

Conclusion: 电十六极自由度是导致涨落减缓的关键因素；多分量超导序参量 (multi-component superconducting order parameters) 与多极自由度之间存在内在关联，可能对理解 Sr₂RuO₄ 的超导配对机制具有重要意义。

Abstract: We performed ultrasonic measurements on the unconventional superconductor Sr$_2$RuO$_4$ to investigate the dynamical properties of the electronic states near its superconducting transition temperature, $T_\mathrm{c} = 1.4$ K. We observed an increase in the in-plane transverse ultrasonic attenuation coefficient as the temperature approached $T_\mathrm{c}$. The ultrasonic attenuation exhibited a Landau-Khalatnikov-type ultrasonic frequency dependence with a typical relaxation time of approximately $10^{-10}$ s. Under an applied magnetic field of 10 T, the superconducting transition was suppressed. However, the ultrasonic attenuation coefficient exhibited an increase down to low temperatures, indicating the slowing down of fluctuations associated with multipole degrees of freedom. Based on group-theoretical considerations, we propose that the electric hexadecapole plays a crucial role in the slowing down. Furthermore, we discuss the relationship between multi-component superconducting order parameters and multipole degrees of freedom.

</details>


### [65] [Evidence for Deconfined Magnetic Order in the Kitaev-$J_3$ Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01815)
*Jiucai Wang,Chuan Chen*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 基于变分蒙特卡洛计算与vison-准粒子分析，本文证明Kitaev-J₃蜂窝模型中的退禁闭磁性相（zigzag或反铁磁序）与残留的ℤ₂拓扑结构共存，磁性序源于vison对凝聚而单vison保持能隙开放，并提供解释异常低温热输运的微观机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 突破磁性序与自旋液体（spin liquid）行为的传统二分法，探索自旋液体中部分序（partial order）与分数化（fractionalization）共存的退禁闭磁性相的存在性及其微观机制。

Method: 采用变分蒙特卡洛（variational Monte Carlo）计算，并结合对母体Kitaev自旋液体的vison-准粒子（vison-quasiparticle）分析，在环面（torus）上考察多个线性无关的拓扑扇区（topological sectors）。

Result: 优化后的变分波函数在环面上保留了多个线性无关的拓扑扇区，而常规有序相的波函数坍缩至单一扇区；磁性序由vison对凝聚（vison-pair condensation）自然产生，单vison保持能隙；所得相进一步支持具有多个马约拉纳锥（Majorana cones）的无能隙自旋子（gapless spinons）。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了通向分数化磁性（fractionalized magnetism）的微观路径，为解释磁有序Kitaev材料（如Na₂Co₂TeO₆）中反常低温纵向热输运提供了可能的微观场景。

Abstract: We investigate the Kitaev-$J_3$ honeycomb model using variational Monte Carlo calculations combined with a vison-quasiparticle analysis of the parent Kitaev spin liquid (KSL). We provide evidence for deconfined magnetic phases in which zigzag or antiferromagnetic order coexists with remnant $\mathbb{Z}_2$ topological structure inherited from the KSL. The optimized variational wave functions retain multiple linearly independent topological sectors on a torus, whereas those of conventional ordered phases collapse to a single sector. The vison-quasiparticle analysis shows that magnetic order naturally arises from vison-pair condensation while single visons remain gapped, yielding a microscopic mechanism for magnetic ordering without immediate confinement. The resulting phases further host gapless spinons with multiple Majorana cones, offering a possible microscopic scenario for the anomalous low-temperature longitudinal thermal transport reported in magnetically ordered Kitaev materials such as Na$_2$Co$_2$TeO$_6$. Our results reveal a microscopic route to fractionalized magnetism beyond the conventional dichotomy between magnetic order and spin-liquid behavior.

### [66] [Plaid-Like Spin Splitting and Chirality of Magnon Bands in Antiferromagnetic MnTe$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02114)
*Dirk Wulferding,Daehyeon An,Jiwon Choi,Dongmin Mun,Youngsu Choi,Sivasakthi Kuppusamy,Sritharan Krishnamoorthi,Raman Sankar,Myung Joon Han,Se Kwon Kim,Kwang-Yong Choi*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 交变磁体（altermagnet）是一类兼具补偿反铁磁序（compensated antiferromagnetic order）与晶体对称性导致的自旋分裂激发的新型磁性材料，尽管理论兴趣浓厚，其实验识别仍十分困难。

Method: 采用螺旋性与角度分辨拉曼散射（helicity- and angle-resolved Raman scattering）测量；结合基于密度泛函理论（DFT+$U$）的第一性原理计算与线性自旋波理论（linear spin-wave theory）进行理论分析。

Result: 拉曼测量揭示了磁振子（magnon）的约化旋转对称性以及左、右圆偏振通道的显著不平衡，表明存在动量依赖的磁振子手性（momentum-dependent magnon handedness）。第一性原理计算进一步在动量空间中发现了特征性的格子状自旋分裂结构（plaid-like spin-splitting structure）。

Conclusion: MnTe₂中的磁振子自旋织构（magnon spin textures）由非常规的子晶格对称性决定，并与交变磁体能带的自旋分裂行为高度相似。该工作提供了此类非共面反铁磁体中独有的手性自旋波激发（chiral spin-wave excitations）的实验证据。

Abstract: Altermagnets constitute an emerging class of magnetic materials that combine compensated antiferromagnetic order with spin-split excitations arising from crystalline symmetries. Despite strong theoretical interest, their experimental identification remains challenging. Here, we demonstrate that helicity- and angle-resolved Raman scattering measurements reveal reduced rotational symmetries of magnons and a pronounced imbalance between left- and right-circular polarization channels, indicating momentum-dependent magnon handedness. First-principles DFT+$U$ calculations combined with linear spin-wave theory uncover a characteristic plaid-like spin-splitting structure in momentum space. The resulting magnon spin textures are dictated by the unconventional sublattice symmetries of MnTe$_2$ and closely emulate those of altermagnetic electronic bands. Our work provides evidence of chiral spin-wave excitations unique to this non-coplanar antiferromagnet.

### [67] [Unconventional Mixed-Parity Magnetism in Rare-Earth Tetraborides](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02117)
*Dong-Choon Ryu,Jae-Ho Han,Bongjae Kim,Chang-Jong Kang*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本研究在三维补偿磁体TbB₄中发现了一种由标量自旋手性（scalar spin chirality）驱动的分量分辨混合宇称自旋劈裂（component-resolved mixed-parity spin splitting），其中面内分量呈现奇宇称p波和f波纹理，而面外分量保持偶宇称d波交变磁（altermagnetic）特征，并由此产生非相对论性Edelstein效应、自旋霍尔响应及贝里曲率偶极子等独特输运现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统交变磁（altermagnetism）研究将非相对论性自旋劈裂严格分类为纯偶宇称或纯奇宇称的自旋纹理。本文旨在揭示一种超越传统分类的新型自旋劈裂机制——在完全三维补偿磁体中实现分量分辨的混合宇称自旋劈裂。

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）、紧束缚模型（tight-binding model）和$\mathbf{k} \cdot \mathbf{p}$模型，结合自旋群对称性分析（spin-group symmetry analysis），对TbB₄的非共面基态（non-coplanar ground state）进行研究。

Result: TbB₄的面内自旋分量呈现奇宇称的p波和f波纹理，而面外分量保持偶宇称的d波交变磁特征。奇宇称纹理的共存并非由相对论性自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）驱动，而是由标量自旋手性（scalar spin chirality）引起的交错贝里相位（staggered Berry phase）所致。该混合宇称结构产生了体非相对论性Edelstein效应、自旋霍尔响应（spin Hall response）以及对称性允许的贝里曲率偶极子（Berry curvature dipole）。

Conclusion: 稀土四硼化物（rare-earth tetraborides）被确立为工程设计复杂自旋-电荷转换现象（spin-charge conversion phenomena）的鲁棒平台。

Abstract: Altermagnetism has advanced the study of compensated magnets by revealing non-relativistic spin splitting, traditionally classified into strictly even- or odd-parity spin textures. Here, we unveil a fundamentally different regime: component-resolved mixed-parity spin splitting in a fully three-dimensional compensated magnet. Using first-principles calculations, tight-binding and $\mathbf{k} \cdot \mathbf{p}$ models, along with spin-group symmetry analysis, we demonstrate that the non-coplanar ground state of $\mathrm{TbB}_4$ enforces a unique momentum-space spin texture. The in-plane spin components exhibit odd-parity $p$- and $f$-wave-like textures, whereas the out-of-plane component retains an even-parity $d$-wave altermagnetic character. Crucially, the coexistence of the in-plane odd-parity textures is driven not by relativistic spin-orbit coupling, but by a staggered Berry phase arising from the inherent scalar spin chirality. This mixed-parity structure dictates distinct transport fingerprints, including bulk non-relativistic Edelstein and spin Hall responses, as well as a symmetry-allowed Berry curvature dipole. These results establish the rare-earth tetraborides as a robust platform for engineering complex spin-charge conversion phenomena.

</details>


### [68] [Phonon spectral function of Holstein polaron: Investigation of many-body effects with self-energy and vertex correction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02136)
*Lawrence Rai,Sudhakar Pandey*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文在反绝热（antiadiabatic）区域内，通过满足电荷守恒 Ward 恒等式（Ward identity）的弱耦合方法，研究了多体效应对一维 Holstein 极化子（Holstein polaron）声子谱函数的影响。发现电子自能（electron self-energy）和顶角修正（vertex corrections）对极化子谱权重有相反的贡献，两者在长波模式（小波矢）下近乎抵消，而在靠近布里渊区边界（大波矢）时，电子自能主导导致谱权重显著抑制。弱耦合微扰方法在深反绝热区域可靠，但当声子能量接近电子带宽时需考虑准粒子谱重整化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究多体效应对一维 Holstein 极化子声子谱函数的影响，特别是在反绝热区域中电子自能项和顶角修正项各自的贡献机制。

Method: 采用满足电荷守恒 Ward 恒等式的弱耦合微扰方法（weak-coupling perturbative approach），同时计入电子自能和顶角修正对声子谱函数的贡献。

Result: 电子自能抑制极化子谱权重，而顶角修正增强之；两者强度均随声子波矢增大而增加。小波矢模式下两者近乎抵消，大波矢模式下电子自能增长更快，导致谱权重显著抑制。

Conclusion: 弱耦合微扰方法在深反绝热区域可靠；当声子能量接近电子带宽时，必须考虑准粒子谱的重整化（renormalization）才能准确估计多体效应。

Abstract: We study the impact of the many-body effects on the phonon spectral function of Holstein polaron in one-dimension in the antiadiabatic regime by incorporating the contributions from the electron self-energy and vertex corrections within a weak-coupling approach that respects the charge-conserving Ward identity. We find that while the polaronic spectral weight is suppressed due to contribution from the electron self-energy, on the other hand, the same is enhanced due to contribution from the vertex corrections. While strength of both the contributions increases with increasing the wave vector ($\q$) of phonons, they nearly cancel each other for the small-$\q$ modes so that the polaronic spectral weight is weakly affected due to the many-body effects. For the large-$\q$ modes near the zone boundary, the net many-body correction is dominated by the contribution of the electron self-energy which increases faster in comparison to that of the vertex corrections with increasing the wave vector thereby resulting in a significant suppression of the polaronic spectral weight. We find that while the weak-coupling perturbative approach provides a reliable estimation of the impact of the many-body effects deep inside the antiadibatic regime, the renormalization of quasiparticle spectrum must be taken into account for an accurate estimation when the phonon energy approaches the electronic bandwidth.

</details>


### [69] [A density matrix renormalization group approach to quantum point contacts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02183)
*Nair Aucar Boidi,Mikhail Kiselev*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文利用密度矩阵重整化群（DMRG）结合修正向量法，研究一维费米子系统中谐振势与排斥相互作用之间的竞争。通过调节势垒曲率，可在势阱（冷原子系统）与量子势垒（介观系统如量子点接触）之间连续过渡，并分析基态粒子分布与局域态密度（LDOS）谱权重的演变。结果表明，在势垒区谱中出现局域化峰，势阱区弱相互作用时出现于空穴区，而强相互作用下外势效应被关联效应掩盖。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究一维费米子系统中谐振势（harmonic potential）与排斥相互作用之间的竞争机制，理解外势的形状（势阱与势垒）如何影响基态粒子分布与局域态密度（LDOS）的谱特征。

Method: 采用密度矩阵重整化群（density matrix renormalization group, DMRG）方法，并结合修正向量法（correction-vector method）进行数值计算。

Result: 在势垒（barrier）区，电子部分（ω>0）的谱中出现局域化峰；在势阱（well）区且弱相互作用下，类似局域化特征出现在空穴部分（ω<0）；当相互作用增强时，LDOS不再显示外势的明显特征。

Conclusion: 强相互作用下关联效应（correlations）主导体系行为，掩盖了单粒子受限（single-particle confinement）效应；外势的竞争结果依赖于相互作用强度与势场曲率的综合作用。

Abstract: Using the density matrix renormalization group (DMRG) combined with the correction-vector method, we investigate the competition between an harmonic potential and repulsive interactions in a one-dimensional fermionic system. The parabolic confinement induces spatial inhomogeneity, and by tuning its curvature one can continuously interpolate between a potential well--relevant for cold-atom setups--and a quantum barrier, as realized in mesoscopic systems such as quantum point contacts. We analyze how the ground-state particle distribution evolves with the strength and sign of the confining potential and how the confinement reshapes the spectral weight of the local density of states (LDOS) at the center of the chain. In the barrier regime, a localized peak emerges in the electron part of the spectrum ($ω>0$) as a direct consequence of the potential. In contrast, in the well configuration and for weak interactions, a localized feature persists but shifts to the hole sector ($ω<0$). However, for stronger interactions, the LDOS no longer displays clear signatures of the external potential, indicating that correlations dominate over single-particle confinement.

</details>


### [70] [Fundamental limitations of single-particle Green's-function zeroes as probes of many-body topology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02326)
*Emile Pangburn,Olivier Gingras*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文证明，基于单粒子格林函数（Green's functions）构建的拓扑不变量无法可靠诊断相互作用多体态的拓扑性质。通过耦合相互作用SSH链的实例，揭示自旋-自旋相互作用可使多体基态平凡化，而不影响格林函数拓扑不变量。该失效源于格林函数无法探测与拓扑简并相关的Fock区电子激发，因此格林函数零点不能表征相互作用拓扑相。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验基于单粒子格林函数（single-particle Green's function）的拓扑不变量在相互作用多体系统中的可靠性，澄清格林函数零点（GF zeroes）是否与物理拓扑准粒子（topological quasiparticles）存在关联，以及其能否作为相互作用拓扑相（interacting topological phases）的普适判据。

Method: 以耦合相互作用的SSH链（Su-Schrieffer-Heeger chain）作为最小模型，通过引入自旋-自旋相互作用（spin-spin interaction），对比多体基态拓扑性质与单粒子格林函数拓扑不变量的行为差异，分析格林函数在探测Fock区（Fock sectors）电子激发方面的能力限制。

Result: 自旋-自旋相互作用可以使多体基态变得平凡（trivial），但基于单粒子格林函数的拓扑不变量保持不变，表明后者无法检测到拓扑相变。格林函数无法探测与拓扑简并（topological degeneracy）相关的Fock区电子激发，导致其零点不对应物理拓扑准粒子。

Conclusion: 单粒子格林函数拓扑不变量不能可靠诊断相互作用多体态的拓扑性质。格林函数零点在一般情况下无法表征相互作用拓扑相，需要发展新的拓扑判据来正确描述强关联系统中的拓扑序（topological order）。

Abstract: We show that topological invariants constructed from single-particle Green's functions (GFs) cannot reliably diagnose the topology of interacting many-body states. Using coupled interacting SSH chains as a minimal example, we demonstrate that a spin-spin interaction can trivialize the many-body ground state without affecting the GF topological invariant. This breakdown originates from the GF's inability to probe electronic excitations in the Fock sectors responsible for the topological degeneracy. Consequently, GF zeroes are not associated with physical topological quasiparticles and cannot generally characterize interacting topological phases.

</details>


### [71] [Anomalous thermopower from the drag of overdamped collective modes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02449)
*G. Mirarchi,G. Seibold,M. Grilli,S. Caprara*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过类比标准声子曳引（phonon drag）机制，提出在过阻尼集体模式（overdamped collective mode）下（阻尼系数随温度降低而增大）可产生热电功率异常，并认为过阻尼电荷密度涨落（overdamped charge density fluctuations）是高温超导铜氧化物中反常金属行为（strange-metal behavior）的可能解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高温超导铜氧化物中观测到的塞贝克系数比（Seebeck coefficient ratio）在低温下呈现看似对数发散（logarithmic divergence）的行为，这一现象缺乏合理解释。

Method: 通过理论分析，将标准声子曳引机制推广至过阻尼集体模式情形，考察阻尼系数随温度降低而增大时热电功率（thermopower）的异常行为。

Result: 研究结果表明，过阻尼集体模式能够导致金属热电功率出现反常特征，与实验中观察到的对数发散行为一致。

Conclusion: 该发现为理解多种体系中观测到的反常金属行为提供了新线索，并支持过阻尼电荷密度涨落是高温超导铜氧化物中该行为之成因的假说。

Abstract: Inspired by the observation of a Seebeck coefficient ratio that exhibits a seemingly logarithmic divergence at low temperature in high-temperature superconducting cuprates, we show that a mechanisms similar to the standard phonon drag can give rise to anomalies in the thermopower of a metal, if the dragged collective mode is overdamped, with a damping coefficient that increases with lowering the temperature. Our finding adds a piece to the puzzle of the strange-metal behavior observed in many different systems and supports our proposal that overdamped charge density fluctuations can be responsible of such a behavior in high-temperature superconducting cuprates.

</details>

### [72] [Ising superconductivity and anomalous metallic states in a bulk crystal with artificial unidirectional stacking layers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01302)
*Xiangqi Liu,Chen Xu,Haonan Wang,Runfeng Zhang,Ziyi Zhu,Zhengyang Li,Lianbing Wen,Ze Yan,Fanbo Shen,Jiawei Luo,Zhengtai Liu,Xia Wang,Leiming Chen,Ke Qu,Jianping Sun,Jinguang Cheng,Shiwei Wu,Zhenzhong Yang,Dawei Shen,Yanfeng Guo*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文报道了一种通过平面Sr-Cl网络实现NbS₂层从反平行AB堆叠到单向平行AA堆叠的结构重构，从而在块体晶体中创造出全局非中心对称的准二维超导态，展现出极端超导各向异性、远超泡利顺磁极限的上临界场以及磁致反常金属态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索宏观块体晶体中的二维极限，为研究奇异量子相提供平台。传统插层仅能扩大层间距，无法改变层间堆叠方式；本文旨在通过堆叠几何工程（stacking-geometry engineering）实现块体晶体中的全局非中心对称准二维超导态。

Method: 合成Sr₀.₇₅ClNbS₂超导体，利用平面Sr-Cl网络强制所有NbS₂层从天然的反对称AB堆叠（antiparallel AB stacking）重构为单向平行AA堆叠（unidirectional parallel AA stacking）。

Result: 实现了具有D₃h点群对称性的全局非中心对称块体晶体；观测到极端超导各向异性（γ ~ 77）、面内上临界场（~10.65 T）远超泡利顺磁极限（Pauli paramagnetic limit）；发现磁致反常金属态（anomalous metallic state），其特征为有限耗散但霍尔响应消失。

Conclusion: 堆叠几何工程是在块体晶体中人工构建全局非中心对称准二维超导态的有效策略，为设计具有可调晶体对称性和电子能带拓扑的量子材料开辟了新途径。

Abstract: The two-dimensional (2D) limit in macroscopic bulk crystals provides a powerful platform for exploring exotic quantum phases. Here, we report the synthesis of a Sr0.75ClNbS2 superconductor that achieves unidirectional, parallel AA stacking-a configuration never before realized in a bulk crystal. Unlike conventional intercalation, which merely expands the interlayer spacing, our approach employs a planar Sr-Cl network to enforce a complete stacking reorganization, driving all NbS2 layers from the native antiparallel AB stacking into a unidirectional, parallel AA arrangement. This stacking switch globally breaks inversion symmetry, transforming centrosymmetric 2H-NbS2 into a noncentrosymmetric bulk crystal with D3h point group symmetry. Crucially, this structural design reproduces, in three dimensions, the electronic environment of an isolated monolayer, thereby preventing cancellation of the local Ising fields. As a result, strong Ising spin-orbit coupling and spin-split bands persist throughout the bulk. Transport measurements reveal extreme superconducting anisotropy (γ ~ 77), an in-plane upper critical field (~ 10.65 T) that far exceeds the Pauli paramagnetic limit, and clean-limit superconductivity indicative of high crystalline quality. Moreover, magnetotransport uncovers a novel magnetic-field-induced anomalous metallic state characterized by finite dissipation yet a vanishing Hall response. Direct band-structure measurements corroborate the layer-decoupled, quasi-2D electronic nature of the system. This work establishes stacking-geometry engineering as a powerful strategy to artificially enforce a globally noncentrosymmetric, quasi-2D superconducting state in bulk crystals, paving the way for designing quantum materials with tunable crystalline symmetry and electronic band topology.

</details>


### [73] [Fermiology and spin polarization of topological surface states in PtBi$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01947)
*Anders Christian Mathisen,Xin Liang Tan,Stefanie Suzanne Brinkman,Kristian Mæland,Fabian Göhler,Øyvind Finnseth,Grigory Shipunov,Falk Pabst,Manuel Alonso Lemos,Balasubramanian Thiagarajan,Craig Polley,Björn Trauzettel,Anna Isaeva,Jorge I. Facio,Hendrik Bentmann*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文利用自旋和角分辨光电子能谱（spin- and angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy, SARPES）揭示了层状PtBi₂中费米弧表面态（Fermi-arc surface states）的单重简并性（singly degenerate）和自旋极化（spin-polarized），证实了其非平庸拓扑性质，并发现费米弧色散对表面终止层（surface termination）具有显著依赖性。这些观测结果为PtBi₂中拓扑超导电性（topological superconductivity）的可能出现提供了关键先决条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 层状PtBi₂被认为是费米弧表面态中可能产生拓扑超导电性的候选材料，但其拓扑性质与超导关联的关键微观特征尚未得到实验证实。本文旨在通过实验手段验证费米弧表面态的自旋极化、简并性及其非平庸拓扑结构，从而为拓扑超导电性的实现提供必要条件。

Method: 采用自旋和角分辨光电子能谱（SARPES）对PtBi₂的费米弧表面态进行测量，结合第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）对比不同表面终止层下的色散行为。

Result: 实验证实PtBi₂的费米弧表面态是单重简并且自旋极化的，确立了其非平庸拓扑性质。此外，费米弧的色散显著依赖于表面终止层，表现为近扁平（nearly flat）或近似线性（approximately linear）两种行为，与第一性原理计算一致。

Conclusion: 观测到的自旋极化和依赖于表面终止层的费米弧表面态带宽，揭示了PtBi₂中拓扑超导电性潜在涌现的关键微观物理要素。

Abstract: Layered PtBi$_2$ is a candidate for topological superconductivity arising in Fermi-arc surface states. Using spin- and angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy, we demonstrate that the Fermi arcs in PtBi$_2$ are singly degenerate and spin-polarized, which establishes their nontrivial topology and constitutes a necessary condition for topological superconductivity. We further uncover a pronounced surface-termination dependence of the Fermi-arc dispersion, yielding either nearly flat or approximately linear bands in agreement with first-principles calculations. Together, the observed spin polarization and termination-dependent bandwidth of the Fermi-arc surface states identify key ingredients underlying the potential emergence of topological superconductivity in PtBi$_2$.

</details>


### [74] [Disorder-induced superconductivity in graphene](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02267)
*Jannes van Poppelen,Tomas Löthman,Annica M. Black-Schaffer*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该论文利用单层石墨烯（monolayer graphene）作为范例，论证了超导现象（superconductivity）可以完全由无序（disorder）诱导产生，无需依赖晶体有序性。通过引入低浓度的空位或氢化，在弱吸引相互作用下即可实现宏观超导相位相干（superconducting phase coherence）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点认为无序对关联物相（correlated phases）有害，但实验中如非晶Al和Bi的超导增强现象表明存在例外。本文旨在探索无序本身是否足以成为超导的起源。

Method: 以单层石墨烯为模型体系，通过理论分析引入低浓度空位（vacancies）或氢化（hydrogenation）所产生的无序效应，研究其对超导序参量、超流权重（superfluid weight）以及转变温度的影响。分别考虑常规s波配对（s-wave pairing）和非常规近邻配对（nearest-neighbor pairing）两种情形。

Result: 在常规s波配对下，无序在任意弱吸引相互作用下均能诱导出有限超导序参量。全局相位相干（global phase coherence）通过纯几何起源的有限超流权重建立，而非形成孤立的超导液滴（superconducting puddles）。在空位的非手征极限（chiral limit）以及氢化情况下，弱相互作用下仍具有有限转变温度和超流权重。对于通常更易被无序破坏的非常规近邻配对，超导表现出类似量子临界（quantum-critical-like）行为，但相位相干在弱相互作用下仍持续存在，并呈现混合d波对称性（mixed d-wave symmetries）。

Conclusion: 该工作证明，宏观超导相位相干可以稳健地由微观无序工程化（engineered）产生，为理解无序诱导的超导现象提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: Correlated phases of matter are typically investigated in crystalline systems, where disorder is considered to be detrimental. However, intriguing exceptions exist, such as superconductivity being enhanced in amorphous realizations of Al and Bi. Here, we demonstrate that superconductivity can even emerge entirely from disorder, using monolayer graphene as an example. In the clean limit, the semi-metallic nature of graphene requires prohibitively strong electronic interactions to achieve superconductivity. Despite the inherently random nature of disorder, we show that introducing low concentrations of vacancies or hydrogenation in graphene provides a large density of low-energy states that easily induce superconductivity. For conventional $s$-wave pairing, disorder induces a finite superconducting order parameter for arbitrarily weak attractive interactions. Rather than forming isolated superconducting puddles, global phase coherence is established through a finite superfluid weight of purely geometrical origin. Away from the chiral limit of vacancies, hydrogenation similarly yields a finite transition temperature and nonzero superfluid weight for weak interactions. For unconventional nearest-neighbor pairing, typically more disrupted by disorder, superconductivity exhibits quantum-critical-like behavior, yet phase coherence persists at low interaction strengths, with mixed $d$-wave symmetries. Our work demonstrates the robust emergence of macroscopic superconducting phase coherence engineered entirely from microscopic disorder.

</details>
