### [75] [Elasto-Hydrodynamic Propulsion of a Magnetically Actuated Filament](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01512)
*Sohum Kapadia,Julien Chopin,Arshad Kudrolli*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文建立了包含偶极磁头的弹性细丝在低雷诺数（low-Reynolds-number）粘性流体中受振荡场驱动的弹性-水动力学（elasto-hydrodynamic, EH）模型，并发现游泳速度在泳体长度与弹性-水动力学长度（EH length）同量级时达到最大值，且粘性边界贡献对定量准确性至关重要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有预设运动学（prescribed-kinematics）模型无法自洽描述弹性细丝在磁驱动下的真实形变和前进运动，亟需一个能自洽耦合驱动、弹性与流体力学边界条件（boundary conditions, BCs）的理论框架来研究其推进机制。

Method: 采用弹性-水动力学（elasto-hydrodynamic, EH）框架，将欧拉-伯努利梁力学（Euler-Bernoulli beam mechanics）与阻力理论（resistive force theory）耦合，结合力和力矩边界条件（BCs）自洽求解细丝形状及净前进运动。

Result: 粘性边界贡献对定量准确性不可或缺；游泳动力学由EH长度和新引入的磁-粘-弹性行程振幅（magneto-viscous-elastic stroke amplitude）共同支配。游泳速度随泳体长度与EH长度之比呈现非单调变化，当二者同量级时速度达到最大值。

Conclusion: 尾部边界条件在解析极限下可近似为自由端；忽略粘性对边界条件的贡献将导致模型出现局限性。

Abstract: We investigate the low-Reynolds-number propulsion of a slender elastic filament with a dipolar magnetic head actuated by an oscillating field in a viscous fluid by studying its strokes and net forward motion. To capture these dynamics, we employ an elasto-hydrodynamic (EH) framework that couples Euler-Bernoulli beam mechanics with resistive force theory. Unlike prescribed-kinematics models, filament shapes here emerge self-consistently from the actuation and the force and torque boundary conditions (BCs). We demonstrate that viscous boundary contributions are crucial for quantitative agreement and show that the swimming dynamics are governed by the EH length and a magneto-viscous-elastic stroke amplitude introduced here. The swimming speed is non-monotonic with increasing ratio of the swimmer length to the EH length, and is shown to reach a maximum when the swimmer length is on the order of the EH length. We further discuss the analytical limit in which the tail BCs can be described as free, and the limitations that arise when viscous contributions to the BCs are ignored.

</details>


### [76] [Mixing induced by microswimmers as probed by mutual information](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01547)
*Yihong Shi,Yuto Hosaka,Andrej Vilfan,Ramin Golestanian*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文利用互信息（mutual information）作为信息论度量标准，研究微游泳者（microswimmers）诱导的流体混合效率。通过对二维 squirmer 模型进行数值模拟，发现游泳者的空间分布显著影响混合效果，聚集抑制混合，位置和取向无序增强混合；在固定能量耗散下，混合效率随 squirmer 参数非单调变化，存在最优值；当考虑流体动力学相互作用时，推进型（pusher）优于牵引型（puller）；互信息随时间呈三阶段衰减；研究证实互信息可推广用于复杂流动中的混合效率度量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有混合效率度量方法在复杂流动系统中存在局限性，互信息此前仅在简化模型中得到验证。本文旨在将互信息这一信息论工具推广至微游泳者驱动的复杂流动，量化其混合效率并揭示关键影响因素。

Method: 采用二维方形域内的 squirmer 模型（squirmer model），通过数值计算游泳者产生的流动场，并求解示踪粒子（tracer particles）在流体中的平流-扩散方程（advection-diffusion equation），以互信息作为全局混合效率的信息论度量。

Result: 游泳者的空间分布强烈影响混合：聚集抑制混合，位置和取向无序增强混合；混合效率随 squirmer 参数呈非单调变化，存在最优值；包含流体动力学相互作用时 pusher 优于 puller；互信息随时间呈现三阶段衰减：初始扩散主导阶段、中间平流增强阶段、最终受系统尺寸控制的弛豫阶段。

Conclusion: 互信息作为混合效率的度量标准可有效应用于微游泳者产生的复杂流动；微游泳者的混合效率受强剪切流生成与全域最优分散之间的权衡（trade-off）所支配。

Abstract: We investigate fluid mixing induced by microswimmers using mutual information as a global, information-theoretic measure of mixing efficiency. For a two-dimensional squirmer model in a confined domain, we compute numerically the swimmer-generated flows and solve the advection-diffusion equation for the transport of tracer particles in the fluid. We show that the spatial distribution of swimmers strongly affects mixing, which is suppressed by swimmer aggregation and enhanced by positional and orientational disorder. At fixed energy dissipation, mixing efficiency depends non-monotonically on the squirmer parameter, with an optimal finite value arising from the balance between swimmer translation and dipolar flow generation. When hydrodynamic interactions are included, pushers outperform pullers. The mutual information as a function of time decays in three stages: an initial diffusion-dominated stage, an intermediate advection enhanced regime, and a final relaxation stage controlled by system size. Our results demonstrate that mutual information, previously validated as a measure of mixing efficiency only in simplified model systems, can equally be used in complex flows. Its application reveals that mixing by microswimmers is subject to a trade-off between the generation of strong shear flows and achieving optimal dispersion across the fluid domain.

</details>


### [77] [Tuning nonlinear waves in nonreciprocal active filaments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01603)
*Sami C. Al-Izzi,Jack Binysh,Yao Du,Corentin Coulais,Andreas Carlson*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文发展了一个非互易细丝（nonreciprocal filaments）的几何精确理论，结合仿真揭示了非互易性与惯性或预应力的耦合如何放大并输运曲率变化，从而产生单向形状变形的模式；这些模式可通过与环境的耗散相互作用进行选择。该工作提供了利用内应力驱动主动单向波（active unidirectional waves）的连续介质策略，无需额外的自由度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 细长结构的失稳现象广泛存在于生物运动和软体机器人驱动中。尽管非互易弹性固体（nonreciprocal elastic solids）已被发现可以单方向放大弯曲波，但如何调控和稳定这些波的设计原理仍然缺失。

Method: 发展了一个非互易细丝的几何精确理论（geometrically exact theory），并提供了能够捕捉失稳后非线性动力学（post-instability nonlinear dynamics）的仿真。

Result: 非互易性（nonreciprocity）在与惯性（inertia）或预应力（pre-stress）耦合时，会放大并输运曲率变化；由此产生的单向形状变形模式可通过与环境之间的耗散相互作用（dissipative interactions）进行选择。

Conclusion: 该工作提供了一种基于连续介质理论（continuum-based strategy）的策略，使得内应力能够驱动主动单向波，而无需增加额外的自由度。

Abstract: The instabilities of slender structures power biological locomotion across scales, and offer a compelling method to actuate soft robots. Nonreciprocal elastic solids have been found to amplify flexural waves in one direction only, but design principles to tune and stabilize these waves are missing. Here we develop a geometrically exact theory of nonreciprocal filaments and provide simulations that capture their post-instability nonlinear dynamics. We find that nonreciprocity, when coupled to inertia or pre-stress, amplifies and advects curvature variations. The resulting one-way patterns of shape morphing can then be selected via dissipative interactions with the environment. Our work offers a continuum-based strategy for how internal stresses can drive active unidirectional waves without need for additional degrees of freedom.

</details>


### [78] [Curvature-driven wall accumulation in chiral active particles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01948)
*Alessandro Petrini,Raphaël Maire,Umberto Marini Bettolo Marconi,Lorenzo Caprini*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 研究了一种由非自发运动的手性活性粒子（chiral active particles）组成的稀薄系统在直通道和圆形边界等几何约束下的行为。通过手性粒子-壁面相互作用（切向壁面力）引入活性，产生边缘流。发现边界曲率驱动壁面聚集现象——粒子在直通道中均匀分布，但在圆形边界附近聚集。数值模拟和流体力学理论一致捕获了这种曲率诱导的壁面聚集。结果表明边界曲率是手性边缘输运和约束诱导组织的基本控制参数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索非自发运动的手性活性粒子在受限几何结构中的边缘流行为，尤其是边界曲率对粒子密度分布的影响机制，从而揭示曲率作为手性边缘输运（chiral edge transport）和约束诱导组织（confinement-induced organization）控制参数的潜力。

Method: 采用数值模拟（numerical simulations）和基于密度与动量场的流体力学理论（hydrodynamic theory）相结合的方法。通过切向壁面力（tangential wall forces）引入手性粒子-壁面相互作用，模拟从直通道到圆形限制等多种几何约束下的粒子行为。

Result: 粒子在直通道（straight channels）中保持均匀分布；在圆形约束（circular confinements）中则出现显著的壁面聚集现象。数值模拟与流体力学理论的结果一致，均成功捕获了这种曲率诱导的壁面聚集（curvature-induced wall-accumulation）效应。

Conclusion: 边界曲率（boundary curvature）是控制手性边缘输运和约束诱导组织的关键参数。这一发现对旋转胶体（spinning colloids）和颗粒自旋体（granular spinners）等实验系统具有潜在的研究意义。

Abstract: We study a dilute system of non-motile chiral active particles confined in geometries ranging from straight channels to circular enclosures. Activity is introduced through chiral particle-wall interactions, modeled as tangential wall forces that generate the edge currents characteristic of chiral active matter. Remarkably, although the particles lack self-propulsion, these boundary currents induce density inhomogeneities. We show that boundary curvature drives a wall accumulation phenomenon: particles remain uniformly distributed in straight channels but accumulate near the boundaries of circular confinements. Numerical simulations and a hydrodynamic theory for the density and momentum fields consistently capture this curvature-induced wall-accumulation. These results identify boundary curvature as a fundamental control parameter for chiral edge transport and confinement-induced organization, with potential experimental relevance to spinning colloids and granular spinners.

</details>


### [79] [Pore-scale distribution and transport of active particles in a two-dimensional lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02143)
*Akhil Varma,David Saintillan*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 通过布朗动力学（Brownian Dynamics）模拟，研究活性粒子（active particles）在方形柱状晶格（模型多孔介质）中的分布与输运，揭示了无流和有流条件下粒子密度、极化场的变化规律以及拓扑缺陷（topological defects）的成核机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 微生物游动体（如细菌）和活性胶体在 porous environments（多孔环境）中常受到障碍物和复杂剪切流的影响，但对此类系统中活性粒子的分布与输运的微观物理机制尚缺乏系统理解。

Method: 将微游动体（microswimmers）建模为细长点粒子（slender point particles），采用布朗动力学（Brownian Dynamics）模拟，系统改变介质孔隙度（porosity）、多分散性（polydispersity）、流动强度（flow strength）和自推进强度（self-propulsion strength）进行参数化研究。

Result: 无流条件下自推进导致粒子在柱面聚集并形成径向极化（radial polarization）；有流条件下粒子优先聚集在支柱尾流（wake）区域，表面附近出现上游极化（upstream polarization）；中等流动强度下极化场中成核出纯运动学起源的拓扑缺陷（topological defects），标志着从全局上游游泳向高低速游泳区域共存的转变。

Conclusion: 该结构化晶格为分离复杂几何中活性输运（active transport）的物理机制提供了可控框架，对结构化微流控（microfluidic）环境中的输运研究具有直接参考价值。

Abstract: Suspensions of motile microswimmers such as bacteria and other active colloids frequently encounter porous environments where obstacles and complex shear flows strongly influence their dynamics. Here, we study the distribution and transport of a dilute suspension of active particles in a square lattice of pillars, which serves as a model porous medium. The microswimmers are modeled as slender point particles, and Brownian Dynamics simulations are performed to determine how their number density and polarization fields change with systematic variations in the medium porosity, polydispersity, flow strength, and self-propulsion strength. We find that in the absence of flow, self-propulsion drives particle accumulation and radial polarization at the pillar surfaces. In the presence of a background flow, particles preferentially accumulate in the wake of pillars and exhibit upstream polarization near their surface, consistent with experimental observations. At moderate flow strengths, topological defects nucleate in the polarization field. These defects are of purely kinematic origin and mark the transition from global upstream swimming at low flow strengths to the coexistence of upstream and downstream swimming regions in the lattice at high flow strengths. The structured lattice studied here provides a controlled framework for isolating the physical mechanisms governing active transport in complex geometries, with direct relevance to transport in structured microfluidic settings.

</details>


### [80] [From microscopic fluctuations to susceptibility spectra: single-molecule relaxation in glassy media](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02248)
*Siyang Wang,Jaladhar Mahato,Laura J. Kaufman*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过长时间追踪聚苯乙烯中荧光探针的单分子（single-molecule）转动动力学，在玻璃化转变温度（$T_g$）附近仅基于热涨落重构了损耗谱（loss spectrum），该谱再现了介电谱（dielectric spectroscopy）中常见的时间-温度叠加（time-temperature superposition）现象，并揭示了宏观系综谱源自单个分子对不同局部环境的响应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上，材料的损耗谱需要通过外场驱动（external field-driven）的频率域谱学（frequency-domain spectroscopy）如介电谱来测量；本文试图探究是否仅从纯热涨落（thermal fluctuations）的单分子转动动力学中即可重构出等同的损耗谱。

Method: 研究者对聚苯乙烯中荧光探针的单分子转动动力学进行了长时间追踪观测，利用单分子（SM）旋转涨落数据重构了损耗谱，而非使用传统的外加电场驱动方法。

Result: 重构得到的损耗谱再现了介电谱中常见的、在$T_g$附近材料出现的时间-温度叠加现象；此外，结果显示宏观系综谱（ensemble spectrum）实际上由每个分子对不同局部环境（distinct environments）的个体响应所组成。

Conclusion: 该方法证明了仅通过单分子热涨落即可重构出与传统频率域谱学等效的损耗谱，并为理解宏观粘弹性响应与微观分子级异质性（heterogeneity）之间的关联提供了直接实验证据。

Abstract: Single-molecule (SM) rotational dynamics of fluorescent probes in polystyrene near the glass transition temperature ($T_g$) are investigated over long times to reconstruct susceptibility spectra. The loss spectrum, commonly recorded using external field-driven (frequency-domain) spectroscopy, such as dielectric spectroscopy, is reconstructed from purely thermal SM rotational fluctuations. The results reproduce time-temperature superposition typically seen in dielectric spectroscopy for materials near $T_g$ and show that the ensemble spectrum is comprised of individual molecular responses to distinct environments.

</details>


### [81] [Hydrodynamics, Renormalization Group, and Universality Classes Far from Equilibrium](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02318)
*Patrick Jentsch,Chiu Fan Lee*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文系统综述了远离平衡态的多体系统中涌现的普适性（universality）现象，重点介绍了基于流体力学（hydrodynamics）和重整化群（renormalization group, RG）的理论框架，并梳理了自2015年以来发现的一系列无平衡对应物的非平衡普适类（universality classes, UCs）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 平衡临界现象的普适性分类已较为成熟，但远离平衡态的普适性理解仍不充分；近年来活性物质（active matter）等非平衡系统的快速发展揭示了许多新的无平衡对应物的普适类，亟需系统梳理和统一的理论介绍。

Method: 首先从对称性和守恒律出发系统构建流体力学理论；然后引入微扰动态重整化群（perturbative dynamic renormalization group）方法，并根据标度行为（scaling behaviour）将流体力学理论归入不同的普适类。

Result: 综述了自2015年以来发现的各种非平衡普适类，强调了它们之间在概念上的联系及其涌现背后统一的物理原理。

Conclusion: 指出了该领域面临的理论与实验开放挑战，包括尚未解决的非平衡普适性分类问题。

Abstract: Universality is one of the central organising principles of modern physics, explaining why systems with vastly different microscopic constituents can exhibit identical large-scale behaviour. While the classification of equilibrium critical phenomena through hydrodynamics and the renormalization group (RG) is now well established, our understanding of universality far from equilibrium remains far less developed. In recent years, however, rapid progress - driven in large part by developments in active and living matter - has uncovered a growing range of genuinely nonequilibrium universality classes (UCs) with no equilibrium counterparts. In this review, we present a pedagogical and unified introduction to hydrodynamic and RG approaches to nonequilibrium many-body systems. We first show how hydrodynamic theories can be systematically constructed from symmetry and conservation laws alone. We then introduce perturbative dynamic RG methods and demonstrate how hydrodynamic theories are organised into distinct UCs according to their scaling behaviour. Building on these foundations, we review the diverse nonequilibrium UCs uncovered since 2015, while emphasizing the conceptual connections and unifying physical principles underlying their emergence. We conclude by discussing open theoretical and experimental challenges for the field.

</details>


### [82] [Curvature-induced host-mediated polarization of active particles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02445)
*Giulia Janzen,D. A. Matoz-Fernandez*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文发现，非对齐的活性布朗粒子（active Brownian particles）嵌入致密被动介质并受限在紧凑曲面上时，可通过主动运动、被动应力重新分布与紧凑几何的耦合产生极性相干（polar coherence），无需粒子间的对齐相互作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 极性的集体运动通常源于对齐相互作用、粒子各向异性或外部方向偏置。本研究旨在探索是否存在不依赖对齐相互作用的、由环境介导的极性有序新路径。

Method: 将非对齐的活性布朗粒子嵌入致密被动介质，并限制在紧凑曲面（compact curved surface）上，通过数值模拟观察粒子的运动与应力分布，分析被动耗尽区域的形成及其对活性流（active flux）的反馈作用。

Result: 当应力传播长度（stress-spreading length）与球面半径相当时，被动耗尽区域合并为细长疤痕（elongated scars），引导活性运动并促进共同方向；移除被动介质后，即使活性粒子仍聚集在同一球面上，极性相干也会消失。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了一种环境介导的集体极性形成机制，其对称性破缺源于主动运动、被动应力重新分布与紧凑几何三者之间的耦合。

Abstract: Polar collective motion commonly arises from alignment interactions, particle anisotropy, or an imposed directional bias. Here we identify a distinct route to polar order that does not rely on alignment interactions between the active particles. We show that non-aligning active Brownian particles embedded in a dense passive medium can develop polar coherence when confined to a compact curved surface. Persistent active motion redistributes stress through the host and creates passive-depleted regions. When the stress-spreading length becomes comparable to the sphere radius, these regions merge into elongated scars that channel active motion and, through feedback with the active flux, promote a common direction of motion. Removing the passive host suppresses polar coherence even though the active particles continue to cluster on the same sphere. Our results establish an environment-mediated route to collective polarity in which symmetry breaking emerges from the coupling between active motion, passive stress redistribution, and compact geometry.

### [83] [Complex dynamics in the Sherrington-Kirkpatrick game](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02422)
*Desmond Chan,Tobias Galla*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文研究了大量玩家在两人两策略博弈中自适应学习（adaptive learning）的典型结果，为Sherrington-Kirkpatrick (SK)博弈提供了博弈论基础，并分析了随机偏置、玩家退出机制以及记忆衰减率与竞争性对学习稳定性的关键影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为最近由Garnier-Brun、Benzaquen和Bouchaud提出的Sherrington-Kirkpatrick (SK)博弈提供博弈论基础，并分析更一般情形下（含随机偏置、玩家可退出）的学习稳定性。

Method: 随机生成两人两策略博弈的收益矩阵（payoff matrices），在收益矩阵固定条件下研究大量玩家的自适应学习过程；引入带随机偏置的SK博弈及正则系综（grand-canonical）版本。

Result: 随机场（random fields）会影响稳定态的性质；在正则系综SK博弈中，学习稳定性由记忆衰减率和博弈竞争性共同决定，复杂情形下学习难以收敛，可能出现唯一不动点、多重不动点或持续波动。

Conclusion: 即使玩家仅面临二选一行动，大量玩家参与的复杂博弈情境也常常是不可学习的（unlearnable）；记忆衰减率与竞争性是决定学习收敛行为的关键参数。

Abstract: We study the outcome of adaptive learning of a large number of players engaging in sets of two-strategy two-player games. We are interested in typical games, and generate the payoff matrices at random at the beginning. The payoff matrices then remain fixed during the learning process. This provides a game theoretic foundation for the Sherrington-Kirkpatrick (SK) game, recently introduced by Garnier-Brun, Benzaquen and Bouchaud. The original model by these authors is a special case, with no bias towards any strategy. We here determine stability of learning for SK games with general random bias, and find that the nature of the stable state is affected by random fields. We also introduce a grand-canonical version of the SK game, in which players can choose to abstain. We determine the stability of learning for this game. Our analysis confirms that complex situations involving many players are frequently unlearnable, even if each player only chooses between two different actions. The rate with which players lose memory of past payoffs and the competitiveness of the game emerge as key parameters determining whether learning converges to a unique fixed point, whether there are many fixed points, or if the dynamics remains persistently volatile.

### [84] [Parent Hamiltonians of Ergodic Matrix Product States](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01446)
*Owen Ekblad,Eloy Moreno-Nadales,Eric B. Roon,Jeffrey H. Schenker*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了由随机张量定义的非平移不变的遍历矩阵乘积态（EMPS），证明其热力学极限是父哈密顿量唯一的无阻基态，并分析了该哈密顿量是否具有能隙的条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 矩阵乘积态（MPS）是无阻有能隙局域相互作用的基态典范，但其研究多集中于平移不变情形。本文旨在将父哈密顿量（parent Hamiltonian）理论推广到统计平移不变（statistically translation-invariant）的遍历MPS（EMPS）情形，并探究能隙（gap）存在的条件。

Method: 采用鞅方法（martingale method），同时追踪局部统计性质，分析EMPS父哈密顿量的能隙条件。对EMPS施加弱单射性假设（mild injectivity assumption），证明其热力学极限下的唯一无阻基态性质。

Result: EMPS的热力学极限是整条自旋链上父哈密顿量的唯一无阻基态，该哈密顿量可能为有限程（finite-range）也可能不是。与平移不变情形不同，该哈密顿量不一定有能隙。鞅方法结合局部统计给出了能隙存在的条件，也解释了为什么一般情形下不一定存在能隙。

Conclusion: 作者通过含能隙和不含能隙的EMPS示例，验证了理论结果的有效性与多样性。

Abstract: Matrix product states (MPS) are quintessential examples of frustration-free gapped ground states of local interactions called parent Hamiltonians. In this work, we investigate parent Hamiltonians for a class of ergodic matrix product states (EMPS), which are MPS defined by site-dependent random tensors $\{X_j^{[k]}\}_{j=1}^D$ which are homogeneously distributed at every site $k$ in the spin chain. Here, the EMPS are not translation-invariant but rather statistically translation-invariant. Under a mild injectivity assumption, we show the thermodynamic limit of an EMPS is the unique frustration-free ground state of a parent Hamiltonian on the whole spin chain, which, depending on the statistical properties of the EMPS, may or may not be finite-range. In contrast to the translation-invariant regime, these Hamiltonians need not be gapped. Nevertheless, applying the martingale method while keeping track of local statistics gives conditions for a gap, in addition to pointing towards why there need not be a gap in general. We include examples of EMPS both with and without spectral gaps to illustrate our results.

### [85] [Small Denominators and Subresonant Accumulation in Weakly Nonlinear Dispersive Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01447)
*P. Yu. Astafieva,O. M. Kiselev*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究弱非线性色散动力学中的小分母机制，提出“次共振累积”（subresonant accumulation）效应：当非共振傅里叶相互作用的失谐量趋于零时，其累积贡献可随时间的幂次增长。通过模型强迫振子和抽象次共振杜阿梅尔和（Duhamel sum）的严格分析，推导出累积增长指数 $α=(κ-1)/p$，并展示该机制在Klein–Gordon色散律的四次傅里叶族中的应用，给出全非线性偏微分方程的近似结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 弱非线性色散方程经傅里叶分解后成为无穷弱耦合振子系统，高阶修正项中存在无穷族非共振（nonresonant）傅里叶相互作用，其失谐量趋于零。这类家族虽不产生严格久期项（secular terms），但其累积效应可能随时间幂次增长，该机制尚未被系统分析。

Method: 首先建立模型强迫振子（model forced oscillator）与抽象次共振杜阿梅尔和（subresonant Duhamel sum）的严格分析框架；假设失谐量 $Δ_n\sim c n^{-p}$ 与系数 $B_n\sim b n^{-κ}$，推导累积贡献的渐近增长行为 $t^{1-α}$，其中 $α=(κ-1)/p$。随后将该机制应用于Klein–Gordon色散律的四次傅里叶族，并针对全非线性偏微分方程建立条件性近似结果。

Result: 严格分析表明，次共振累积效应的增长指数由参数 $α=(κ-1)/p$ 控制；该机制在Klein–Gordon色散律的四次傅里叶族中确实出现；在全非线性偏微分方程框架下，若所有剩余共振（resonant）与近共振（almost resonant）相互作用得到控制，则次共振项主导长期修正。

Conclusion: 次共振累积是弱非线性色散系统中的一个新机制，其累积贡献可达到与久期效应相当的时间增长量级。该结果为理解非共振高阶相互作用的长期行为提供了理论工具。

Abstract: We study a small-denominator mechanism in weakly nonlinear dispersive dynamics. After Fourier decomposition, a nonlinear dispersive equation becomes an infinite system of weakly coupled oscillators. Higher-order correction terms may then contain infinite families of nonresonant Fourier interactions whose detunings tend to zero. Such families do not produce exact secular terms, but their accumulated contribution may grow as a power of time. We call this effect subresonant accumulation. The rigorous part of the paper is the analysis of a model forced oscillator and of an abstract subresonant Duhamel sum. If the detuning and coefficients have the form $Δ_n\sim c n^{-p}$ and $B_n\sim b n^{-κ}$, then the accumulated contribution grows as $t^{1-α}$, where $α=(κ-1)/p$. We then show how this mechanism appears in a quartic Fourier family for the Klein--Gordon dispersion law. For the full nonlinear partial differential equation we formulate a conditional approximation result: provided that all remaining resonant and almost resonant interactions are controlled, the subresonant term gives the leading long-time correction.

Method: 引入 $r$-对数定义三参数的 $r$-deformed $\alpha$-$z$-Rényi 相对熵族；验证其满足散度的必要公理；通过分析参数 $\alpha$、$z$ 和 $r$ 的范围，确定数据处理不等式成立的条件；将新提出的量作为 Tsallis 相对熵的上界，并与文献中已有的上界进行序关系比较。

Result: $r$-deformed $\alpha$-$z$-Rényi 相对熵族的全体成员均满足散度公理；给出了使数据处理不等式成立的参数范围；证明了该新量是 Tsallis 相对熵的一个上界；在密度算子（density operator）的应用场景中，该新上界比文献中已有的上界更紧。

Conclusion: $r$-deformed $\alpha$-$z$-Rényi 相对熵作为 Tsallis 相对熵的一个更紧上界，在信息论和量子信息处理中具有潜在应用价值。

Abstract: In this article, we consider the $r$-logarithm for defining three-parameter family of Rényi relative entropies that are generalization of the $α$-$z$-Rényi relative entropies. All the members of $r$-deformed $α$-$z$-Rényi relative entropies satisfy the necessary axioms to be a divergence. We expose the range of parameters $α$, $z$ and $r$ for which the data processing inequality holds. We also establish that $r$-deformed $α$-$z$-Rényi relative entropy is an upper bound of the Tsallis relative entropy. Now, we have two upper bounds of the Tsallis relative entropy, which are $r$-deformed $α$-$z$-Rényi relative entropy and the other one, which is discussed in literature. We investigate the order relationship between these two upper bounds of the Tsallis relative entropy. We observe that our new upper bound is more tighter when applicable to the density operators.

### [87] [Open-boundary integrable quantum circuits with different geometries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02093)
*Miguel García Fernández,Chiara Paletta,Ana L. Retore*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文对具有开放边界条件和任意电路几何结构的可积杨-巴克斯特量子电路进行了完整分类，通过引入第三种非均匀性参数，证明了最小电路深度为四，并提供了检测杨-巴克斯特可积性的算法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 可积量子电路（integrable quantum circuits）在量子信息和统计物理中具有重要地位，但此前对于开放边界条件和任意几何结构下的可积性分类尚不完整。本文旨在建立一般性的映射框架，系统分类并构造满足杨-巴克斯特方程（Yang-Baxter equation）的可积量子电路。

Method: 基于标准转移矩阵构造（transfer-matrix construction），引入两种交错非均匀性（staggered inhomogeneities），推导出由非均匀性和系统大小决定电路门排列的一般映射。进一步引入第三种非均匀性参数ρ，并利用反射矩阵（reflection matrices）构造边界门。

Result: 证明了当局部体门与边界门满足杨-巴克斯特方程，且每个周期内每个最近邻自旋对恰好作用一次相同体门时，时间周期量子电路是可积的。证明了最小电路深度为四。当ρ非均匀性置于端点及其紧邻区域时，边界门可解释为作用在多格点上的单门。

Conclusion: 该构造完全一般，适用于正则R矩阵（regular R-matrices），包括差分型与非差分型，及其关联的边界矩阵。以6-顶点和8-顶点R矩阵对应的两量子比特门为例，构造了生成可积量子电路的反射矩阵。

Abstract: We present a complete classification of integrable Yang-Baxter quantum circuits with open boundary conditions and arbitrary circuit geometries. Starting from the standard transfer-matrix construction with two types of staggered inhomogeneities, we derive a general mapping that determines the arrangement of circuit gates in terms of the inhomogeneities and the system size. We conjecture that time-periodic quantum circuits are integrable whenever the local bulk and boundary gates satisfy the Yang-Baxter equation and the same bulk gate is applied exactly once per period to every nearest-neighbor pair of spins. Our construction also provides an algorithm to detect Yang-Baxter integrability for circuits with arbitrary geometries. Furthermore, we introduce a third type of inhomogeneity, denoted by $ρ$, and demonstrate that the minimum possible circuit depth is four. We show that when these $ρ$-inhomogeneities are placed at the endpoints and in their immediate neighborhood, the resulting boundary gates can be interpreted as single gates acting on multiple sites. Our construction is fully general and applies to regular $R$-matrices, both of difference and non-difference type, together with their associated boundary matrices. As an application, we consider two-qubit gates corresponding to 6- and 8-vertex $R$-matrices of non-difference form satisfying the Yang-Baxter equation, and we construct the associated reflection matrices that generate integrable quantum circuits.

*Yoshitsugu Sekine*

Abstract: This paper studies the imperfect Bose gas after the Kac density law and the mean-field Euler equations have selected a condensed density with positive zero-mode excess. In this BEC regime the selected chemical potential cancels the mean-field shift, so the selected one-particle Hamiltonian is exactly the free one. The resulting zero-mode covariance defines a mean-field BEC ideal in the resolvent algebra, while the nonregular quotient and the direct-integral center record distinct representation-theoretic data. Occupation-number and Brownian-loop formulations recover the same density selection, excess density, ODLRO data, local tests, and the separation between finite-density BEC and Buchholz's stricter infinite-occupation proper-condensate criterion.

### [89] [Mesoscopic Linear Statistics for Two Ensembles of Quantum Graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02356)
*Anna Maltsev,Mohammed Osman*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在理解随机量子图（random quantum graph）在中观尺度上的谱统计行为，并探讨其与经典随机矩阵系综（random matrix ensemble）之间的关系。

Method: 定义了两种随机量子图系综：第一种通过从所有$d$-正则图（$d$-regular graph）中均匀采样离散底图得到；第二种通过对每个顶点的酉矩阵（unitary matrix）$U^{(v)}$独立地从Haar测度（Haar measure）均匀采样得到。然后分析了其线性谱统计量（linear spectral statistic）在大图极限（large graph limit）下的方差。

Result: 证明了在多项式中观尺度（polynomial mesoscopic scale）上，两种随机量子图系综的线性谱统计量的方差与高斯正交系综（GOE）或高斯幺正系综（GUE）的方差相同。

Conclusion: 随机量子图在中观尺度上的谱波动行为与经典随机矩阵理论中的GOE/GUE一致，表明该系综在此尺度下具有普适性（universality）。

Abstract: We study mesoscopic linear spectral statistics for two ensembles of random quantum graphs. These are defined by a discrete graph $G$ and a unitary-matrix-valued function $U(k)$ indexed by directed edges of $G$. The matrix function $U(k)$ is constructed from unitary matrices $U^{(v)}$ indexed by the neighbours of each vertex $v$. The first ensemble is obtained by sampling the underlying discrete graph uniformly from the set of $d$-regular graphs. The second ensemble is obtained by sampling $U^{(v)}$ uniformly from the Haar measure, independently for each vertex. We prove that the variance of a linear spectral statistic in the large graph limit on polynomial mesoscopic scales coincides with that of the Gaussian Orthogonal/Unitary Ensemble.

</details>


### [90] [On a Rosenzweig-Porter-type model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02446)
*Giorgio Cipolloni,László Erdős,Joscha Henheik*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了一类非常广泛的Rosenzweig-Porter-type模型，精确刻画了特征向量局域化性质与本征态热化假说（ETH）随耦合常数λ的变化过程，证明结果对H₀和λ一致成立，显著推广了以往变形Wigner矩阵的局部律，并揭示了迁移率边（mobility edge）的出现和再入局域化（re-entrant localization）现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有关于变形Wigner矩阵（deformed Wigner matrices）的局部律（local laws）在一般性和一致性上仍有局限，尤其是在非平均场区域和任意厄米矩阵H₀作为基准的情形下缺乏统一刻画。作者希望填补这一空白，为Rosenzweig-Porter-type模型提供普适的理论框架。

Method: 采用解析方法，精确追踪特征向量局域化性质与本征态热化假说（eigenstate thermalisation hypothesis, ETH）随耦合常数λ的变化；通过精确刻画具有强非均匀结构（strongly inhomogeneous structure）的预解式（resolvent）的确定性近似（deterministic approximation）来证明主要结论。

Result: 结果对任意厄米矩阵H₀和耦合常数λ一致成立，显著推广了所有以往关于变形Wigner矩阵的局部律，即使在平均场（mean field）区域也不例外。此外，还揭示了迁移率边（mobility edge）的出现以及再入局域化（re-entrant localization）现象。

Conclusion: 本文建立的统一框架不仅深化了对Rosenzweig-Porter-type模型局域化-热化过渡的理解，也为更一般的无序系统中迁移率边与再入局域化的研究提供了理论工具。

Abstract: We consider a very general Rosenzweig-Porter-type model, $H=H_0+λW$, where $H_0$ is an arbitrary Hermitian matrix and $W$ is a standard Wigner matrix. We precisely trace the localization properties of the eigenvectors and the eigenstate thermalisation hypothesis (ETH) as the coupling constant $λ$ interpolates between the trivial $λ=0$ case and the fully mean field regime of large $λ$. Our results hold uniformly in $H_0$ and $λ$, substantially generalising all previous local laws on deformed Wigner matrices even in the mean field regime. Our proof precisely captures the deterministic approximation to the resolvent which exhibits a strongly inhomogeneous structure. As a byproduct, we conclude the emergence of a mobility edge and study the phenomenon of re-entrant localization.

</details>

### [91] [Fractional-Dimension Gravity and the Milky Way Galaxy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01412)
*Gabriele U. Varieschi*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文利用盖亚DR3数据与旋转曲线数据，以分数维引力（FDG）分析银河系，成功通过变分数维函数复现观测旋转曲线，并探讨了分数维时空中可能存在的有效超光速运动及其对星际旅行的启示。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在将分数维引力（Fractional-Dimension Gravity, FDG）这一无需暗物质（dark matter）范式的替代引力模型应用于银河系（Milky Way, MW），利用最新的Gaia DR3数据与先前的旋转曲线（rotation curve, RC）数据检验其适用性。

Method: 采用变分数维函数$D(R)$，沿用先前分析其他星系的同一方法论，对银河系旋转曲线进行拟合；同时，基于质量-维数场方程（mass-dimension field equation）引入另一种维数函数$D_m(R)$进行对比分析。此外，论文还从分数维时空的FDG度规（metric）出发，探讨了额外权重（additional weights）对狭义相对论（Special Relativity, SR）结构的影响。

Result: FDG方法成功复现了银河系观测旋转曲线，其中变分数维函数$D(R)$的拟合效果优于基于质量-维数场方程的$D_m(R)$。此外，在空间维度$D<3$的星系区域中，可能存在有效超光速运动（effective superluminal motion）。

Conclusion: FDG能够在无需暗物质假设的前提下有效描述银河系的旋转曲线；尽管超光速运动的推论尚属推测性（speculative），但它为银河系内可能的星际旅行（interstellar travel）开辟了新的理论视角。

Abstract: In this work, we focus our analysis of Fractional-Dimension Gravity (FDG) on our home galaxy, the Milky Way (MW), by using the latest Gaia DR3 data as well as previous rotation curve (RC) data for this galaxy. FDG is an alternative gravitational model (previously known as Newtonian Fractional-Dimension Gravity - NFDG) which does not require the dark matter (DM) paradigm.
  The MW is studied here with the methods of FDG and its observed rotation curves are successfully reproduced by using a variable fractional dimension $D\left (R\right)$, following previous studies of several other galaxies which were analyzed with the same methodology. An alternative dimension function $D_{m}\left(R \right)$, based on the mass-dimension field equation, was also used and yielded less accurate fits to the experimental data.
  In addition, we also considered possible implications of the FDG metric, based on the presence of additional weights, on the structure of Special Relativity (SR) for spacetimes with fractional dimension. One notable outcome of this analysis is the possibility of an effective superluminal motion in galactic regions where the space dimension is $D<3$. Although this result is very speculative, it opens interesting new perspectives for possible interstellar travel in our galaxy.

</details>

### [92] [Learning Lax Pairs: Revisiting the Classical Paradigm](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01493)
*Jimmie Adriazola,Gino Biondini,Wei Zhu,Panayotis G. Kevrekidis*

Main category: nlin.SI

TL;DR: 本文通过五个案例（欧拉陀螺、自由薛定谔方程、无粘伯格斯方程、浅水波系统、KdV方程）展示了Lax对与可积性之间的关系远比传统认知复杂：相容性条件并不能唯一确定Lax表示，异常Lax对（anomalous Lax pair）是可积系统景观中的常见现象，将Lax对简单区分为"真"与"假"的二分法过于简化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管Lax对（Lax pair）$(L,P)$通常被视为可积系统的结构证书——空间算子$L$携带谱数据，其等谱演化$\partial_t L = [L,P]$编码非线性动力学——但实际经验表明，方程与Lax对之间的对应关系远比该图景所暗示的更为微妙；一些方程存在无法编码预期可积结构的Lax对，这一异常角落（anomalous corner）尚未得到充分理解。

Method: 采用分析计算与稀疏识别Lax算子（Sparse Identification of Lax Operators, SILO）框架相结合的方法，对五个案例进行系统研究，在部分案例中确认了教科书上的标准Lax对，在另一些案例中发现了值得独立理解的替代性Lax对。

Result: 五个案例（欧拉陀螺、自由薛定谔方程、无粘伯格斯方程、浅水波系统、KdV方程）各自展示了可积性链接被扭曲的不同方式；特别地，一个被标准判据归类为虚假（fake）的谱简并KdV Lax对，仍然通过其算子代数生成了完整的守恒量层级（conservation hierarchy）。

Conclusion: 相容性（compatibility）条件并不足以唯一确定Lax表示，异常Lax对是可积系统景观中的规则特征而非病态现象；"真"与"假"Lax对之间的简单二分法过于简化，需要更细致的分类框架。

Abstract: A Lax pair $(L,P)$ is sometimes thought of as a structural certificate, in that the spatial operator $L$ carries the spectral data of an integrable system, and its isospectral evolution under $\partial_t L = [L,P]$ encodes the nonlinear dynamics. Yet, experience shows that the correspondence between equations and Lax pairs is much more nuanced than this picture suggests. Equations can admit Lax pairs that fail to encode the expected integrable structure. This paper probes that anomalous corner of the Lax pair landscape through five case studies (the Euler top, the free Schrödinger equation, the inviscid Burgers equation, the shallow water system, and the Korteweg--de Vries equation), each illustrating a different way the link to integrability can be distorted. The approach combines analytical calculations with the Sparse Identification of Lax Operators (SILO) framework, which proved useful throughout, in some cases confirming the textbook pair and in others surfacing alternatives worth understanding on their own terms. The recurring lesson across the five cases is that compatibility underdetermines the Lax representation, so that anomalous pairs are regular features of the landscape rather than pathologies. Notably, we show that a spectrally degenerate Korteweg--de Vries Lax pair, classified as fake by standard criteria, still generates the full conservation hierarchy through its operator algebra, which shows that a blunt dichotomy between true and fake Lax pairs can be too reductive.

</details>

### [93] [Existence of weak solutions of the surface Beris-Edwards model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01638)

TL;DR: 本文证明了定义在d维（d=2,3）闭超曲面上的表面Beris-Edwards模型弱解的存在性，该模型耦合了不可压缩切向Navier-Stokes方程与Q-张量场的运动学方程，通过基于切向Stokes算子和张量Laplace-Beltrami算子特征函数的Faedo-Galerkin格式及紧性论证得到弱解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为表面Beris-Edwards模型（由Bouck、Nochetto和Yushutin于2024年提出的热力学一致模型）建立弱解存在性的严格数学理论基础，将其从平坦区域推广到曲面情形。

Method: 设计一种Faedo-Galerkin格式（Faedo-Galerkin scheme），基于适当的切向Stokes算子（tangent Stokes operator）和张量Laplace-Beltrami算子（tensor-valued Laplace-Beltrami operator）的特征函数，并结合标准的紧性论证（compactness arguments）恢复弱解。

Result: 在C^{2,1}类的d维闭超曲面（d∈{2,3}）上，证明了表面Beris-Edwards模型弱解的存在性。

Conclusion: 该工作将Abels、Dolzmann和Liu（2014）以及Guillén-González和Rodríguez-Bellido（2015）在平坦区域上针对Beris-Edwards模型的思想推广到了曲面情形。

Abstract: We prove the existence of weak solutions to the surface Beris-Edwards model for nematic liquid crystals posed on a $d$-dimensional ($d \in \{2,3\}$) closed hypersurface of class $C^{2,1}$. This thermodynamically consistent model, recently introduced by Bouck, Nochetto and Yushutin (2024), couples the incompressible tangent Navier-Stokes equations with a kinematic equation for the Q-tensor field that encodes the orientation of the liquid crystal particles with a general state of orientational order. Extending ideas by Abels, Dolzmann and Liu (2014) and Guillén-González and Rodríguez-Bellido (2015) for the Beris-Edwards model in flat domains, we design a Faedo-Galerkin scheme based upon eigenfunctions of an appropriate tangent Stokes operator and tensor-valued Laplace-Beltrami operator and recover a weak solution via standard compactness arguments.

### [94] [A Local Linking Theorem for Relativistic Action Functionals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01845)
*Manuel Garzón,Salvador López-Martínez*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文为源自相对论作用量原理的Szulkin型泛函建立了Brezis-Nirenberg局部链接定理的类比，通过引入有效域诱导的拓扑来表述Palais-Smale紧性，并应用该抽象结果证明了洛伦兹力方程和Minkowski空间中预定平均曲率Dirichlet问题至少存在两个非常数解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将经典的Brezis-Nirenberg局部链接定理（local linking theorem）推广到由相对论作用量原理（relativistic action principles）导出的Szulkin型泛函（Szulkin-type functionals）框架中，以处理这类泛函所特有的非平凡结构。

Method: 证明方法结合了基于负梯度流（negative gradient flow）的极小极大几何（min-max geometry）原始构造与Ekeland-Lasry正则化（Ekeland-Lasry regularization）。核心创新在于提出了一种新的扰动构造（perturbative construction），以克服正则化泛函与原始泛函分别关联不同拓扑（强拓扑 vs. 有效域诱导拓扑）所导致的紧性不匹配问题。

Result: 在有效域诱导拓扑下建立了Palais-Smale序列的紧性条件，并成功证明了抽象的抽象多解性结论。将该结果应用于洛伦兹力方程（Lorentz force equation）和Minkowski空间中预定平均曲率算子的Dirichlet问题（Dirichlet problem for prescribed mean curvature operator），证明在自然假设下每个问题至少存在两个非常数解（non-constant solutions）。

Conclusion: 本文为Szulkin型泛函提供了局部链接理论的广义框架，有效处理了相对论模型中泛函有效域（effective domain）与函数空间强拓扑之间的冲突，并为两类重要的相对论模型给出了多解性存在性的严格证明。

Abstract: We establish an analogue of the Brezis-Nirenberg local linking theorem for a class of Szulkin-type functionals arising from relativistic action principles. In this framework, compactness of Palais-Smale sequences is formulated with respect to a topology induced by the effective domain of the functional, replacing the classical strong Palais-Smale condition. The proof combines the original construction of the min-max geometry, based on a negative gradient flow, with the Ekeland-Lasry regularization. The main difficulty is that the regularized functional is naturally associated with the strong topology of the underlying functional space, whereas compactness for the original functional is formulated in the topology induced by the effective domain. We overcome this obstacle through a new perturbative construction that recovers the required min-max structure. We apply our abstract multiplicity result to two representative relativistic models: the Lorentz force equation, describing the dynamics of a charged particle in an electromagnetic field, and the Dirichlet problem for the prescribed mean curvature operator in Minkowski space. As a consequence, under natural assumptions, each problem admits at least two non-constant solutions.

### [95] [Electron stability constrains neutrino time delays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01339)
*Mauricio Bustamante,José Manuel Carmona,José Luis Cortés,Ardit Gkioni,Maykoll A. Reyes*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文指出，用于解释高能中微子时间延迟的洛伦兹不变性破缺（LIV）理论，在同时考虑真空对发射和电子衰变通道后，会与TeV-PeV能量范围电子观测稳定性相矛盾，从而排除了通过LIV解释中微子时间延迟的可能性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究中，通过洛伦兹不变性破缺（Lorentz-invariance violation, LIV）解释高能宇宙中微子与伽马射线之间时间延迟的尝试，通常假设亚光速（subluminal）中微子传播以避免超光速情形下真空对发射（vacuum pair emission）导致的能量快速耗散。然而，这一图像忽略了亚光速中微子对应的LIV修正同样会开启电子衰变通道（$e^- \to e^- + ν+ \barν$），从而与观测到的电子稳定性（electron stability）相矛盾。

Method: 从洛伦兹不变性破缺（LIV）的色散关系修正出发，同时分析超光速（superluminal）和亚光速（subluminal）中微子传播所对应的互补的粒子衰变与产生过程；利用近期TeV-PeV能区天体物理电子的观测数据，推导电子稳定性对LIV参数的约束。

Result: 电子稳定性（electron stability）的限制排除了通过LIV解释高能宇宙中微子时间延迟（neutrino time delays）的理论方案；无论是超光速还是亚光速侧，中微子时间延迟均受到约束。

Conclusion: 可观测的中微子时间延迟若要存在，需要纯天体物理起源、一种对所有粒子种类产生相同影响的LIV实现方式，或者超越标准有效场论（effective field theory, EFT）框架的新物理。

Abstract: Superluminal neutrino propagation, induced by Lorentz-invariance violation (LIV), is strongly constrained by vacuum pair emission, $ν\to ν+ e^- + e^+$, a process ordinarily forbidden, which rapidly degrades the energy of high-energy neutrinos. Consequently, observable neutrino time delays are often preferentially associated with subluminal propagation, prompting LIV interpretations of claimed time delays between high-energy cosmic neutrinos and gamma rays. However, this expectation is at odds with the observed stability of high-energy electrons. The same Lorentz-violating correction associated with subluminal neutrino propagation opens the overlooked complementary decay channel $e^- \to e^- + ν+ \barν$, leading to electron instability. We derive constraints on LIV from recent observations of TeV--PeV astrophysical electrons. These electron stability limits rule out LIV invoked to explain delays of high-energy cosmic neutrinos. Consequently, neutrino time delays are constrained on both the superluminal and subluminal sides. Therefore, observable delays require either purely astrophysical origins, a realization of LIV that affects all particle species equally, or physics beyond the standard effective-field-theory framework.

</details>


### [96] [Subensemble Acceptance Method 3.0: General Corrections to Cumulants from Exact Conservation Constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01783)
*Roman Poberezhnyuk,Volodymyr A. Kuznietsov,Grégoire Pihan,Volodymyr Vovchenko*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了子系接受方法3.0（SAM-3.0），通过多元偏指数贝尔多项式（multivariate partial exponential Bell polynomials）的封闭递归，修正多重电荷全局严格守恒对子系统可观测量累积量（cumulants）的影响。该方法统一了SAM-1.0和SAM-2.0，适用于任意数量可观测量的微观正则系综（microcanonical ensemble），并推导了有限尺寸修正。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法（如SAM-2.0）在处理多重电荷全局守恒对子系统累积量修正时存在局限（例如无法精确再现二项式接受极限）。需要发展一种普适框架，能够同时处理任意数量的守恒荷和可观测量，并适用于从正则系综到微观正则系综的完整映射。

Method: 以联合巨正则累积量（joint grand-canonical cumulants）为输入，借助（多元）偏指数贝尔多项式建立封闭递归，代数地导出正则累积量。通过鞍点展开（saddle-point expansion）推导主导有限尺寸修正。该方法将SAM-1.0和SAM-2.0作为特例纳入，并能精确再现二项式接受极限。

Result: 将方法应用于RHIC-BES能区净质子累积量的基于流体的非临界基准（Hydro-EV），获得精炼的基准线，与直接正则蒙特卡罗采样（canonical Monte Carlo sampling）一致，且接近SAM-2.0结果。进一步在重子数、电荷、奇异数严格同时守恒条件下，结合强子后燃器效应（hadronic-afterburner effects），验证了形式体系与直接蒙特卡罗采样的吻合。

Conclusion: SAM-3.0为多重守恒荷约束下的子系统累积量计算提供了统一且精确的解析框架，优于SAM-2.0并推广至微观正则系综，适用于重离子碰撞中非临界基准线的理论更新。

Abstract: We present the subensemble acceptance method 3.0 (SAM-3.0), which corrects cumulants of an observable measured in a subsystem of a large system for the effect of exact global conservation of multiple charges. The required input is the set of joint grand-canonical cumulants of the acceptance observable with the total event charges, from which the canonical cumulants follow algebraically via a closed recursion based on (multivariate) partial exponential Bell polynomials. The framework accommodates any number of observables, including non-conserved quantities such as net protons, and any number of simultaneously conserved charges, including the total energy, which yields the microcanonical ensemble. The mapping contains SAM-1.0 and SAM-2.0 as special cases and, unlike SAM-2.0, reproduces the exact binomial-acceptance limit. We also derive the leading finite-size corrections from the saddle-point expansion. We apply the method to update the hydrodynamics-based non-critical baseline (Hydro-EV) for net-proton cumulants at RHIC-BES energies, finding a refined baseline that agrees with direct canonical Monte Carlo sampling and stays close to the earlier SAM-2.0 result. We further validate the formalism against direct Monte Carlo sampling with exact simultaneous conservation of baryon number, electric charge, and strangeness, including hadronic-afterburner effects.

</details>


### [97] [A Comprehensive Analysis of $B_s \to D_s^{**}\ellν_\ell$ Decays Within and Beyond the Standard Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02276)
*Karthik Jain,Tarun Kumar,Barilang Mawlong,Shantanu Sahoo*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文在标准模型（Standard Model）及其新物理（New Physics）框架下，利用重夸克有效理论（Heavy Quark Effective Theory, HQET）中的形状因子（form factors），研究了 $B_s \to D_s^{**} \ell 
u_\ell$ 四类粲介子的半轻衰变；通过数据驱动方法提取 HQET 参数并采用 $z$-展开（$z$-expansion）参数化形状因子，精确预言了轻子普适性比率（lepton flavor universality ratios），并系统分析了弱有效理论（Weak Effective Theory, WET）、标准模型有效场论（Standard Model Effective Field Theory, SMEFT）及一般双希格斯二重态模型（Two Higgs Doublet Model, 2HDM）中实、复 Wilson 系数的新物理贡献，发现标量和张量算符可导致显著偏离标准模型预言。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 精确预判 $B_s \to D_s^{**}$ 半轻衰变中的轻子普适性比率及其他可观测量，并检验其对新物理的敏感性，为未来实验探测标准模型偏离提供理论依据。

Method: 基于重夸克有效理论（HQET）计算包含 $\mathcal{O}(α_s, Λ/{m_Q})$ 修正的形状因子；采用数据驱动方法提取 HQET 参数，并通过 $z$-展开在全运动学区域参数化形状因子；利用弱有效理论（WET）、标准模型有效场论（SMEFT）及一般双希格斯二重态模型（2HDM）进行全局分析，同时考虑实数和复数Wilson系数（Wilson coefficients）。

Result: 精确预言了四个衰变道的轻子普适性比率：$R_{D_{s0}^*}= 0.158(20)$, $R_{D_{s1}^*}= 0.045(5)$, $R_{D_{s1}}= 0.073(4)$, $R_{D_{s2}^*} = 0.066(9)$；发现标量（scalar）和张量（tensor）新物理算符具有高敏感性，部分可观测量与标准模型预言偏差超过 $2σ$。

Conclusion: $B_s \to D_s^{**} \ell 
u_\ell$ 衰变是检验轻子普适性及探测标量、张量类新物理的有效探针；未来实验可通过这些可观测量检验标准模型并约束新物理参数空间。

Abstract: We examine the exclusive semileptonic decays $B_s \to D_s^{**} \ell ν_\ell$, with $D_s^{**} =$ $\bigl\{D_{s0}^*,D_{s1}^*,D_{s1},D_{s2}^*\bigr\}$, within the Standard Model and beyond, using form factors evaluated in the Heavy Quark Effective Theory, including corrections up to $\mathcal{O}(α_s, Λ/{m_Q})$. A data-driven approach is employed to extract Heavy Quark Effective Theory parameters, and the resulting synthetic data are used to parameterize the form factors via the $z$-expansion. With the resulting form factor information across the full kinematic region, we compute various observables derived from the two-fold angular decay distribution, and predict precise lepton flavor universality ratios: $R_{D_{s0}^*}= 0.158(20)$, $R_{D_{s1}^*}= 0.045(5)$, $R_{D_{s1}}= 0.073(4)$, $R_{D_{s2}^*} = 0.066(9)$. We also analyse potential new physics effects using the Weak Effective Theory and the Standard Model Effective Field Theory, performing a global analysis considering both real and complex Wilson coefficients. Furthermore, we investigate new physics contributions arising from the general Two Higgs Doublet Model. We evaluate the sensitivity of decay observables to new physics, highlighting their potential to probe deviations from the Standard Model in future measurements. Notably, the scalar and tensor new physics operators induce large sensitivity, with some observables deviating by more than $2 σ$ from Standard Model predictions.

</details>


### [98] [New constraints on non-unitary neutrino mixing from 8 years of IceCube DeepCore atmospheric neutrino data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02355)
*Sharmistha Chattopadhyay,Anil Kumar,Sanjib Kumar Agarwalla*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 基于 IceCube DeepCore 8 年大气中微子数据，对非幺正中微子混合（non-unitary neutrino mixing）进行了探测，未发现与标准幺正混合框架的显著偏离，并在 $α_{33}$ 参数上给出了目前最严格的限制（$α_{33} > -0.027$, 90% CL）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 活性中微子（active neutrinos）的味本征态与质量本征态之间的混合通常由 $3\times3$ 幺正矩阵描述，但额外重惰性中微子（sterile neutrino）的存在可能导致非幺正混合。大气中微子因其基线（baseline）和能量范围宽广，是探测此类效应的理想探针，尤其在地球物质效应（matter effect）中，非幺正性会使中性流势（neutral-current potential）产生非平凡贡献。

Method: 采用 IceCube DeepCore 探测器 8 年公开的大气中微子数据，使用高纯度 $ν_μ$ 带电流（charged-current, CC）样本，该样本对 $ν_μ\rightarrow ν_μ$ 通道中主导阶（leading order）的非幺正参数（non-unitary parameters）具有较强灵敏度，通过分析数据检验非幺正混合场景。

Result: 数据样本与标准幺正混合框架（standard unitary mixing framework）一致，未发现显著偏离。在该数据样本下，对非幺正参数 $α_{33}$ 给出了当前最严格的限制：$α_{33} > -0.027$（90% 置信水平），其余非幺正参数也获得了具有竞争力的约束水平。

Conclusion: IceCube DeepCore 的大气中微子数据目前支持标准幺正混合图像，未探测到非幺正混合的显著迹象；同时，研究给出了迄今最强和具有竞争力的非幺正参数约束，为未来中微子混合的精确检验提供了重要参考。

Abstract: The mixing between flavor and mass eigenstates of active neutrinos is described by a $3\times3$ unitary matrix. However, the presence of additional heavy sterile neutrino states can lead to a non-unitary neutrino mixing scenario. Atmospheric neutrinos, with their wide range of baselines and energies, provide an excellent probe of such effects. In particular, Earth matter effects in neutrino oscillations play an important role, as the neutral-current potential contributes non-trivially in the presence of non-unitarity. In this work, we use 8 years of publicly available atmospheric neutrino data of IceCube DeepCore to probe this non-unitary neutrino mixing scenario. This high-purity $ν_μ$ CC sample provides strong sensitivity, especially to the non-unitary parameters appearing at leading order in the $ν_μ\rightarrow ν_μ$ channel. The data sample is found to be consistent with the standard unitary mixing framework with no significant deviation. Using this data sample, we place the most stringent bound to date of $α_{33} > -0.027$ at 90% CL, while the other non-unitary parameters are constrained at competitive levels.

</details>


### [99] [Event-axis TMD measurements in $e^+e^-$ and SIDIS](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02438)
*Daniel Diaz Fernandez,Patricia Andrea Gutierrez Garcia,Ignazio Scimemi,Wouter Waalewijn*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文建立并完善了基于推力轴（thrust axis）测量e⁺e⁻碰撞中横动量依赖（TMD）碎裂函数的因子化框架，完成了软因子的算符级表述与单圈验证，并扩展至半单举深度非弹性散射（SIDIS）中的1-jettiness因子化。通过提出包含事件形貌依赖与横向动量关联的非微扰模型，在artemide中实现了对数重求和，并在Pythia8.3模拟数据上进行了验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统背靠背强子对测量需要解耦两个TMD碎裂函数，而基于推力轴的测量提供了一种互补途径，避免这一困难。同时，SIDIS中类似的可观测量可用于提取TMD部分子分布函数（PDF），但现有因子化框架尚不完整，需要进一步扩展。

Method: 利用已建立的因子化定理，完成软因子（soft ingredient）的算符级表述，并采用δ-正规化（δ-regulator）进行单圈检验。将结果扩展至SIDIS中的1-jettiness因子化。提出一种非微扰模型，同时描述事件形貌（event-shape）依赖及其与横向动量测量的关联。在artemide软件中实现横动量与推力的对数重求和（resummation），并探索多种处理方案。

Result: 在Pythia8.3模拟e⁺e⁻数据上的验证表明，所提出的非微扰模型能够灵活地描述模拟数据，拟合参数的量级符合Λ_QCD/Q的幂次预期。测试中发现，q_T/(τQ)对数的重求和（resummation）对拟合质量影响很小，但改变了拟合参数值。

Conclusion: 基于推力轴的TMD碎裂函数测量框架在算符层面得到完善，且非微扰模型在模拟数据中表现良好。该工作为未来从e⁺e⁻实验（如Belle）中提取TMD碎裂函数、并从SIDIS实验中提取TMD部分子分布函数提供了理论工具和数值实现基础。

Abstract: Transverse-momentum-dependent (TMD) fragmentation in $e^+e^-$ collisions can be studied by measuring hadrons with respect to the thrust axis, and has been measured at Belle. This provides a complementary way to extract TMD fragmentation functions, avoiding the need to disentangle the two TMD fragmentation functions that enter conventional back-to-back hadron-pair measurements. Starting from the established factorization theorems for this observable, we complete the operator-level formulation of the soft ingredients and perform one-loop checks using the $δ$-regulator. We also extend existing results for 1-jettiness factorization in semi-inclusive deep-inelastic scattering (SIDIS), where analogous measurements give access to the TMD parton distribution functions of the incoming hadron. For phenomenology, we discuss the nonperturbative effects and propose a model that captures both the event-shape dependence and correlations between the event-shape and transverse-momentum measurements. We resum the transverse-momentum and thrust logarithms, explore several schemes for treating the latter, and implement it in artemide. As a first validation, we compare to simulated $e^+e^-$ data from Pythia8.3. We find that the proposed nonperturbative model is flexible enough to describe the simulated data, with fitted parameters of the expected size in powers of $Λ_{\rm QCD}/Q$. In this test, the resummation of the logarithms of $q_T/(τQ)$ appears to have little impact on the fit quality, but changes the fit parameters.

</details>


### [100] [Can Primordial Black Holes Be Seeds for Early Galaxies in Models Satisfying the Covariant Entropy Bound?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01292)
*Sidan A,Tom Banks,Willy Fischler*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文论证了满足协变熵界（Covariant Entropy Bound, CEB）的宇宙学模型在数学上倾向于无局域激发或仅含一个包含所有能量的大黑洞的初始状态。为获得长辐射主导期，需假设早期宇宙的大部分视界体积（horizon volumes）中包含衰变为辐射的微小黑洞。通过进一步引入当时至少达到视界尺度的随机原初黑洞（primordial black holes），该模型可同时解释暗物质（dark matter）和詹姆斯·韦伯空间望远镜（JWST）观测到的早期星系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 作者从协变熵界（CEB）出发，论证宇宙学初始态倾向于无局域激发或单一黑洞态。为获得长辐射主导期，引入早期微小黑洞衰变机制；为解释暗物质，进一步引入视界尺度（horizon-sized）原初黑洞分布。模型分别用广义相对论（General Relativity）的近似解和满足CEB的量子引力（quantum gravity）流体力学模型进行描述。

Result: 该模型发现：满足协变熵界（CEB）的宇宙学初始态或无局域激发，或仅含一个大黑洞；通过合适的原初黑洞分布，可同时解释全部暗物质及詹姆斯·韦伯空间望远镜（JWST）看到的早期星系；部分暗物质可能来自衰变黑洞的普朗克尺度（Planck-scale）残余。

Conclusion: 一个包含早期微小黑洞衰变和适当原初黑洞分布的宇宙学模型，能够在满足协变熵界（CEB）的前提下，同时拟合宇宙微波背景（CMB）数据、解释暗物质成分以及早期星系观测结果。

Abstract: We argue that cosmological models obeying the Covariant Entropy Bound (CEB) mathematically favor states with no localized excitations or one large black hole containing all the energy in a constrained initial state. In order to get a long radiation-dominated era, one must postulate that at a very early time, most horizon volumes of the universe contained tiny black holes that decayed into radiation. A previous work by two of the authors showed that such a scenario could fit the data on the Cosmic Microwave Background (CMB). In order to account for dark matter, we also postulate some random black holes of at least horizon size at that time. A reasonable distribution of such primordial black holes can account for all of dark matter as well as the early galaxies seen by the James Webb Space Telescope. Some of the dark matter may also be in Planck-scale remnants of the decaying black holes. We describe our model both in terms of approximate solutions to General Relativity and a speculative quantum gravity model whose hydrodynamics matches the flat $p = \pm ρ$ FRW model that saturates the CEB.

### [101] [No Evidence for Superradiant Axions in LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA GWTC-5 Binary Black Hole Spins](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01317)
*Orion Ning,Benjamin R. Safdi,Catherine Welch*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本研究利用LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA GWTC-5目录中257个双黑洞并合事件的自旋测量数据，通过分层贝叶斯分析对超轻轴子进行了约束。在95%置信度下排除了轴子质量范围1.7×10⁻¹⁴ eV至3.3×10⁻¹² eV，这是对QCD轴子质量最稳健的下限约束之一。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: QCD轴子（QCD axion）及类轴子粒子（axion-like particles）可能在旋转黑洞周围形成束缚云，通过超辐射不稳定性（superradiance instability）消耗黑洞自旋。观测黑洞自旋分布中的质量-自旋关系异常可以提供轴子存在的间接证据，从而限制轴子质量范围。

Method: 基于LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA合作组提供的GWTC-5目录，该目录是当前最大的公开双黑洞（BBH）并合目录，包含257个并合事件，黑洞质量跨度约5-135 M☉。研究采用分层贝叶斯分析（hierarchical Bayesian analysis），在黑洞自旋种群模型框架下对超轻轴子（ultralight axions）进行约束。

Result: 在超过两个数量级的质量范围内未发现轴子信号，以95%置信度排除了轴子质量1.7×10⁻¹⁴ eV ≲ m_a ≲ 3.3×10⁻¹² eV的范围。由于此前该质量窗口的超辐射界限基于X射线自旋测量，存在较大的建模系统误差，本结果被认为是目前对QCD轴子质量最稳健的下限约束之一。

Conclusion: 利用引力波数据进行的贝叶斯分析在广泛质量范围内未发现轴子存在的证据，并给出了强约束排除区间。该结果相较于依赖X射线自旋测量的此前研究具有更低的建模系统误差，因而提供了更可靠的轴子质量下界。

Abstract: The quantum chromodynamics (QCD) axion and axion-like particles may form bound clouds around spinning black holes (BHs) when their Compton wavelength is comparable to the BH gravitational radius, depleting the BH spin through what is known as a $\textit{superradiance}$ instability. Using binary BH (BBH) spin measurements obtained from the LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA GWTC-5 catalog, the most extensive public BBH catalog to date containing $N=257$ mergers with BH masses spanning roughly $5$-$135$ $M_\odot$, we perform a hierarchical Bayesian analysis in the context of a BH spin population model to constrain ultralight axions. The presence of axions at a given mass would imprint a unique signature in the observed mass-spin relation relative to the formation distribution. We find no evidence for axions across more than two decades in mass, excluding axion masses $1.7 \times 10^{-14} \, {\rm eV} \lesssim m_a \lesssim 3.3 \times 10^{-12} \, {\rm eV}$ at 95% confidence. Because prior superradiance bounds in this range derive from X-ray spin measurements with substantial modeling systematics, this result represents one of the strongest robust lower bounds on the QCD axion mass.

</details>


### [102] [Sideband Structure of Axion Electrodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02232)
*Run-Min Yao,Xiao-Jun Bi,Peng-Fei Yin,Qing-Guo Huang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文发展了线性化麦克斯韦-轴子系统（Maxwell-axion system）在相干周期轴子背景下的Floquet-Bloch边带（sideband）形式，揭示了光子和轴子分支的边带阶梯结构，并通过辛符号（symplectic signatures）分类了稳定与不稳定的模式耦合，统一了多种共振机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在线性化麦克斯韦-轴子系统中，周期轴子背景对光子传播的调制效应尚未被系统描述，尤其是边带模式之间的耦合稳定性及其与已知共振机制的关系缺乏统一框架。

Method: 采用Floquet–Bloch边带形式（Floquet–Bloch sideband formulation）线性化处理预置磁场和轴子场；通过近简并折叠（folded degeneracy）简化为二模交叉（two-mode crossing）分析，利用辛签名（symplectic signatures）和单值性计算（monodromy calculations）研究时间演化和定态传输行为。

Result: 相同Krein符号（same-Krein-sign）碰撞产生稳定的避免交叉（avoided crossings），异号碰撞产生参数不稳定性（parametric instabilities），统一了轴子-光子差频通道与Mathieu和Masaki-Aoki-Soda共振；定态传输中的通量特征区分了有界正向转换、前后向阻带及分布反射；射线投影给出局域WKB描述，有效波数区别于真实轴子动量；外场图（external-field diagrams）再现边带选择定则，全时单值性计算验证了不稳定性拓扑与有限耦合偏移。

Conclusion: 所建立的边带形式为周期轴子背景下光子和轴子耦合提供了一个统一的理论框架，揭示了稳定性与辛签名之间的深层联系，并成功将已知的不同共振机制纳入同一代数结构。

Abstract: We develop a Floquet--Bloch sideband formulation of the linearized Maxwell--axion system in a coherent periodic axion background. Linearizing around prescribed magnetic and axion fields, we show that the pump generates a sideband ladder of photon and axion branches. Near an isolated folded degeneracy, this ladder reduces to a two-mode crossing whose algebra is fixed by the symplectic signatures of the colliding modes. In temporal fixed-momentum evolution, same-Krein-sign collisions give stable avoided crossings, whereas opposite-sign collisions give parametric instabilities, unifying the axion-photon difference channel with the Mathieu and Masaki-Aoki-Soda resonances. In stationary fixed-frequency transfer, the corresponding flux signatures distinguish bounded forward conversion from forward-backward stop bands and distributed reflection. Ray projection of a temporal pump gives a related but local WKB description of driven forward mixing, with an effective wavenumber distinct from the true axion momentum. External-field diagrams reproduce the sideband selection rules, and full temporal monodromy calculations verify the instability topology and finite-coupling shifts.

</details>


### [103] [Chebyshev Approximations of Feynman Integrals for Collider Physics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02411)
*Samuel Abreu,Afonso Guerreiro,Ben Page*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于切比雪夫多项式（Chebyshev polynomials）逼近的新方法，用于求解费曼积分（Feynman integrals）的规范微分方程（canonical differential equations）。该方法利用费曼积分的解析性，沿路径构建快速收敛的多项式逼近，并引入自适应采样优化收敛。在双精度浮点运算下，通过一系列双圈、五点示例验证了其在物理相空间（phase space）中的稳定性，其实现与最先进的单重积分方法相比具有竞争力，且几乎无需逐例干预处理虚假奇点（spurious singularities）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决费曼积分中规范微分方程的数值求解问题：现有方法在处理高圈、多点费曼积分时面临计算效率低或需大量人工干预以处理虚假奇点的困难。

Method: 利用切比雪夫多项式对费曼积分进行逼近；基于积分的解析性（analyticity properties）沿路径构建快速收敛的多项式近似；引入自适应逼近方法（adaptive approximation method）动态采样以优化收敛；在双精度浮点算术（double-precision arithmetic）中实现该框架。

Result: 通过双圈、五点示例的测试表明：该方法在物理相空间中数值稳定性良好；与最先进的单重积分方法（state-of-the-art one-fold integral methods）相比具有竞争力；几乎不需要针对虚假奇点进行逐例人工干预。

Conclusion: 所提出的基于切比雪夫多项式逼近的框架能够高效、稳定地求解费曼积分的规范微分方程，降低了对人工干预的依赖，为高圈多点费曼积分的高精度数值计算提供了有前景的新途径。

Abstract: We present a novel approach for solving canonical differential equations for Feynman integrals based on an approximation of the integrals with Chebyshev polynomials. By exploiting the analyticity properties of Feynman integrals, the method constructs rapidly converging polynomial approximations along a path, enabling highly efficient numerical evaluation. Moreover, we introduce an adaptive approximation method that dynamically samples to optimise convergence. We implement this framework in double-precision arithmetic and demonstrate its stability across physical phase space using a series of two-loop, five-point examples. Our proof-of-principle implementation proves competitive with state-of-the-art one-fold integral methods, while requiring little to no case-by-case intervention to handle spurious singularities.

</details>

### [104] [Dirac oscillator in a helically twisted spacetime with axial torsion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01301)
*Matheus D. Moro,Fabiano M. Andrade,Faizuddin Ahmed,Edilberto O. Silva*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了具有均匀轴向挠率（axial torsion）的螺旋扭曲时空中狄拉克振子（Dirac oscillator）的量子动力学，揭示了其二阶问题的有序乘积结构、径向耦合自伴系统、超对称零模（supersymmetric zero mode）的扭转敏感性，以及分扇区热力学函数和手征流（chiral current）的谱学性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索弯曲时空与扭转效应（torsion）对相对论量子系统（狄拉克振子）的影响，特别是螺旋时空几何如何调制能谱、零模态（zero mode）和拓扑保护（topological protection）性质。

Method: 从标准正交余标架（orthonormal coframe）出发，显式计算Levi-Civita自旋联络（spin connection）并分离出轴向扭曲（axial contortion）的几何贡献；通过保留Moshinsky耦合中的矩阵β，将二阶问题化为有序乘积算子 $\hat{\Pi}_+ \hat{\Pi}_-$；采用有限元方法（finite-element method）求解径向耦合自伴方程组。

Result: 在平坦极限下重现了平面狄拉克振子谱；发现了纵向动量（longitudinal momentum）的不对称依赖、避免能级交叉（avoided level crossings）以及 $E=Mc^2$ 处的超对称零模。轴向挠率和纵向动量保持该零模，而螺旋扭曲（helical twist）使其二次型抬升。获得了分扇区热力学函数和纵向矢量流与轴矢流（axial current），Witten指标分析表明螺旋扭曲是移除保护零模的形变。

Conclusion: 螺旋时空的几何形变（尤其是螺旋扭曲）能够解除超对称零模的保护，而均匀轴向挠率与纵向动量则维持其存在；该结果为扭转时空中的相对论量子系统提供了完整的能谱和流-热力学描述。

Abstract: We investigate the Dirac oscillator in a helically twisted spacetime endowed with a uniform axial torsion. Starting from an orthonormal coframe, we compute the Levi--Civita spin connection explicitly and separate the geometric contribution from the axial contortion. Retaining the matrix $β$ in the radial Moshinsky coupling, we show that the second-order problem is the ordered product $\hatΠ_+\hatΠ_-$ rather than the square of a single operator. The resulting radial dynamics is a coupled, self-adjoint two-component system in which the spin connection supplies the correct cylindrical radial operator, while the off-diagonal metric generates the helical combination $m/r-ωk$ and a Coulomb-like geometric term. A finite-element solution reproduces the planar Dirac-oscillator spectrum in the flat limit and reveals asymmetric dependence on the longitudinal momentum, avoided level crossings, and a supersymmetric zero mode at $E=Mc^2$. The axial torsion and longitudinal momentum preserve this zero mode, whereas the helical twist lifts it quadratically. Sector-resolved thermodynamic functions are obtained from the relativistic bound-state spectrum. The explicit spinors further determine longitudinal vector and axial currents, and a Witten-index analysis identifies the helical twist as the deformation that removes the protected zero mode.

</details>

Abstract: We revisit the problem of minimally coupling matter to Einstein gravity in three dimensions with negative cosmological constant. States in the Hilbert space correspond to Virasoro conformal blocks with operators of conformal weight $h<c/24$. Our answer reproduces the AdS$_3$ Wilson spool and agrees with the known one-loop result. ### [107] [Wormholes as red herrings: reflection positivity and the reconstruction of unitary quantum field theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01322)
*Jacob McNamara,Zhencheng Wang*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文证明了量子场论（QFT）可由闭流形配分函数唯一确定（至多相差幺正同构），并据此指出希尔伯特空间因子化（Hilbert-space factorization）的明显破坏与欧几里得虫洞（Euclidean wormholes）情形类似，均源于对荷空间（charged states）谱的不完全限制，而非量子引力（quantum gravity）的深层问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Coleman曾指出，量子引力中与欧几里得虫洞相关的配分函数因子化（partition-function factorization）的明显破坏，实际上源于对理论系综（ensemble of theories）的隐式平均。本文旨在为空间虫洞（spatial wormholes，即爱因斯坦-罗森桥，Einstein-Rosen bridges）导致的希尔伯特空间因子化明显破坏提供类似的论证。

Method: 本文建立了一个关于量子场论的重构定理（reconstruction theorem）：幺正QFT（unitary QFT）由闭流形配分函数（closed-manifold partition functions）唯一确定（至多相差幺正同构）；每个反射正性（reflection-positive）配分函数都来自某个幺正QFT；流形制备的态（states prepared by manifolds）张成重构理论对称群下的不变态空间（space of invariant states）。

Result: 定理表明，量子场论的结构完全由其闭流形配分函数决定，且反射正性保证了QFT的幺正性。

Conclusion: 从引力角度解释，任何希尔伯特空间因子化的明显破坏都是误导性的（red herring），其根源在于限制了一个不完全的荷态谱（incomplete spectrum of charged states），而非量子引力的根本性问题。

Abstract: As Coleman famously argued, the apparent breakdown of partition-function factorization in quantum gravity associated with Euclidean wormholes is a red herring, arising from a hidden average over an ensemble of theories. We present a direct analog of Coleman's argument for the apparent breakdown of Hilbert-space factorization associated with spatial wormholes, i.e., Einstein--Rosen bridges. Our main result is the following reconstruction theorem for quantum field theories: unitary QFTs are determined, up to unitary isomorphism, by their closed-manifold partition functions; every reflection-positive partition function arises from a unitary quantum field theory; and the states prepared by manifolds span the space of invariant states under the reconstructed theory's symmetry group. Interpreting the result gravitationally, we conclude that any apparent breakdown of Hilbert-space factorization is a red herring, arising from restricting to an incomplete spectrum of charged states.

Method: 引入拓扑 QFT 模块（topological QFT block）与重子 QFT 模块（baryonic QFT block），并定义针对这些模块的新的 $SL(2,\mathbb{Z})$ 对偶移动（duality moves）。在此基础上对“好”的循环箭形理论推导镜像对称性（mirror symmetry）并扩展至完整对偶网络；对“坏”的循环箭形理论区分局域坏（由欠平衡规范节点导致）与全局坏（由循环拓扑本身导致）两种类型。

Conclusion: 所提出的场论算法能够系统构造三维 $\mathcal{N}=4$ 循环箭形理论的完整 $SL(2,\mathbb{Z})$ 对偶网络。对“坏”循环箭形的分析深化了对循环拓扑导致的对偶性失效模式的理解，指标匹配进一步支持了所提出对偶方案的正确性。

Abstract: We introduce a field-theoretic algorithm to find the $SL(2,\mathbb{Z})$ duality web of 3d $\mathcal{N}=4$ circular quiver theories with unitary gauge groups, extending the algorithm for linear quivers. Although circular and linear quivers share the same local structure, the circular topology requires additional ingredients, which we formulate in terms of topological and baryonic QFT blocks, together with new $SL(2,\mathbb{Z})$ duality moves acting on them. For good circular quivers, this provides a field-theoretic derivation of mirror symmetry and extends it to the full $SL(2,\mathbb{Z})$ duality web. We then study bad circular quivers, distinguishing between local badness, associated with under-balanced gauge nodes, and global badness, arising from the circular topology itself. In particular, we analyze the magnetic and electric dual frames of globally bad circular quivers and provide additional evidence for the proposed duality by matching the Higgs branch index with the dual Coulomb branch index. Abstract: We study the fusion of two conjugate conformal line defects on the sphere. At small separation, their spectrum is governed by a universal Fusion Master Equation. ### [110] [Wigner negativity in Krylov space and emergent semiclassicality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01351)

TL;DR: 本文提出Krylov基（Krylov basis）在大$N$复杂多体系统中可提供半经典（semiclassical）动力学表示，并通过Wigner负性（Wigner negativity）在多个可解模型中的增长行为，论证Krylov空间中的动力学表现出半经典性——负性要么保持为常数，要么仅以$t^{1/2}$缓慢增长，不随希尔伯特空间维度缩放。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在多个可解模型中研究时间演化下Krylov空间中Wigner负性的增长行为：2D共形场论（CFT）（初始态为真空或热场双重态（thermofield double state）被初级算符激发）、随机矩阵理论（random matrix theory）（初始态为两副本间的最大纠缠态）、以及双尺度化SYK模型（double-scaled SYK model）。

Result: 2D CFT中Wigner负性保持$O(1)$常数，不在后期增长；随机矩阵理论中Krylov基下的Wigner负性在$O(1)$时间尺度上以$t^{1/2}$增长，但不随希尔伯特空间维度缩放；双尺度化SYK模型中，早期呈现常数负性（近似经典相），后期呈现$t^{1/2}$增长（半经典相）。

Conclusion: 所有例子中Wigner负性要么保持恒定要么缓慢增长，表明Krylov空间中动力学的半经典性是普遍涌现的。

Abstract: We propose that the Krylov basis gives a semiclassical representation of dynamics in general large-$N$, complex, many-body systems. As a probe of this semiclassicality, we study the growth of Wigner negativity -- a measure of the complexity of classical simulation -- under time evolution in Krylov space in several solvable models. We begin with 2d CFTs, initially in either the vacuum or the thermofield double state on a line excited by a primary operator. In both cases, Wigner negativity remains an $O(1)$ constant and does not grow at late times, indicating approximately classical dynamics in the Krylov basis. We then study random matrix theory with the maximally entangled state between two copies as the initial state. For general one-cut matrix models, we argue that Wigner negativity in the Krylov basis grows as $t^{1/2}$ at large $O(1)$ times but does not scale with the Hilbert space dimension, thus indicating semiclassical dynamics in Krylov space. Finally, in the double-scaled SYK model, we find an approximately classical phase (constant negativity) at early times and a semiclassical phase ($t^{1/2}$ growth) at late times. In all these examples, Wigner negativity either remains constant or grows slowly, demonstrating emergent semiclassicality of dynamics in Krylov space.

### [111] [Quantum JT Gravity in a box as a Pöschl-Teller Scattering Problem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01385)
*Luca Griguolo,Jacopo Papalini,Lorenzo Russo,Domenico Seminara,Alex Tarana*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文对具有有限狄利克雷边界条件的Jackiw-Teitelboim引力进行了正则量子化，将动力学重新表述为排斥性Pöschl-Teller势中非相对论粒子的散射问题，得到了精确的宇宙波函数、圆盘配分函数以及热两点函数和四点函数的闭式表达，并提出了超越黑洞视界的紫外完备方案。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 获得了精确的宇宙波函数（wavefunctions of the universe）和圆盘配分函数（disk partition function），可解释为裸长度为零的态之间的跃迁矩阵元。在渐近极限下还原为刘维尔量子力学（Liouville quantum mechanics），重现标准Schwarzian谱密度。在有限截止下，谱测度出现了现有$T\bar T$方法中不存在的非微扰修正。热两点函数和四点函数也获得了闭式表达。

Conclusion: 有限截止下的JT引力存在超越微扰的非微扰修正，且通过解析延拓Brown-York电荷可自然地将散射问题推广至黑洞内部构型，从而为模型提供一种紫外完备方案。

Abstract: We present a canonical quantization of Jackiw-Teitelboim gravity with finite Dirichlet boundary conditions, using the geodesic length between the two boundaries and its conjugate momentum as reduced phase space variables. The dynamics is recast as the scattering problem of a nonrelativistic particle in a repulsive Pöschl-Teller potential, naturally embedded within a hyperbolic reduction of the $\mathfrak{sl}(2,\mathbb{R})$ Casimir. We obtain exact wavefunctions of the universe and the disk partition function, interpreted as a transition matrix element between states of vanishing bare length. In the asymptotic limit, the theory reduces to Liouville quantum mechanics and reproduces the standard Schwarzian spectral density. At finite cutoff, however, the spectral measure exhibits genuinely nonperturbative corrections, absent in existing $T\bar T$ treatments. We also obtain closed form expressions for thermal two-point functions in terms of Wilson functions and propose diagrammatic rules for time- and out-of-time-ordered four-point functions. We further address the issue of the branch cut singularity of the quasi-local energy and propose a UV completion of the model in which the Brown-York charge is analytically continued beyond the black hole horizon. This continuation naturally extends the scattering problem to configurations that foliate the black hole interior.

### [112] [Preparing a Thermofield Double State with Feedback Quantum Algorithms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01653)
*Guilherme E. L. Pexe,Lucas A. M. Rattighieri,Felipe F. Fanchini,Dario Rosa,Amilson R. Fritsch*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文针对Maldacena-Qi模型（双耦合Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev模型）的热场双态（TFD）制备问题，发现标准反馈量子算法（FALQON）及其时间重标变体（TR-FALQON）存在动力学限制而无法收敛；提出混合ITE-TR-FALQON协议，通过结合虚时演化（imaginary-time evolution）与时间重标机制，成功突破了对称性陷阱，实现接近单位保真度的TFD态高效制备。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 有效制备关联热态（correlated thermal states），特别是热场双态（Thermofield Double, TFD），是在量子处理器上模拟量子引力模型和多体热力学（many-body thermodynamics）的基本前提。本文聚焦于与AdS_2可穿越虫洞（traversable wormhole）对偶的Maldacena-Qi模型，旨在解决其基态制备中反馈量子算法面临的收敛困难。

Method: 提出混合ITE-TR-FALQON协议，该协议将虚时演化增强型FALQON（ITE-FALQON）中的虚时演化（imaginary-time evolution）与时间重标机制（time-rescaling mechanism）相结合，以克服标准反馈量子算法（FALQON）及其时间重标变体（TR-FALQON）在平凡乘积态（product state）初始化下的动力学限制。

Result: 数值结果表明，引入非幺正动力学（non-unitary dynamics）是打破对称性陷阱（symmetry traps）和滤除激发态（excited states）的必要条件；时间重标机制则显著加速算法收敛。所提方法实现了接近单位保真度的高精度结果，并精确复现了精确TFD态的冯·诺伊曼熵（von Neumann entropy）和Rényi熵（Rényi entropy）谱。

Conclusion: 混合ITE-TR-FALQON协议能够高效制备Maldacena-Qi模型的基态（即TFD态），克服了标准反馈算法在高度纠缠态制备中的动力学局限，为量子引力模型的多体量子模拟提供了可行路径。

Abstract: The efficient preparation of correlated thermal states, such as the Thermofield Double (TFD) state, is a fundamental prerequisite for simulating quantum gravity models and many-body thermodynamics on quantum processors. In this work, we investigate the ground state preparation of the Two Coupled Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev model, known as the Maldacena-Qi model, which is dual to a traversable wormhole in $AdS_2$, utilizing feedback-based quantum algorithms. We demonstrate that the standard feedback-based quantum algorithm (FALQON) and its time-rescaled variant (TR-FALQON) face severe kinetic limitations in this system, failing to converge to the highly entangled ground state when initialized in trivial product states. To overcome these barriers, we propose the hybrid ITE-TR-FALQON protocol, which integrates the imaginary-time evolution present in imaginary-time-enhanced FALQON (ITE-FALQON) with the time-rescaling mechanism. Our numerical results indicate that the introduction of non-unitary dynamics is strictly necessary to break symmetry traps and filter out excited states, while time-rescaling drastically accelerates algorithm convergence. The proposed method achieves fidelities close to unity and reproduces the von Neumann and Rényi entropy spectra of the exact TFD state with high precision.

</details>


### [113] [Morse Bridge between Planar Kepler and Hyperbolic Landau Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01778)
*Mikhail S. Plyushchay*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文揭示平面开普勒-库仑问题和双曲平面兰道问题通过一维莫尔斯哈密顿量（Morse Hamiltonian）相互联系。通过刘维尔变换（Liouville transformation）、耦合常数变异（coupling-constant metamorphosis）和轨道圆归约（horocyclic reduction），两个系统的动力学均可映射到同一个莫尔斯谱问题，从而建立起包括束缚谱、连续阈、共振和散射数据在内的完整对应关系，并进一步推导出开普勒圆锥曲线与磁力圆（magnetic circles）、轨道圆（horocycles）和超圆（hypercycles）之间的几何字典。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索经典量子系统中两个看似迥异的范式系统——平面开普勒-库仑问题（planar Kepler–Coulomb problem）与双曲平面兰道问题（Landau problem on the hyperbolic plane H²）——之间是否存在深层数学联系。

Method: 在开普勒侧，使用刘维尔变换和耦合常数变异将径向动力学转化为莫尔斯问题，其中开普勒极角演变为莫尔斯演化参数；在兰道侧，通过对双曲磁性动力学进行轨道圆归约（horocyclic reduction），得到相同的莫尔斯哈密顿量，并引入量子半密度修正（quantum half-density correction）。

Result: 径向开普勒问题和双曲兰道问题中固定轨道圆动量扇区被映射到同一个莫尔斯谱问题，从而关联两者的束缚谱、连续阈、共振和散射数据。兰道时间演化具有开普勒圆锥曲线形式，可归约为莫尔斯系统的束缚、阈和散射轨迹。

Conclusion: 建立了一个联系开普勒圆锥曲线与磁力圆、轨道圆和超圆的几何字典，并将兰道问题的磁SL(2,ℝ)对称性转化为莫尔斯系统的谱生成代数结构（spectrum-generating algebraic structure），揭示了两个系统深层的统一数学框架。

Abstract: We show that two paradigmatic systems, the planar Kepler--Coulomb problem and the Landau problem on the hyperbolic plane $H^2$, are connected by a common one-dimensional mediator: the Morse Hamiltonian. On the Kepler side, a Liouville transformation and coupling-constant metamorphosis turn the radial dynamics into the Morse problem, with the Kepler polar angle becoming the Morse evolution parameter. On the Landau side, horocyclic reduction of the hyperbolic magnetic dynamics gives the same Morse Hamiltonian, with a quantum half-density correction. Consequently, the radial Kepler problem and the fixed-horocyclic-momentum sectors of the hyperbolic Landau problem are mapped to one Morse spectral problem, relating their bound spectra, continuum thresholds, resonances and scattering data. We further show that the Landau time evolution has a Kepler-conic form and reduces to the bound, threshold and scattering trajectories of the Morse system. The resulting dictionary connects Kepler conics with magnetic circles, horocycles and hypercycles, and turns the magnetic $SL(2,\mathbb R)$ symmetry of the Landau problem into the spectrum-generating algebraic structure of the Morse system.

### [114] [Uniqueness and Analytic Structures of Bosonic String Effective Amplitudes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01790)

Main category: hep-th

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过对振幅施加规范不变性（gauge invariance）、局域性（locality）和循环性（cyclicity）等最小假设，唯一确定一组维度提升算子；并在有限$α'$下，利用由规范不变且依赖于$α'$的导数算子构成的逆算子，从杨-米尔斯振幅进行递归构造。

Conclusion: 该构造方法不仅恢复了完整的玻色弦有效振幅，还揭示了其与杨-米尔斯-标量振幅之间的普适分解结构，且这一结构具有广泛的推广性。

Abstract: We revisit the zero-transcendentality sector of bosonic string effective amplitudes with spin-1 external states, conjectured to correspond to a mass-deformed $(DF)^2$ theory, known as the $(DF)^2{+}\text{YM}$ theory. Imposing gauge invariance, locality, and cyclicity under minimal assumptions uniquely fixes a set of dimension-raising operators and leads to a recursive construction of amplitudes from Yang-Mills amplitudes in the $α'{\to}0$ limit. At finite $α'$, certain derivative operators dressed with gauge invariant and $α'$-dependent factors, what we call $\textit{inverse operators}$, reconstruct the full bosonic string effective amplitudes, yielding compact expressions that universally factorize into tachyon-pole coefficients times Yang-Mills-Scalar amplitudes. This structure holds at arbitrary multiplicity and also extends to the amplitudes of the pure $(DF)^2$, $(DF)^2{+}φ^{3}$ and $(DF)^2{+}\text{YM}{+}φ^{3}$ theories.
