### [115] [Lubkin-Page typicality bounds for Type~II von~Neumann factors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01873)
*Zhi-Wei Wang,Samuel L. Braunstein*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文证明 Lubkin-Page 界限可推广至 Type II von Neumann 代数因子，涵盖量子场论与量子引力中的可观测量代数；对于 Type II₁ 因子，子系统的互信息在有限维近似下以 $O((d_A d_B / d_E)^2)$ 消失；对于 Type II_∞ 因子（包括引力代数），界限额外受 Bekenstein-Hawking 熵指数抑制；同时指出向 Type III 因子推广的障碍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 涌现时空（emergent spacetime）的典型性论证依赖于 Lubkin-Page 界限，但该界限假设张量积希尔伯特空间（Type I von Neumann 代数），而量子场论与量子引力中的可观测量代数普遍为 Type II 或 Type III 型，因此需要检验该界限在更一般代数结构下是否仍然成立。

Method: 论文分别对超有限 Type II₁ 因子（具有三部分分解 $R \cong A \otimes B \otimes E$）和 Type II_∞ 因子（包括通过交叉积方法构造的引力代数）进行理论证明；对 Type II₁ 因子在有限维近似下计算互信息的上界，对 Type II_∞ 因子分析 Bekenstein-Hawking 熵对界限的指数抑制效应，并识别向 Type III 因子推广的障碍。

Result: 对于 Type II₁ 因子，当 $d_A d_B \leq d_E$ 时，子系统 $A$ 与 $B$ 的互信息以 $O((d_A d_B / d_E)^2)$ 消失（定理1）；对于 Type II_∞ 因子，界限额外受到 Bekenstein-Hawking 熵控制的指数抑制（定理2）。

Conclusion: Lubkin-Page 界限对 Type II von Neumann 代数因子成立，但向 Type III 因子的推广存在障碍；论文还提出了可观测量代数的交换子（commutant）能否作为天然热浴（thermal bath）以进一步收紧界限的开放问题。

Abstract: Typicality arguments for emergent spacetime rely on the Lubkin-Page bounds, which show that generic quantum states have vanishing correlations between subsystems. These bounds assume a tensor-product Hilbert space (a Type~I von~Neumann algebra), but the observable algebras in quantum field theory and quantum gravity are generically Type~II or Type~III, raising the question of whether the bounds survive. We prove that they do for all Type~II von~Neumann factors. For the hyperfinite Type~II$_1$ factor with a tripartite decomposition $R \cong A \otimes B \otimes E$, the mutual information between subsystems $A$ and $B$ vanishes as $O((d_A d_B / d_E)^2)$ in finite-dimensional approximations, provided $d_A d_B \leq d_E$ (Theorem~1). For Type~II$_\infty$ factors, including the gravitational algebras constructed via the crossed-product method by Witten and by Chandrasekaran, Longo, Penington, and Witten, the bound acquires an additional exponential suppression controlled by the Bekenstein-Hawking entropy (Theorem~2). We identify the obstructions to extending the result to Type~III factors and discuss the open question of whether the commutant of the observable algebra can serve as a natural thermal bath that tightens the bound further.

</details>


### [116] [Tuning quantum magic of pure quantum chaotic states with a gravity dual](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01930)
*Antonio M. García-García,Xianlong Liu,Jie-ping Zheng*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了基于Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev（SYK）模型的量子态中的量子魔法（quantum magic）资源，在大量子数极限下，纯Kourkoulou-Maldacena（KM）态的量子魔法随N线性增长，其斜率可随黑洞温度在0到1/2之间调节；而高斯态经实时演化后的反平坦度（FAF）则以指数速率趋近于N/2。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子魔法（quantum magic）是一种衡量量子态能否被经典计算机高效模拟的基本资源。本文旨在研究由Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev（SYK）哈密顿量构建的量子态中量子魔法的行为，特别是其与黑洞物理、量子混沌以及低维量子引力的关系。

Method: 采用费米子反平坦度（fermionic anti-flatness, FAF）作为量子魔法的度量，对大量子数（N）极限下的纯Kourkoulou-Maldacena（KM）态进行解析分析；对SYK哈密顿量实时演化后的高斯态，通过Ruelle-Pollicot共振（Ruelle-Pollicot resonance）分析其指数收敛速率；对SYK能量本征态中N的次主导修正，结合Krylov子空间（Krylov subspace）与GPU加速技术进行数值计算（N ≤ 54）。

Result: 在大N极限下，纯KM态的量子魔法随N线性增长，其斜率可在0到1/2之间随黑洞温度调节；高斯态实时演化后的FAF以指数速率趋近于N/2，速率由主导的Ruelle-Pollicot共振倍数决定；SYK能量本征态中N的次主导修正随N指数衰减，但若SYK耦合变稀疏则呈幂律衰减，且靠近基态（具有对应引力类比区域）的态中修正量级更大。

Conclusion: 本文结果为量子信息、量子混沌与低维量子引力之间的关系提供了新的见解。

Abstract: Quantum magic is a fundamental resource that quantifies to what extent quantum states can be efficiently simulated on a classical computer. We study it for states constructed from the Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev (SYK) Hamiltonian with $N$ Majoranas by the fermionic anti-flatness (FAF). We show analytically that, in the large $N$ limit, the quantum magic of pure Kourkoulou-Maldacena (KM) states, dual to a quantum black hole with an end-of-world particle behind the horizon, is linear in $N$ with a slope, depending on the black hole temperature, that can be tuned between zero and $1/2$. By contrast, the FAF of Gaussian states evolved in real time with the SYK Hamitonian approaches $\approx N/2$ exponentially at a rate given by a multiple of the leading Ruelle-Pollicot resonance. Subleading corrections in $N$ for SYK energy eigenstates, computed numerically for $N \leq 54$ by combining Krylov subspace with GPU acceleration techniques, decay exponentially with $N$, but power-law if the SYK couplings are sparsified, and are order of magnitude larger for states close to the ground state, a region with an established gravity analogue. Our results offer new insights about the relation between quantum information, quantum chaos and low-dimension quantum gravity.

### [117] [Local symmetry and the dependence on extended spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01999)
*Keith Glennon,Peter West*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文证明了在低阶展开下，线性化E-理论（E theory）具有局部对称性（local symmetry），但其参数必须满足关于拓展时空（extended spacetime）的微分约束。在将E-理论分解为Siegel理论（即双重场论，Double Field theory）时，类似的参数限制也被发现，但与普遍使用的截面条件（section conditions）不同。此外，Siegel理论的膨胀子方程（dilaton equation）在该对称性下保持不变，前提是参数满足类似的非线性约束。文章主张无需对E-理论或Siegel理论的场施加额外条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨线性化E-理论在低阶水平上是否具有局部对称性，并澄清该对称性参数所需的约束条件，以及其与双重场论中截面条件的关系。

Method: 通过分解E-理论导出Siegel理论（双重场论），分析局部对称性参数需满足的微分条件，并与标准截面条件进行比较；同时验证Siegel理论的膨胀子方程在非线性参数约束下的不变性。

Result: 发现局部对称性参数必须满足关于拓展时空的微分约束；在双重场论框架中，这些约束不同于普遍的截面条件；膨胀子方程在参数满足非线性约束时具有对称不变性。

Conclusion: 线性化E-理论在低阶具有局部对称性，其参数约束与双重场论的截面条件不同，且无需对场本身施加额外条件。

Abstract: We show that linearised E theory possesses a local symmetry at low levels provided the parameters of the local symmetry obey differential conditions that restrict their dependence on the extended spacetime. In the decomposition of E theory that leads to Siegel theory, also known as Double Field theory, we also find the analogous restrictions on the parameters. They are different to the section conditions which are universally used in this context. We also show that the dilaton equation of Siegel theory is invariant under the local symmetry if the parameters satisfy an analogous non-linear constraint on the parameters. We argue that there is no need to impose conditions on the fields of E theory or Siegel theory.

We find out that the exponential growth depends strictly on the number of bosons in the system as well as their inherent squeezing of the matter wave packets. ### [119] [Supersymmetric twists in twistor space and holography](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02145)
*Matheus Balisa,Eduardo Casali*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在扭量空间（twistor space）中计算了若干超对称场论的超对称扭变（supersymmetric twists），包括超对称自对偶杨-米尔斯理论的最小超对称扭变与手征代数扭变，以及$\mathcal{N}=1$自对偶超引力的最小扭变。对于$\mathcal{N}=4$情形，还在手征全息（chiral holography）框架下找到了它们的全息对偶。研究表明，扭量空间中的规范理论最小扭变将理论局域化到时空上，使得复结构选择显式化，并复现了时空上的最小扭变；超共形理论经进一步扭变后局域化到时空中的平面，复现了$\mathcal{N}=4$超对称杨-米尔斯理论的手征代数扭变。体态（bulk）对偶也表现出类似的局域化，复现了扭变全息（twisted holography）的结果。

Conclusion: 扭量空间中的超对称扭变提供了一种系统化的框架，将场论局域化到时空或更低维子流形上，并自然复现已知的时空扭变与扭变全息结果，深化了对超对称场论与全息对偶之间几何联系的理解。

Abstract: We compute some supersymmetric twists of field theories in twistor space, including the minimal supersymmetric and the chiral algebra twists of supersymmetric self-dual Yang-Mills, and the minimal twist of $\mathcal{N}=1$ self-dual supergravity. In the case of $\mathcal{N}=4$ we also find their holographic duals in the framework of chiral holography. We find that the minimal twist of gauge theories in twistor space localizes them to spacetime, making the choice of complex structure manifest, and reproducing the minimal twist on spacetime. For superconformal theories we apply a further twist which localizes the theory to a plane contained on spacetime, reproducing the chiral algebra twist of $\mathcal{N}=4$ sYM. *Eric Perlmutter*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本论文将Fyodorov-Hiary-Keating猜想推广至量子引力中的黑洞微观态计数，通过全息对偶（holography）得到共形场论（conformal field theory）中高维本原算符（primary operators）区间计数的严格界限。极端涨落由具有指定尾部分布的随机变量刻画，在大N极限下这些O(1)的剧烈涨落对半经典AdS引力路径积分（path integral）的分辨率设置了定量极限。研究指出AdS黑洞微观态谱及其场论对偶应呈现随机矩阵（random matrices）的极值统计（extreme value statistics），属于高斯对数关联场（Gaussian log-correlated fields）的普适类（universality class）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将Fyodorov-Hiary-Keating猜想从随机矩阵理论引入量子引力与全息对偶领域，旨在理解AdS/CFT对应中黑洞微观态计数的极端统计行为及其对半经典引力路径积分分辨率的限制。

Method: 通过全息对偶将黑洞微观态计数问题映射为CFT中高维本原算符的区间计数问题；引入高斯随机模型（Gaussian random models）刻画态计数的剧烈N依赖（erratic N-dependence）并将其表达为去相关性质（decorrelation property）。

Result: 推导出CFT高维本原算符区间计数的严格界限；揭示了态计数的极端涨落由具有特定尾部分布的随机变量支配；指出在大N下单粒子（order-one）的剧烈涨落为半经典AdS引力路径积分的分辨率设置了基本极限。

Conclusion: AdS黑洞微观态谱及其场论对偶应属于随机矩阵的极值统计普适类，具体而言属于高斯对数关联场的普适类，从而将黑洞微观态计数的剧烈N依赖现象统一到随机矩阵理论的框架内。

Abstract: We formulate an avatar of the Fyodorov-Hiary-Keating conjecture for black hole microstate counts in quantum gravity. By holography, this implies sharp bounds on interval counts of high-dimension primary operators in conformal field theory. The extremal fluctuations of these counts are characterized by a random variable, with a prescribed tail distribution. At large $N$, these order-one erratic fluctuations set a quantitative limit on the resolution of the semiclassical AdS gravitational path integral. Gaussian random models for state counts arise naturally in this context; we express the phenomenon of erratic $N$-dependence in AdS/CFT as a decorrelation property of these models. Our broader point is to suggest that AdS black hole microstate spectra and their field theory duals should exhibit the extreme value statistics of random matrices, lying in the universality class of Gaussian log-correlated fields.

</details>


### [121] [Boundary observables in string field theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02454)
*Klaus Kaja,Carlo Maccaferri,Ulisses Portugal,Jakub Vošmera*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文基于自由弦场论（free string field theory）中带边界的规范不变作用量，定义了类比广义相对论中Brown-York荷的新型规范不变可观测量。该可观测量源自边界蝌蚪图（boundary tadpole），与弦场论（SFT）规范群在给定背景下的等度规（isometries）相关联。构造的一致性仅要求背景运动方程在边界上成立，因此这些可观测量也可定义于由体源（bulk sources）生成的背景。在开弦场论中，计算了常电磁场强度解的边界通量和Coulomb解对应的荷；在闭弦场论中，刻画了二维弦论中弦毛黑洞（stringy-haired black-hole）解的无限守恒荷。此外，还将这些边界可观测量推广至完整相互作用弦场论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在弦场论（string field theory, SFT）中定义类似于广义相对论中Brown-York荷的规范不变边界可观测量，从而为含边界的弦场论系统提供新的守恒荷和物理诊断工具。

Method: 从已有工作（2506.05969）中自由弦场论的规范不变带边界作用量出发，通过边界蝌蚪图构造新型规范不变可观测量，并利用SFT规范群在给定背景下的等度规关联这些可观测量。构造仅要求背景运动方程在边界上满足，从而允许包含体源的情形。

Result: 在开弦场论中，计算了常电磁场强度解的边界通量和Coulomb解对应的荷；在闭弦场论中，表征了二维弦论中弦毛黑洞解的无限守恒荷。

Conclusion: 该构造在自由弦场论中成功建立了与广义相对论Brown-York荷类似的边界可观测量，并推广至完整相互作用弦场论，为弦场论中边界物理的规范不变描述提供了新框架。

Abstract: Starting from the gauge invariant action for free string field theory with boundary recently constructed in 2506.05969, we define new gauge invariant observables which are analogous to the Brown-York charges of General Relativity. Just like the Brown-York charges, our observables originate from a boundary tadpole, and are associated to isometries of the SFT gauge group around a given background. The consistency of the construction requires the equation of motion of the background to be satisfied only at the boundary and therefore these observables can also be defined for backgrounds generated by sources in the bulk. As examples of our construction in open string field theory, we compute the flux through the boundary of constant electromagnetic field-strength solutions and the charge associated to the Coulomb solution. As a further example in closed string field theory, we characterize the infinite conserved charges associated to stringy-haired black-hole solutions in two-dimensional string theory. We also construct a generalization of these boundary observables to the full interacting string field theory.

</details>


### [122] [BRST-BV approach to fields in Poincare patch of AdS](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02495)
*R. R. Metsaev*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文利用AdS空间的庞加莱参数化（Poincaré parametrization）发展了一种适用于自由场的通用BRST-BV形式体系，得到了任意质量和对称类型的场的BRST-BV拉格朗日量（Lagrangian）的一般表达式，并应用于全对称无质量、有质量、部分无质量及连续自旋场，同时建立了约束与非约束两种BRST-BV表述，验证了与度规类拉格朗日量的一致性，并在场与反场空间中实现了AdS空间对称性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在AdS空间中发展一种通用的BRST-BV形式体系，以统一处理具有任意质量和对称类型的自由场，并建立约束与非约束两种表述，弥补已有方法在普适性和对称性实现方面的不足。

Method: 采用AdS空间的庞加莱参数化（Poincaré parametrization），构建适用于任意质量和对称类型自由场的BRST-BV框架，推导出BRST-BV拉格朗日量的一般表达式。将该框架应用于全对称无质量（massless）、有质量（massive）、部分无质量（partially-massless）以及连续自旋（continuous-spin）场，并分别给出约束（constrained）与非约束（unconstrained）两种BRST-BV表述。通过对比验证所得BRST-BV拉格朗日量与基于修正的de Donder散度（modified de Donder divergence）的度规类拉格朗日量（metric-like Lagrangian）之间的一致性。最后在引入场与反场（fields and antifields）的空间中实现AdS空间对称性。

Result: 得到了具有任意质量和对称类型的自由场的BRST-BV拉格朗日量的一般表达式；针对全对称无质量、有质量、部分无质量及连续自旋场，分别建立了约束与非约束两种BRST-BV表述；证明了所得BRST-BV拉格朗日量与基于修正de Donder散度的度规类拉格朗日量之间的匹配性；在包含场与反场的扩展空间中实现了AdS空间对称性的具体表示。

Conclusion: 所发展的基于庞加莱参数化的BRST-BV方法能够统一且系统地处理AdS空间中各种类型自由场的规范对称性与动力学，约束与非约束表述的建立以及对称性在场-反场空间中的实现为该形式体系的进一步推广（如相互作用）奠定了基础。

Abstract: We use the Poincare parametrization of AdS space to develop a general BRST-BV approach for free fields. A general expression for the BRST-BV Lagrangian of fields with arbitrary masses and symmetry types is obtained. We apply this general framework to study totally symmetric massless, massive, and partially-massless fields with arbitrary integer spin and a continuous-spin field. For these fields, both the constrained and unconstrained BRST-BV formulations are developed. In addition, we demonstrate the matching between the obtained BRST-BV Lagrangian and the metric-like Lagrangian formulated in terms of the modified de Donder divergence. Finally, a realization of AdS space symmetries is obtained within the space of fields and antifields entering the BRST-BV formulation.

</details>

### [123] [Secondary Production of Photons from ALP Dark Matter interacting with a Cosmological Magnetic Field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01399)
*Abdias Aires,Robert Brandenberger,Ashu Kushwaha*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文研究在暗物质为相干振荡赝标量场（pseudoscalar field）并经由Chern-Simons项与电磁场耦合的假设下，暗物质涨落与预先存在的磁场相互作用所产生的次级光子。分析适用于重组时期存在的任意宇宙学尺度磁场涨落谱，并表明在Lyman-Werner频段获得足够大的光子通量与CMB及X射线观测约束一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索暗物质作为相干振荡赝标量场与电磁场耦合的次级光子产生机制，并检验其在Lyman-Werner频段产生的光子通量是否与现有天文观测（CMB和X射线）约束兼容。

Method: 假设暗物质通过Chern-Simns项与电磁场耦合；考虑磁场自身的频谱分布，将形式化框架应用于之前由同一耦合机制经参量共振不稳定性（parametric resonance instability）产生的大尺度磁场情形，并推广至任意宇宙学尺度磁场涨落谱。

Result: 在Lyman-Werner频率范围内能够获得足够大的次级光子通量，且该结果不违反CMB与X射线的观测约束。

Conclusion: 所提出的暗物质-磁场耦合机制可以在满足现有观测限制的条件下，在Lyman-Werner波段产生可观测的次级光子信号。

Abstract: Under the assumption that dark matter is a coherently oscillating pseudoscalar field coupled to electromagnetism by the usual Chern-Simons term, we study the production of secondary photons from dark matter fluctuations coupled to a pre-existing magnetic field, taking into account the spectral distribution of the magnetic field. Specifically, we apply the formalism to the case of a large-scale magnetic field generated previously via a parametric resonance instability due to the same Chern-Simons coupling. However, our analysis is applicable to any spectrum of cosmological scale magnetic field fluctuations present at the time of recombination. We show that obtaining a sufficiently large flux of photons in the Lyman-Werner frequency range is consistent with constraints from CMB and X-ray observations.

</details>


### [124] [Gravitational Waves from Primordial Black Holes: Connecting Low-Frequency Scalar-Induced Signatures to High-Frequency Binary Mergers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01818)
*Ashu Kushwaha*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文针对单色原初黑洞（primordial black hole, PBH）质量函数，建立了一种模型无关的理论框架，将低频标量诱导引力波（scalar-induced GW, SIGW）与高频PBH双星并合引力波信号联系起来，并发现两信号峰值频率之间存在普适关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 原初黑洞的形成需显著增强的曲率扰动，这种机制会同时产生低频SIGW随机背景与高频PBH双星并合引力波信号。现有研究通常分别处理这两种信号，缺乏统一的框架来建立两者间的定量联系。

Method: 基于单色PBH质量函数，利用PBH丰度对原初曲率功率谱的约束，分别计算球对称坍缩与椭球坍缩模型下的SIGW背景；同时分析PBH双星并合的引力波信号，推导双星最内稳定圆轨道（innermost stable circular orbit, ISCO）频率与SIGW频率之间的直接对应关系，并进一步建立完整并合引力波谱峰值频率与ISCO频率之间的普适比例关系。

Result: 椭球坍缩模型产生的SIGW信号显著强于球对称坍缩模型；完整并合引力波谱的峰值频率与ISCO频率满足$f_{\text{peak}} = 1.79 \, f_{\text{ISCO}}$，该关系与双星质量无关。

Conclusion: 该统一框架将两种不同频段的引力波通道联系起来，使得相同的原初扰动能够在跨度很大的不同频带上被探测与检验。

Abstract: Formation of primordial black holes (PBHs) requires a significant enhancement of curvature perturbations. This mechanism leaves a twofold gravitational-wave (GW) signature: a \emph{low-frequency} stochastic background of scalar-induced GWs (SIGWs) and a distinct \emph{high-frequency} signal from subsequent PBH binary mergers. We leverage this shared origin to establish a consistent, \emph{model-independent} connection between these two observables for a monochromatic PBH mass function. Using PBH abundance constraints on the primordial curvature power spectrum, we evaluate the stochastic SIGW background for spherical and ellipsoidal collapse models, demonstrating that the ellipsoidal scenario yields a significantly stronger signal. Furthermore, we analyze the GW signal from PBH binary mergers and find a direct correspondence between the SIGW frequency and the innermost stable circular orbit (ISCO) frequency of the binaries. Because GW emission is nearly maximal near the ISCO, we additionally show that the peak of the full merger GW spectrum relates to the ISCO frequency via $f_{\text{peak}} = 1.79 \, f_{\text{ISCO}}$, a relation that is independent of the binary masses. Remarkably, this unified framework connects these distinct GW channels, enabling the same primordial fluctuations to be probed across widely separated frequency bands.

Abstract: We construct an exhaustive family of constant spacetime mean curvature (STCMC) surfaces for initial data sets close to the anti-de Sitter-Schwarzschild hyperboloid. Funct. Anal., 2009). As an application, inspired by the definition of STCMC center of mass for initial data sets proposed in the asymptotically Euclidean setting by Cederbaum-Sakovich (Calc. Var. PDE, 2021), we study the center of mass of an asymptotically hyperboloidal initial data set.

### [126] [Feigin-Semikhatov duality at the critical level](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02155)
*Thomas Creutzig,Xuanzhong Dai,Bailin Song*

Main category: math.RT

TL;DR: 本文在临界/大水平极限下研究 Feigin-Semikhatov 对偶性，证明了次正则 W-代数（subregular W-algebra）与主 W-超代数（principal W-superalgebra）在大水平极限下的结构等价关系，并建立了相应的范畴等价。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Feigin-Semikhatov 对偶性断言两类顶点代数（vertex algebras）之间存在对偶关系，本文旨在临界/大水平极限（critical/large level limit）下深入刻画这一对偶的结构。

Method: 将无中心（centerless）的临界水平次正则 W-代数描述为大水平极限主 W-超代数与格点顶点代数（lattice VOA）的轨形（orbifold）构造，并由此建立两类顶点代数之间某些范畴的函子（functor）。

Result: 证明在该设定下可实现分块（block-wise）的范畴等价；通过对主 W-超代数大水平极限的主块（principal block）的分析，揭示了次正则 W-代数在权模（weight modules）范畴中的主块结构，该范畴远大于常见的下界模（lower bounded modules）范畴。

Conclusion: 临界/大水平极限为 Feigin-Semikhatov 对偶性提供了清晰的范畴等价框架，并拓展了对次正则 W-代数表示理论的理解。

Abstract: The Feigin-Semikhatov duality asserts that the Heisenberg cosets of the subregular $W$-algebra of $\mathfrak{sl}_n$ at level $k$ and the one of the principal $W$-superalgebra of $\mathfrak{sl}_{n|1}$ at level $\ell$ coincide when the levels satisfy the Feigin-Frenkel relation $(k+n)(\ell+n-1)=1$. A similar duality holds between the subregular $W$-algebra of $\mathfrak{so}_{2n+1}$ and the principal $W$-superalgebra of $\mathfrak{osp}_{2|2n}$.
  We study these dualities in the critical/large level limit.
  We describe the centerless subregular $W$-algebra at the critical level as an orbifold of the large level limit of the principal $W$-superalgebra times a lattice VOA. Our construction yields a functor between certain categories of the two involved vertex algebras. We show that in this set-up one in fact gets block-wise equivalences of categories. Studying the principal block of the large level limit of the principal $W$-superalgebra then gives us the structure of the principal blocks of the subregular $W$-algebras in the category of weight modules (which is much larger than the more common category of lower bounded modules).

### [127] [From orthoposets to orthomodular posets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01259)
*John Harding,Gejza Jenda,Bert Lindenhovius*

Main category: math.CO

TL;DR: 本文证明了正交模偏序集（orthomodular posets）范畴是强正交偏序集（strong orthoposets）范畴的一个全余反射子范畴（full coreflective subcategory），并构造了一个核心反射子（coreflector），该核心反射子进一步限制为正交格（ortholattices）范畴到正交模偏序集范畴的一个函子（functor），且该函子是右伴随（right adjoint）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 建立正交模偏序集（orthomodular posets）与强正交偏序集（strong orthoposets）之间的范畴论关系，揭示正交模偏序集在更广泛的强正交偏序集结构中作为余反射子范畴的结构位置。

Method: 从一个强正交偏序集 $P$ 出发，保持其底层集合（underlying set）和正交补（orthocomplementation）不变，但修改其偏序关系（order），从而构造出一个具有相同底层集合的正交模偏序集。由此得到全余反射子（full coreflector）的构造。

Result: 正交模偏序集范畴是强正交偏序集（即任意两个正交元素都存在并（join）的正交偏序集）范畴的一个全余反射子范畴。该核心反射子限制在正交格（ortholattices）范畴到正交模偏序集范畴上仍为一个函子，且该函子是右伴随。

Conclusion: 本文揭示了正交模偏序集（orthomodular posets）在强正交偏序集（strong orthoposets）范畴中的精确范畴论位置，并建立了从正交格（ortholattices）到正交模偏序集的右伴随函子，丰富了相关结构的范畴论性质。

Abstract: We show that the category of orthomodular posets is a full coreflective subcategory of the category of strong orthoposets, those orthoposets in which any two orthogonal elements have a join. This coreflection is obtained by building from a strong orthoposet $P$, an orthomodular poset with the same underlying set and same orthocomplementation as $P$, but with modified order. This coreflector restricts to a functor from the category of ortholattices to the category of orthomodular posets, and this functor is right adjoint.

</details>


### [128] [Double-scaled SYK from boundary metrics of planar maps](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01995)
*Timothy Budd*

Main category: math.CO

TL;DR: 本文研究了一类具有特殊q-变形面权重的二分平面地图（bipartite planar map）的计数问题。作者证明，当边界度量由测地弦图（geodesic chord diagram）编码时，计数结果仅依赖于弦图的交叉数（crossing number），并且该弦图的诱导分布与双标度Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev模型（DSSYK）的弦图表示完全一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 带边界度量约束的平面地图枚举通常是一个困难问题，该研究试图寻找一类可解的特例，以简化这一计数问题。

Method: 研究聚焦于一类来自物理背景（DSSYK模型）的二分平面地图模型，该模型具有特殊的q-变形面权重（q-deformed face weights）。通过引入测地弦图来编码平面地图的边界度量，并分析弦图交叉数与加权计数之间的关系。

Result: 证明对于这类模型，加权枚举结果仅取决于弦图的交叉数；在固定周长条件下，测地弦图的诱导分布与DSSYK模型中的弦图表示完全一致。

Conclusion: 该工作发现了一类边界度量可控的二分平面地图模型，其计数具有简洁的显式形式，并建立了与DSSYK模型之间的精确对应关系。

Abstract: The enumeration of planar maps with control on the boundary metric, i.e. the pseudometric induced on the outer face of the map by its bulk graph distance metric, is a difficult problem in general. However, we show that for a family of bipartite planar map models with special q-deformed face weights that arise in the physics context of the double-scaled Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev model (DSSYK) the enumeration admits a very simple answer. Encoding the boundary metric of a bipartite planar map by its so-called geodesic chord diagram, we prove that the weighted enumeration depends only on the crossing number of the chord diagram. At fixed perimeter, the induced law of the geodesic chord diagram in these planar map models coincides exactly with the chord diagram representation of the DSSYK model.

</details>

# physics.geo-ph [[Back]](#toc)

### [129] [How effective normal stress oscillations advance failure in fault gouge: frequency dependence, non-failure window, and the role of dilation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01448)
*Pritom Sarma,Einat Aharonov,Renaud Toussaint,Stanislav Parez*

Main category: physics.geo-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过耦合离散元-流体动力学数值模拟，研究了流体饱和或干燥断层泥充填断层在有效正应力振荡（0.5–10000 Hz）下的响应。发现尽管加载条件低于Mohr-Coulomb阈值，断层在大多数频率下仍会发生破坏，且存在一个中间频率（30–200 Hz）的无破坏窗口，破坏由低频的剪切棘轮膨胀和高频的声学流化（acoustic fluidization）两种机制驱动，频率是颗粒材料破坏的关键控制参数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自然地震与工程地下系统中均会出现循环孔隙压力或正应力变化，但这些变化在颗粒尺度上对断层稳定性的影响尚不明确（poorly constrained at the grain scale）。

Method: 采用耦合离散元-流体动力学模型（coupled Discrete Element–fluid dynamics model），数值模拟剪切、流体饱和或干燥断层泥充填断层在宽频率范围（0.5–10000 Hz）的有效正应力振荡响应，通过循环孔隙压力或直接循环正应力实现有效正应力振荡，且保持应力状态低于连续加载下的Mohr-Coulomb阈值。

Result: 在亚临界（sub-critical）加载条件下，大多数频率下仍观察到破坏，且频率依赖性是非单调的；中间频率（30–200 Hz）出现明显的无破坏窗口，系统呈现从循环破坏-停滞到持续滑动的四个状态区间；孔隙压力振荡与正应力振荡产生相同的状态结构，验证了Terzaghi有效应力原理的等价性；流体耦合仅通过膨胀硬化（dilatant hardening）引入延迟。

Conclusion: 亚临界破坏源于膨胀引起的强度劣化（dilation-induced strength deterioration），低频和高频分别通过剪切棘轮膨胀和动态膨胀（声学流化）两种机制实现，中间无破坏窗口是这两种机制之间的间隙；频率是颗粒材料破坏的一个控制参数，对动态地震触发和循环注入方案具有启示意义。

Abstract: Cyclic pore-pressure or normal stress variations arise both in relation to natural earthquakes and in engineered subsurface systems, yet their effect on fault stability remains poorly constrained at the grain scale. Here we numerically model, using a coupled Discrete Element--fluid dynamics model, the response of a sheared, fluid-saturated or dry, gouge-filled fault to effective normal stress oscillations over a wide frequency range (0.5-10000 Hz). The effective normal stress is oscillated either by cycling the pore-pressure or by directly cycling the normal stress, while keeping the stress state below the Mohr-Coulomb threshold measured in continuous loading. Despite this sub-critical loading, we observe failure across most frequencies, with a non-monotonic frequency dependence. A distinct non-failure window emerges at intermediate frequencies (30-200 Hz), bounded by failure at both lower and higher frequencies; the system exhibits four regimes from cyclic failure-and-arrest to continuous sliding. Pore-pressure and normal stress oscillations produce the same regime structure, confirming that they act as equivalent forcings via Terzaghi's principle, with fluid coupling adding only a delay due to dilatant hardening. Sub-critical failure arises from dilation-induced strength deterioration via two mechanisms: (i) low-frequency cycles allow sufficient time for shear-driven ratcheting dilation, while (ii) high-frequency cycles induce dynamic dilation (acoustic fluidization) via amplified seepage forces, stress gradients and inertial forces. The intermediate non-failure window represents the gap between these mechanisms. These results identify frequency as a controlling parameter for failure in granular materials, with implications for dynamic earthquake triggering and cyclic injection protocols.

</details>

### [130] [Magneto-rotational instabilities in solids: application to neutron-star crusts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01505)
*Arthur G. Suvorov,Thomas Celora,Kostas D. Kokkotas*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文首次研究了固体中的磁旋转不稳定性（magneto-rotational instability, MRI），发现只有当流动剪切足够强、使得液态中的磁张力超过弹性空腔的剪切模量（shear modulus）时，磁场才能在固体中增长。在双中子星并合的动力学潮汐（dynamical tides）背景下，这意味着仅当恒星自转频率≥300 Hz时，地壳中的磁场才能在并合前被放大；若粘性加热在共振前弱化了晶体结构，所需自转频率可降低。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究广泛探讨了流体的微观物理因素（如分层和扩散率）对磁旋转不稳定性（MRI）的影响，但尚未考察该不稳定性是否能在固体中运作。行星或简并星内部的固态区域可能在生命周期的某些阶段与液态或气态层发生差速旋转，这促使作者分析弹性（elasticity）在多大程度上抑制了MRI。

Method: 采用简化的平面平行（plane-parallel）线性稳定性分析方法，比较因MRI产生的磁张力（magnetic tension）与弹性空腔的剪切模量，以确定固体中磁场增长的条件。

Result: 只有当流动剪切足够强、使得液态MRI产生的磁张力超过弹性空腔的剪切模量时，固体中才能发生磁场增长。在双中子星并合背景下，只有自转频率≥300 Hz的恒星，其地壳中的磁场才能在并合前被放大；若粘性加热在共振前弱化了晶体结构，所需自转频率可降低。

Conclusion: 固体中的MRI受到弹性抑制，需要强剪切流动才能恢复磁场增长。该结果为双中子星并合前地壳磁场的放大条件提供了定量约束。

Abstract: The magneto-rotational instability can generate strong, turbulent substructure within magnetised shear flows. The efficacy of the mechanism as a function of microphysical aspects of the fluid, such as stratification and diffusivity, has been explored extensively. One aspect that has not been studied thus far, however, is whether the instability can also operate in solids. Motivated by the possibility that solid regions within planets or degenerate stars may rotate differentially with respect to liquid or gaseous layers during some phase of their life, we examine the extent to which elasticity suppresses the instability. A simplified, plane-parallel analysis reveals that only in cases where the flow is strongly sheared, such that the magnetic tension that would result from the instability in a liquid exceeds the shear modulus of the elastic cavity, can magnetic growth occur. In the context of dynamical tides in binary neutron-star mergers, this implies that the magnetic field can be amplified in the crust prior to coalescence only if the star boasts a spin frequency of $\gtrsim 300$Hz. If viscous heating weakens the crystalline structure prior to resonance, the required spin frequency is reduced.

</details>


### [131] [Polarization Architecture of Steady GRMHD Jets from the Horizon to Infinity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01820)
*Zhenyu Zhang,Yehui Hou,Yu Song,Yosuke Mizuno,Bin Chen*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文建立了一个半解析框架（semi-analytic framework），用于高效生成从近水平区域到约10⁵倍引力半径（r_g）的稳态、轴对称GRMHD喷流的偏振图像，并揭示了一种新的尺度依赖的偏振诊断分离：在光子环（photon ring）外部，等离子体载荷通过惯性驱动的磁场缠绕改变偏振角轮廓；而在近水平区域，喷流收敛于由黑洞自旋（black hole spin）唯一控制的普适偏振模式，该收敛具有层级性，允许将不同物理效应解耦。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有GRMHD喷流偏振图像模拟计算成本高，难以在宽参数空间内高效探索重力和磁流体动力学（magnetohydrodynamic flows）在喷流形态和偏振上留下的尺度依赖特征。

Method: 开发了一个用于稳态、轴对称GRMHD喷流的半解析框架（semi-analytic framework），能够在从近水平区域到约10⁵ r_g的广域范围内高效生成高分辨率的偏振图像，从而快速扫描宽参数空间。

Result: 发现了尺度依赖的偏振诊断分离：光子环外，等离子体载荷通过惯性驱动的磁场缠绕显著改变喷流层的偏振角轮廓；在大像平面半径处，偏振角呈半径的幂律（power-law）关系，幂指数由喷流准直剖面决定；近水平区域，喷流收敛于仅由黑洞自旋控制的普适偏振模式，且收敛具有层级性——速度与磁场结构的差异先被抹除，准直相关的差异持续到更小半径。

Conclusion: 这些结果建立了一种几乎消色差（achromatic）的偏振诊断方法，将GRMHD喷流动力学与分辨图像结构联系起来，对高分辨率偏振测量以及约束黑洞自旋和喷流形成具有直接意义。

Abstract: We develop a semi-analytic framework for stationary, axisymmetric GRMHD jets that efficiently generates resolved polarized images from the near-horizon region out to $\sim 10^5\,r_g$ across a broad parameter space, enabling rapid exploration of how gravity and magnetohydrodynamic flows imprint scale-dependent signatures on jet morphology and polarization. We identify a new scale-dependent separation in polarimetric diagnostics. Outside the photon ring, plasma loading strongly modifies the polarization-angle profile of the integrated jet-layer emission through inertia-driven winding of the magnetic field. At large image-plane radii, the polarization angle follows a power-law in radius, with an index determined by the jet collimation profile. Near the horizon, in contrast, jets converge to a universal polarization pattern controlled solely by black hole spin. This convergence is hierarchical: differences in velocity and magnetic-field structure are erased first, whereas collimation-dependent differences persist to smaller radii, thereby allowing these effects to be disentangled. These results establish a largely achromatic polarimetric diagnostic that connects GRMHD jet dynamics to resolved image structure, with direct implications for high-resolution polarimetry and for constraining black hole spin and jet formation.

</details>


### [132] [Testing Gravity with Binary Pulsars in the SKA Era](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02064)
*V. Venkatraman Krishnan,L. Shao,V. Balakrishnan,A. Carleo,M. Colom i Bernadich,A. Corongiu,A. Deller,P. C. C. Freire,M. Geyer,E. Hackmann,H. Hu,Z. Hu,M. Kramer,J. Kunz,K. Liu,M. E. Lower,X. Miao,D. Perrodin,D. S. Pillay,A. Possenti,S. Ransom,I. Stairs,B. Stappers,The SKA Pulsar Science Working Group*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文综述了利用双（三）星射电脉冲星（binary/trinary radio pulsars）作为强场引力实验室的已有成果，并展望了平方公里阵列（SKA）望远镜将通过提升计时精度和发现新致密双星系统（如脉冲星-黑洞双星）来拓展广义相对论（GR）检验的能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 双（三）星射电脉冲星是强场引力（strong-field gravity）的天然实验室，目前已实现了强等效原理（strong equivalence principle）和引力辐射性质（radiative properties of gravity）等最精确的检验。但现有系统仍存在广义相对论（general relativity, GR）潜在偏离的探索空间，且亟需发现更多如脉冲星-黑洞双星（pulsar-black hole binaries）这类极端系统，以检验宇宙监督假设（cosmic censorship hypothesis）和“无毛”定理（no-hair theorem）。

Method: 通过SKA望远镜在南半球的高灵敏度（high sensitivity）来大幅提升再生脉冲星（recycled pulsars）的计时精度（timing precision），并在已知系统中深入搜寻GR的潜在偏离；同时通过银河系脉冲星普查（Galactic census）发现数十个新的相对论性脉冲星系统（relativistic pulsar systems），包括潜在的脉冲星-黑洞双星。

Result: SKA将显著提高计时精度，从而对已知双星系统开展更严格的GR检验；新发现的相对论性脉冲星系统（含可能的脉冲星-黑洞双星）将使宇宙监督假设和“无毛”定理的检验成为可能。可探索的引力方面包括强等效原理检验、引力偶极辐射（gravitational dipole radiation）、引力的额外场分量（extra field components）、引力磁效应（gravitomagnetism）及时空对称性（spacetime symmetries）。

Conclusion: 本章描述了利用双星脉冲星实现的各种引力检验类型，并概述了SKA为最佳地服务于这一科学目标所必须具备的特征和能力。

Abstract: Binary (and trinary) radio pulsars are natural laboratories in space for understanding gravity in the strong field regime, with many unique and precise tests carried out so far, including the most precise tests of the strong equivalence principle and of the radiative properties of gravity. The Square Kilometre Array (SKA) telescope, with its high sensitivity in the Southern Hemisphere, will vastly improve the timing precision of recycled pulsars, allowing for a deeper search of potential deviations from general relativity (GR) in currently known systems. A Galactic census of pulsars will, in addition, will yield the discovery of dozens of relativistic pulsar systems, including potentially pulsar -- black hole binaries, which can be used to test the cosmic censorship hypothesis and the ``no-hair'' theorem. Aspects of gravitation to be explored include tests of strong equivalence principles, gravitational dipole radiation, extra field components of gravitation, gravitomagnetism, and spacetime symmetries. In this chapter, we describe the kinds of gravity tests possible with binary pulsar and outline the features and abilities that SKA must possess to best contribute to this science.

</details>

### [133] [Fabrication of high-quality topological insulator nanodevices from bulk-insulating air-sensitive Sb-Bi$_2$Se$_3$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01439)
*Linh T. Dang,Ayushi Solanki,Yongjian Wang,Oliver Breunig,Yoichi Ando*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本论文研究了锑替代硒化铋（Sb-substituted Bi₂Se₃, SBS）这一非补偿拓扑绝缘体材料在微加工过程中的热工艺对输运性质的影响，并开发出一种室温制备工艺，成功保持了SBS的低体态载流子密度，观测到量子干涉振荡、大栅极可调性与弱反局域化（WAL）特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高质量拓扑绝缘体（topological insulator, TI）材料是实现TI-超导体混合体系中马约拉纳束缚态（Majorana bound states, MBSs）的关键。广泛使用的补偿型TI存在强无序和电荷不均匀性，可能损害马约拉纳器件性能。Sb替代硒化铋（SBS）因非补偿且具有极低体态载流子密度而成为有前景的候选材料，但其微加工过程中的热工艺影响尚需系统研究。

Method: 系统研究了微加工过程中热工艺（thermal processing）对SBS输运性质的影响，并开发了一种室温制备工艺（room-temperature fabrication protocol），用于制备霍尔条（Hall bar）和纳米线（nanowire）器件。

Result: 所开发的室温制备工艺成功保持了剥离SBS的低载流子密度，在纳米线中观测到量子干涉振荡（quantum interference oscillations）、较大的栅极可调性（large gate tunability）以及清晰的弱反局域化（weak antilocalization, WAL）特征。

Conclusion: 该室温制备工艺能够有效保留SBS的低体态载流子密度，表明SBS在拓扑绝缘体-超导体混合平台中具有应用潜力，有利于马约拉纳束缚态的实现与探测。

Abstract: High-quality topological insulator (TI) materials are essential for the realization and detection of Majorana bound states (MBSs) in TI-superconductor hybrid platforms. Widely used compensated TIs exhibit substantial disorder and charge inhomogeneity, which may be detrimental for Majorana devices. In this regard, Sb-substituted Bi$_2$Se$_3$ (SBS) is promising, because it is non-compensated and yet achieves very low bulk carrier density. We systematically investigate the impact of thermal processing during microfabrication on the transport properties of SBS. We developed a room-temperature fabrication protocol that preserves the low carrier density of exfoliated SBS upon fabrication of Hall bar and nanowire devices as evidenced from the observation of quantum interference oscillations in nanowires, a large gate tunability, and clear signatures of weak antilocalization (WAL).

### [134] [Resonant cooling of nuclear spins by optically-oriented holes in MAPbI$_3$ perovskite crystals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01441)
*Mladen Kotur,Dmitri R. Yakovlev,Nataliia E. Kopteva,Bekir Turedi,Maksym V. Kovalenko,Manfred Bayer*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 在MAPbI$_3$钙钛矿晶体中，通过光生自旋取向空穴实现了核自旋的共振冷却，并由Hanle效应测量在可变频率螺旋度调制激发下得以证实。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在MAPbI$_3$钙钛矿材料中利用光生载流子对核自旋进行冷却的可能性，以理解核自旋与载流子自旋之间的相互作用机制。

Method: 采用Hanle效应（Hanle effect）测量，在可变频率的螺旋度调制（helicity-modulated）激发条件下，通过分析核自旋共振位置随调制频率的变化以及Hanle曲线的形状来揭示冷却机制。

Result: 共振磁场位置随调制频率增加而向高场方向移动；Hanle曲线在面内旋转时保持不变，证实涉及自旋I=1/2的$^{207}$Pb核（无四极分裂）；共振特征形状表明核自旋由负g因子的载流子（即空穴）冷却；共振场位置超过弱局域空穴的Hanle曲线半宽，表明强局域空穴是核自旋冷却的主要载流子。

Conclusion: 在MAPbI$_3$钙钛矿中，光生自旋取向空穴能够有效实现核自旋的共振冷却，其中强局域空穴起主导作用，且$^{207}$Pb核因不具有四极分裂而成为主要冷却对象。

Abstract: Resonant cooling of nuclear spins by photogenerated spin-oriented holes is demonstrated for MAPbI$_3$ perovskite crystals. It is evidenced by Hanle-effect measurements under helicity-modulated excitation with variable frequency. The resonance position in magnetic field shifts toward higher fields with increasing modulation frequency. The invariance of the Hanle curve upon in-plane sample rotation is consistent with the involvement of $^{207}$Pb nuclei with spin $I = 1/2$, which do not exhibit quadrupolar splitting. The shape of the resonance feature in the Hanle curve reveals that the nuclear spins are cooled by carriers with a negative $g$-factor, consistent with holes. The resonance fields associated with the modulation frequencies exceed the half-width of the weakly localized hole contribution to the Hanle curve, indicating that strongly localized holes are the primary carriers responsible for the nuclear spin cooling.

### [135] [Quantum Heat Under the Microscope: A Perspective on Cryogenic Scanning Thermal Microscopy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01691)
*Valentin Fonck,Jean Spiece,Pascal Gehring*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文综述了低温（cryogenic）条件下局域热输运表征技术的现状与局限，提出发展低温扫描热显微镜（cryogenic Scanning Thermal Microscopy）的必要性，并通过五个案例研究展示该技术对理解奇异量子相（exotic quantum phases）和催生变革性技术的潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 低温热输运（thermal transport at cryogenic temperatures）研究既充满挑战也富有洞见，但目前尚无方法能在低温条件下实现纳米尺度的局域热输运成像。这一技术空白阻碍了对量子现象热对应物（thermal counterpart）的深入探索。

Method: 以Perspective（观点文章）形式，综述现有局域热输运表征技术的现状并指出其局限性。在此基础上，提出发展低温扫描热显微镜（cryogenic Scanning Thermal Microscopy）的动机，并通过五个案例研究论证该方法的潜在价值。

Result: 现有技术无法在低温条件下对纳米尺度局域热输运进行成像。五个案例研究表明，低温扫描热显微镜有望深化对维德曼-弗兰兹定律（Wiedemann-Franz law）破坏、声子量子化（quantisation of phonons）等量子相的理解，并推动变革性技术的出现。

Conclusion: 低温扫描热显微镜的发展将填补低温纳米热成像的技术空白，为探索奇异量子相的热性质及催生新技术提供有力工具。

Abstract: Exploring thermal transport at cryogenic temperatures presents both significant challenges and valuable insights. By uncovering the thermal counterpart of well-known quantum phenomena, researchers investigated fascinating phenomena ranging from the violation of the Wiedemann-Franz law to the quantisation of phonons. One key frontier remains : no existing method can image local heat transport at the nanoscale under cryogenic conditions. In this Perspective, we review the current state state of the art of local heat transport characterisation techniques and highlight their limitations. As a motivation for the development of cryogenic Scanning Thermal Microscopy, we provide five case studies illustrating how this approach could deepen our understanding of exotic quantum phases and enable the emergence of transformative technologies.

</details>


### [136] [An efficient formalism for inertial spin waves: Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya antiferromagnets as case studies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02021)
*De-Yun Zhao,Ri-Xing Wang,Meng-Qiu Cai,Mikhail Cherkasskii,Peng-Bin He*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文建立了一个系统性地描述惯性自旋波（inertial spin waves）手性（chirality）和偏振（polarization）的理论框架，通过椭圆率角（ellipticity angle）统一定义这些内禀性质，并系统研究了单轴反铁磁体（uniaxial antiferromagnets）中均匀与非均匀磁构型下的进动（precessional）和章动（nutational）自旋波模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管惯性自旋波作为新型磁激发受到广泛关注，但目前缺乏系统性地表征其手性和偏振等内禀性质的形式化方法，且其在空间非均匀磁构型中的行为尚未被充分探索。

Method: 通过椭圆率角这一统一参数（编码频率符号、相位差和椭圆轴比），建立惯性自旋波的计算框架及其手性与偏振的通用定义；并将其应用于具有交错（staggered）和均匀（homogeneous）Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya相互作用（DMI）的单轴反铁磁体，涵盖均匀共线、倾斜和螺旋磁构型。

Result: 小交错DMI保持自旋波简并性，而小均匀DMI则解除简并；倾斜和螺旋结构中的时空反演对称性破缺在整布里渊区内完全解除自旋波简并；长波章动模式表现为后向波，且在临界惯性弛豫时间附近出现平带（flat bands）；倾斜和螺旋构型中章动模式为左手性、进动模式为右手性；偏振在均匀构型中对波数不敏感，在非均匀构型中则呈现强色散关系。

Conclusion: 该工作推进了对磁惯性动力学的理解，并为超快磁子器件（ultrafast magnonic devices）的发展提供了理论依据。

Abstract: Magnetic inertia, emerging in the ultrafast regime, supports inertial spin waves (SWs) as novel magnetic excitations. Despite considerable efforts devoted to inertial SWs, a systematic formalism for fully characterizing their intrinsic properties, especially chirality and polarization, is still lacking, and inertial SWs in spatially nonuniform magnetic configurations remain poorly explored. Here, we develop a framework for calculating inertial SWs and establish a general definition of their chirality and polarization via the ellipticity angle, a unified parameter encoding frequency sign, phase difference, and elliptical axis ratio. Using this method, we systematically investigate precessional and nutational SWs in uniaxial antiferromagnets with staggered and homogeneous Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya interactions (DMIs), covering uniform collinear, canted, and spiral magnetic configurations. The results reveal that small staggered DMI preserves spin-wave degeneracy, whereas small homogeneous DMI lifts it. Further space-time inversion symmetry breaking in canted and spiral structures fully removes spin-wave degeneracy across the entire Brillouin zone. Long-wavelength nutational SWs behave as backward waves, and flat bands emerge in canted and spiral configurations near a critical inertial relaxation time. In canted and spiral configurations, nutational modes are always lefthanded whereas precessional modes are always righthanded; additionally, the dispersion spectra of the canted configuration can be derived from those of the spiral configuration via band folding. Polarization is wavenumber insensitive for uniform configurations but becomes strongly dispersive for nonuniform ones. This work advances the fundamental understanding of magnetic inertial dynamics and provides theoretical insights for the development of ultrafast magnonic devices.

Result: 透射率表现出强各向异性（strong anisotropy），特定入射方向出现显著抑制，暗示载流子的方向滤波（directional filtering）效应；磁势垒强度和宽度均可调谐电荷输运性质。

Abstract: We present a theoretical study of electron tunneling through a magnetic barrier in 8-Pmmn borophene, created by depositing two ferromagnetic strips on the borophene sheet. Using a low-energy effective Hamiltonian that captures the anisotropic Dirac spectrum, we solve the Dirac equation in three regions and impose wave-function continuity at the interfaces. From the resulting spinor solutions, we compute current densities and determine transmission and reflection probabilities as functions of incident energy, angle, and barrier parameters. The transmission exhibits strong anisotropy due to the tilted Dirac cones, with pronounced suppression for specific incident directions, suggesting directional filtering of carriers. We further calculate the conductance using the Landauer-Büttiker formalism, revealing that both magnetic strength and barrier width can tune the charge transport properties. The results demonstrate that engineered magnetic barriers in 8-Pmmn borophene enable precise control over electron flow, offering a platform for anisotropic transport control and tunable quantum devices. The interplay between the intrinsic anisotropy of borophene and external magnetic barriers provides rich opportunities to manipulate Dirac fermions in two-dimensional systems.

### [139] [Quantum-geometric shift of quasiequilibrium: Origin of nonreciprocal current driven by quantum-metric dipole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02100)
*Sota Kitamura,Takahiro Anan,Takahiro Morimoto*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过结合绝热微扰论（adiabatic perturbation theory）与非平衡格林函数方法（nonequilibrium Green function approach），建立了量子度规（quantum metric）起源的非线性直流电输运的完全量子力学框架，发现纵向非互易电流受量子度规偶极（quantum-metric dipole）调控，并指出其物理起源是偏置场下电子波包弛豫过程中的有限扩展所导致的偏移准平衡（shifted quasiequilibrium）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有量子度规输运理论多基于半经典处理，缺乏对分布函数量子修正的完整描述，且不同规范（如速度规范与长度规范）之间的形式联系尚不清晰，因此需要建立一个自洽的完全量子力学理论框架。

Method: 将绝热微扰论与非平衡格林函数方法相结合，在速度规范（velocity gauge）中直接处理直流电场，而非将其视为交流场的零频极限；由此构建的绝热基哈密顿量（adiabatic-basis Hamiltonian）与长度规范（length gauge）形式一致，便于不同表述间的系统性比较。

Result: 发现存在一个由量子度规偶极（quantum-metric dipole）调控的纵向非互易电流（longitudinal nonreciprocal current）。该电流的关键源于分布函数中的量子修正项，而这一修正项在半经典处理中是缺失的。

Conclusion: 将上述量子修正追溯至偏置场下电子波包弛豫过程中的有限空间扩展（finite spread of an electron wave packet），从而将偏移准平衡（shifted quasiequilibrium）确立为量子度规非互易输运（quantum-metric nonreciprocal transport）的物理起源。

Abstract: We study nonlinear DC electric transport of quantum-metric origin by combining adiabatic perturbation theory with the nonequilibrium Green function approach. The adiabatic ansatz provides a basis for directly treating a DC electric field in the velocity gauge, rather than introducing it as the zero-frequency limit of an AC field. The resulting adiabatic-basis Hamiltonian takes the same form as in the length gauge, enabling a systematic comparison across different formulations. Applying this fully quantum formulation, we find a longitudinal nonreciprocal current governed by the quantum-metric dipole. The essential ingredient is a quantum correction to the distribution function that is absent in semiclassical treatments. We trace this correction to the finite spread of an electron wave packet during relaxation under a bias field, thereby identifying shifted quasiequilibrium as the physical origin of quantum-metric nonreciprocal transport.

Result: 该伊辛机可在 341 ms 内找到 MAX-CUT 问题的近似解，且通过使用更高频率的延迟线有望将求解时间缩短至亚毫秒级。针对数字划分（number partitioning）和数独（Sudoku）问题也展示了求解能力。与最先进的相干伊辛机相比，热稳定性提升四个数量级；与模拟分岔算法（simulated bifurcation algorithm）相比，在 MAX-CUT 问题上表现相当，在更复杂的数字划分和数独问题上表现更优。

Conclusion: 基于微波固态延迟线的时间复用伊辛机在热稳定性、功耗、成本和桌面化方面具有显著优势，能够在多种组合优化问题上达到或超越现有方法的性能，具备良好的可扩展性。

Abstract: Optical coherent Ising machines based on time-multiplexing have demonstrated significant progress in terms of connectivity and spin scalability. However, they are constrained by large physical footprints, high power consumption, poor thermal stability, and high cost. Here, we present a time-multiplexed Ising machine leveraging propagating wave packets in solid-state delay lines at microwave frequencies, enabling thermally stable, robust, low-power, tabletop, and affordable design. We use two serially connected 20.5 MHz, 707 μs bulk acoustic wave delay lines supporting 2,048 spins. Our design provides all-to-all connectivity with 15-bit coupling resolution and finds approximate MAX-CUT solutions in 341 ms, potentially scalable to sub-ms by using higher frequency delay lines. Additionally, we demonstrate solutions to number partitioning and Sudoku problems. Compared with state-of-the-art Coherent Ising machines, our machine exhibits four orders of magnitude higher thermal stability. Against the simulated bifurcation algorithm, our design achieves comparable results on the MAX-CUT problem, while outperforming it on the more complex number-partitioning and Sudoku problems.

### [141] [Electrical transport in ultra-thin films: from Fuchs-Sondheimer to quantum-confinement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02120)
*Alessio Zaccone*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本篇综述讨论了超薄膜（ultra-thin films）中从经典尺寸效应到量子限域（quantum-confinement）电阻率机制的转变，重点介绍了新近提出的倒易空间限域理论（reciprocal-space confinement theory），该理论预测纳米尺度电阻率随厚度减小呈指数增长，并可与经典表面散射模型结合形成统一描述框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本文采用综述方法，讨论从经典散射到量子限域（quantum-confinement）的交叉过程；重点介绍倒易空间限域理论（reciprocal-space confinement theory），并探讨其与经典表面散射模型的结合方式，以建立统一的理论描述。

Result: 倒易空间限域理论预测，在纳米尺度下电阻率随厚度减小呈指数增长（exponential increase）；该理论可与经典表面散射模型组合，为超薄金属和半导体薄膜提供统一描述；同时已有近期实验证据支持这一理论图景。

Abstract: Ultra-thin films are fundamental components of modern nanoelectronics, where reducing thickness to the few-nanometer scale leads to a dramatic increase in electrical resistivity. For decades, this behavior has been interpreted in terms of classical size effects, primarily surface scattering within the Fuchs--Sondheimer theory and grain-boundary scattering in the Mayadas--Shatzkes model. While these approaches successfully describe transport when the film thickness is comparable to the electronic mean free path, growing experimental evidence indicates that they become insufficient under extreme confinement. This review discusses the crossover from classical scattering to a quantum-confinement regime in which the electronic states available for transport are fundamentally restructured by finite size. We review the recently proposed reciprocal-space confinement theory, which predicts an exponential increase of resistivity with decreasing thickness at the nanoscale, and discuss how it can be combined with classical surface-scattering models to provide a unified description of ultra-thin metallic and semiconducting films. Finally, we summarize recent experimental evidence supporting this picture and discuss its implications for future nanoelectronic devices, nanoscale interconnects, and quantum transport under extreme spatial confinement.

*Eran Sela,Mitali Banerjee*

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于干涉仪中嵌入反点（antidot）的方案，通过非局域电荷测量提取分数量子霍尔态中非阿贝尔任意子（non-Abelian anyons）的特征熵 \( \Delta S = k_B \log d \)，其中量子维度 \( d = \sqrt{2} \) 对应 \( \nu = 5/2 \) 态，该方案适用于中间温度范围。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出将反点嵌入干涉仪（interferometer）的方案，通过观测干涉相位的时间依赖性开关（time-dependent switching）来推断电荷；这种非局域电荷测量在平衡条件下进行。

Conclusion: 所提出的干涉仪嵌入反点方案能够通过非局域平衡电荷测量，在合适的温度窗口内有效提取非阿贝尔任意子的特征熵，从而为探测非阿贝尔任意子统计性质提供可行的实验途径。

Abstract: Non-Abelian anyons emerging in fractional quantum Hall states carry a characteristic entropy, $ΔS = k_B \log d$, where \(d\) is the anyon's quantum dimension. This \(\mathcal{O}(1)\) entropy can, in principle, be extracted from charge measurements of an antidot via Maxwell relations. However, equilibrium charge measurements in fractional antidots have proven to be challenging with conventional charge detectors. Here, we propose a scheme based on an antidot embedded in an interferometer, in which the charge can be inferred from the recently observed time-dependent switching of the interference phase. Performing such non-local charge measurements at equilibrium, the characteristic \(\mathcal{O}(1)\) entropy of non-Abelian anyons (e.g., $d = \sqrt{2}$ for the $ν= 5/2$ state) can be extracted for intermediate temperatures, which exceed the level spacing of the interferometer edge, but are much smaller than the level spacing of the antidot.

Motivation: 理解耦合自旋子极化激元网络中的粒子流与自旋流行为，特别是在封闭几何结构中自旋守恒隧穿与TE-TM效应诱导的自旋翻转隧穿共同作用下的复杂电流模式，以及如何利用这些电流作为平衡相（equilibrium phases）的直接诊断工具。

Method: 采用能量最小化方法获得稳态构型，对最小几何结构（等边三角形和正方形）推导出边缘分辨流的解析表达式；通过参量平面划分分析粒子流、面内自旋流（in-plane spin current）与面外自旋流（out-of-plane spin current）的分布；对更大环状结构，利用绕数与分支不变公共相位相干度组织相结构。

Result: 封闭几何中自旋守恒隧穿与TE-TM自旋翻转隧穿的结合产生了环流粒子流、隐藏自旋反向流和键相关自旋流模式；粒子流与自旋流可有效划分参量平面并提供平衡相的直接特征；在更大环状结构中，绕数与公共相位相干度指标共同组织相结构。

Conclusion: 电流分辨诊断方法（current-resolved diagnostics）可用于表征耦合自旋子极化激元网络中的平衡相，并推广至更复杂的多边形环结构。

Abstract: We analyze particle and spin currents in networks of coupled spinor exciton-polariton condensates arranged as plaquettes and regular polygonal rings. In closed geometries, spin-conserving and TE-TM-induced spin-flip tunnelling combine to generate circulating particle currents, hidden spin counterflows, and bond-dependent spin-current patterns. For the minimal geometries - an equilateral triangle, and a square plaquette - we derive analytical expressions for edge-resolved currents from stationary configurations obtained by energy minimization. We then show how particle, in-plane spin, and out-of-plane spin currents partition the parameter plane and provide direct signatures of the equilibrium phases. Finally, we apply the same current-resolved diagnostics to larger rings, where winding numbers and a branch-invariant common-phase coherence metric organize the resulting phase structure.

</details>


### [144] [Coupled Spin-Orbital $p$-Wave Magnetism via Structural and Magnetic Chirality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02378)

Method: 通过理论分析，证明自旋-轨道耦合使手性晶体的轨道极化对p波自旋劈裂产生额外贡献；由此定义相对手性η=χ_c χ_m作为分类序参量，将自旋-轨道态划分为同手性和异手性两种对称性不同的p波相。

Conclusion: 相对手性（relative chirality）被确立为一个实验可观测的对称性自由度，为手性磁系统（chiral magnetic systems）中的物态分类和输运探测提供了新框架。

Abstract: Helical spin textures represent the minimal realization of $p$-wave magnetism which is characterized by momentum-odd spin polarization. Independently, structurally chiral crystals exhibit momentum-odd orbital polarization arising from broken inversion symmetry. Here, we demonstrate that spin-orbit coupling couples these two independent microscopic chirality degrees of freedom, allowing the orbital polarization of a chiral crystal to generate an additional contribution to the $p$-wave spin splitting. The resulting spin-orbital state is naturally classified by the relative chirality $η=χ_{\mathrm c}χ_{\mathrm m}$, giving rise to two symmetry-distinct $p$-wave phases corresponding to homochiral and heterochiral configurations which can be directly probed by the longitudinal conductivity. These phases exhibit distinct transport signatures, establishing relative chirality as an experimentally accessible symmetry degree of freedom in chiral magnetic systems.

Focusing on the intrinsic orbital Hall effect in the dc limit under a spatially nonuniform electric field, we show that its conductivity can be expressed in terms of universal geometric quantities, such as the orbital Berry curvature and quantum metric. This formulation provides a term-by-term correspondence with the geometric description of intrinsic charge Hall transport established in previous studies. Using a tight-binding model, we further illustrate that the higher-order orbital Hall response can exhibit enhanced sensitivity to the orientation of an anisotropic sample. Our work deepens the understanding of diverse intrinsic transverse transport phenomena and the role of quantum geometry in electronic systems.

### [147] [Logarithmic negativity typically equals exact entanglement cost](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01320)
*Bowen Ouyang,Jonah Kudler-Flam*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 纠缠（entanglement）在现代物理中占有核心地位，但大型量子系统中缺乏计算高效的纠缠量化算法，使得操作上有意义的纠缠度量难以评估。

Method: 通过分析大型随机诱导混合态（random induced mixed states），证明对数负性（logarithmic negativity）这一可高效计算的纠缠度量，在一般情况下与正部分转置保持（positive-partial-transpose-preserving, PPT-preserving）操作下的纠缠代价（entanglement cost）精确相等。

Result: 对数负性（logarithmic negativity）在一般多体态中可作为纠缠的精确刻画（exact characterization），为复杂量子系统中的纠缠量化提供了一条易于处理的计算路径。

Conclusion: 对数负性不仅是可高效计算的，而且获得了精确的操作性解释（operational interpretation），可以作为大型量子系统中纠缠度量的实用工具。

Abstract: Quantum entanglement plays a leading role in modern understanding of physical systems, from quantum phases of matter to quantum gravity. In quantum information theory, one seeks operationally meaningful quantifiers of entanglement, which for large quantum systems are notoriously difficult to evaluate due to the lack of computationally efficient algorithms. In this Letter, we show that for large random induced mixed states the logarithmic negativity, an efficiently computable entanglement measure, generically coincides with the exact entanglement cost under positive-partial-transpose-preserving operations, thereby acquiring a precise operational interpretation. Our results establish logarithmic negativity as an exact characterization of entanglement in generic many-body states and provide a tractable route for quantifying entanglement in complex quantum systems.

### [148] [Quantum Noncommutativity Uniquely Determines Relative Entropy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01712)
*Gilad Gour*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明，在所有可加的（additive）态区分度度量中，唯一满足单次量子区分（single-shot quantum discrimination）最优测量所揭示赔率（odds）的度量是Umegaki相对熵（Umegaki relative entropy），从而将量子相对熵从渐近量确立为单次场景下的唯一可加区分度度量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子相对熵（quantum relative entropy）是物理学中的核心概念，但数据-处理不等式（data-processing inequality）允许存在无数种替代的散度度量（divergence measures）。作者旨在寻找一个更尖锐的操作性原理，以唯一确定量子相对熵，从而解释其在众多散度度量中的特殊地位。

Method: 通过二元猜测游戏（binary guessing games）来评估区分度，在该游戏中观察者使用最优测量（optimal measurement）区分一对量子态。作者证明，任何满足可加性（additivity）且尊重这些最优测量所揭示赔率的度量，必须等同于Umegaki相对熵。

Result: 该结果是精确的（exact），既不需要无穷多副本的热力学极限（thermodynamic limit），也不需要对关联态（correlated states）的超可加性（super-additivity）假设。这一刚性（rigidity）是纯粹的量子现象：经典理论允许包括Rényi散度（Rényi divergences）在内的连续族散度度量，而量子非对易性（quantum noncommutativity）消除了这种数学自由度。

Conclusion: 量子相对熵不仅是渐近量（asymptotic quantity），而且是唯一与单次量子区分兼容的可加区分度度量。该结果将量子相对熵置于更牢固的操作性基础之上。

Abstract: Quantum relative entropy is a core concept in physics, governing the limits of communication, thermodynamic irreversibility and quantum resource conversion. However, the requirement that physical processes cannot increase state distinguishability, the data-processing inequality, permits an infinite family of alternative divergence measures. Here we show that quantum relative entropy is uniquely selected by a sharper operational principle. We evaluate distinguishability through binary guessing games, in which an observer discriminates between pairs of quantum states using the optimal measurement. We prove that any additive measure that respects the odds revealed by these optimal measurements must coincide with the Umegaki relative entropy. This rigidity is a purely quantum phenomenon. Whereas classical theory permits a continuous family of valid divergence measures, including Rényi divergences, quantum noncommutativity. collapses this mathematical freedom. The result is exact, requiring neither a thermodynamic limit of infinitely many copies nor super-additivity assumptions for correlated states. It establishes quantum relative entropy not merely as an asymptotic quantity, but as the unique additive distinguishability measure compatible with single-shot quantum discrimination.

</details>


### [149] [Coherent states in minimal-length Quantum Mechanics: inequivalent characterizations and emergent squeezing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01393)
*Giuseppe Gaetano Luciano,Pasquale Bosso,Daniel Chemisana*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文对最小长度量子力学（minimal-length quantum mechanics）中一维谐振子的相干态（coherent states）进行了系统分析，揭示了广义不确定原理（GUP）框架下相干态三种标准表征之间的等价性被破坏，并研究了由此导致的动力学与半经典后果，包括相空间轨迹的非平凡形变和内在压缩机制（intrinsic squeezing mechanism），为GUP量子理论中的相干性建立了统一框架，并识别了最小长度物理的独特半经典信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本文对一维谐振子的相干态进行了系统分析，分别考察了其标准表征——湮灭算符（annihilation operator）本征态、位移真空态（displaced vacuum state）和最小不确定波包（minimum-uncertainty wave packet）。通过比较广义相干态与饱和GUP态的演化，研究了最小长度效应导致的动力学和半经典差异。

Result: 研究发现，在存在最小长度的情况下，相干态三种标准表征之间的正则等价性（canonical equivalence）被破坏。最小长度效应导致了相空间轨迹（phase-space trajectories）的非平凡形变，并产生了一种在普通量子力学中没有对应物的内在压缩机制。

Conclusion: 本文为基于GUP的量子理论中的相干性建立了统一框架，并识别了最小长度物理的独特半经典信号，为探测量子引力效应开辟了新途径。

Abstract: Several approaches to quantum gravity suggest the emergence of a fundamental minimal length at the Planck scale. In quantum mechanics, this feature is naturally encoded through deformations of the Heisenberg algebra, leading to the Generalized Uncertainty Principle (GUP). While the phenomenological implications of GUP have been extensively explored, a consistent characterization of coherent states in minimal-length quantum mechanics remains elusive. In this work, we present a systematic analysis of coherent states for the one-dimensional harmonic oscillator. We show that the canonical equivalence among their standard characterizations - as eigenstates of the annihilation operator, displaced vacuum states and minimum-uncertainty wave packets - is generically lost in the presence of a minimal length. We then investigate the dynamical and semiclassical consequences of this inequivalence by comparing the evolution of generalized coherent states with that of states saturating the GUP. In particular, we demonstrate that minimal-length effects induce nontrivial deformations of phase-space trajectories and give rise to an intrinsic squeezing mechanism with no counterpart in ordinary quantum mechanics. These results establish a unified framework for coherence in GUP-based quantum theories and identify distinctive semiclassical signatures of minimal-length physics, opening a new avenue for probing quantum-gravitational effects.

### [150] [Bockstein braiding statistics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02280)
*Po-Shen Hsin,Yu-An Chen*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文在辫子统计（braiding statistics）的框架下，识别了相邻情形（adjacent case）$p+q=d-1$ 下新型的互统计（mutual statistics），称为 Bockstein 辫子统计（Bockstein braiding statistics），并通过场论中的 Bockstein 上同调运算进行描述，揭示了其对对称性凝聚与对称性分数量化（symmetry fractionalization）的约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 通常的辫子统计要求 $p+q=d-2$，但对于相邻情形 $p+q=d-1$ 下的互统计尚未被系统研究。本文旨在填补这一空白，识别并刻画这类新型统计行为。

Method: 采用场论方法，将 $\mathbb Z_N$ 激发耦合到背景场 $A_{d-p}$ 和 $B_{d-q}$，利用 Bockstein 运算 $\beta_N$ 构造互统计的场论描述 $(2πi/N)\int A_{d-p}\cupβ_N B_{d-q}$。同时构造局域创建算符 $X$ 和 $Y$，通过闭幺正过程 $W_N(X,Y)$ 测量统计效应。

Result: 新统计在 $1$ 维空间产生粒子-粒子统计，$2$ 维空间产生粒子-环统计，$3$ 维空间产生环-环或粒子-膜统计。非平凡的 Bockstein 辫子统计会阻碍两个 $\mathbb Z_N$ 激发同时凝聚，排除对应的混合反常（mixed anomaly）系统中完全对称的有能隙相，并在其中一个 $\mathbb Z_N$ 对称性破缺时导致对称性分数量化。

Conclusion: Bockstein 辫子统计是相邻维度激发间的新型互统计，扩展了辫子统计的适用范围，并对拓扑相的分类和对称性实现有重要约束意义。

Abstract: Braiding statistics, from the Aharonov-Bohm phase to anyons in fractional quantum Hall systems, play a central role in quantum physics. For $p$- and $q$-dimensional excitations in $d$ spatial dimensions, ordinary braiding requires $p+q=d-2$. In a field-theoretic description of $\mathbb Z_N$ excitations, ordinary braiding is described by the linking response $(2πi/N)\int A_{d-p}\cup B_{d-q}$, where $A_{d-p}$ and $B_{d-q}$ are background fields coupled to the two excitation types. In this work, we identify new mutual statistics in the adjacent case $p+q=d-1$. For two invertible excitations obeying $\mathbb Z_N$ fusion, one can choose local creation operators $X$ and $Y$ whose supports have a staggered one-dimensional overlap. The closed unitary process $W_N(X,Y)=(Y^{-1}X^{-1})^N(YX)^N$ measures the resulting mutual statistic. Its field-theory description is $(2πi/N)\int A_{d-p}\cupβ_N B_{d-q}$, where $β_N$ is the Bockstein operation; we therefore call the invariant Bockstein braiding statistics. The construction yields particle-particle statistics in one dimension, particle-loop statistics in two dimensions, and loop-loop or particle-membrane statistics in three dimensions. Nontrivial Bockstein braiding statistics obstructs simultaneous condensation of the two $\mathbb Z_N$ excitations. It also rules out a fully symmetric gapped phase for systems with the corresponding mixed anomaly and implies symmetry fractionalization when one of the $\mathbb Z_N$ symmetries is broken.

</details>


### [151] [Lamb Shift of a Static Atom Facing a Rotating Surface](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01495)
*César D. Fosco,Fernando C. Lombardo,Francisco D. Mazzitelli*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了静态原子附近刚性旋转的平面体如何修正原子的兰姆移位（Lamb shift），推导了适用于任意轴对称平面材料的通用公式，并识别出轨道角动量和自旋角动量两个独立贡献，后者在旋转轴上仍然存在。旋转对石墨烯和金属表面的卡西米尔-波尔德相互作用（Casimir-Polder interaction）有增强作用，而对掺杂半导体则有减弱作用；超过阈值角速度时，原子能级会出现有限线宽，可作为量子摩擦（quantum friction）的光谱特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究当附近平面材料绕其法线刚性旋转时，静态原子的兰姆移位如何被修正，从而理解旋转运动对原子-表面相互作用的影响机制。

Method: 推导了基于多普勒频移（Doppler shift）的反射系数的兰姆移位通用公式，并将其展开到角速度Ω的二阶项，分离出轨道和自旋两个贡献。利用石墨烯片、有限厚度Drude导体、等离子体导体及掺杂半导体等模型进行示例计算。

Result: 轨道贡献正比于(Ωρ)²，局域复现了表面以切向速度Ωρ平移时的兰姆移位；自旋贡献正比于(aΩ)²，源于光子螺旋度（helicity）的旋转多普勒频移，且在旋转轴上仍存在。旋转增强石墨烯和金属表面的卡西米尔-波尔德相互作用，但削弱掺杂半导体的该相互作用，取决于载流子等离子体频率是否达到近场尺度1/a。

Conclusion: 超过阈值角速度时原子能级出现有限线宽，为量子摩擦提供了一种光谱学可探测的特征信号。

Abstract: We study how the Lamb shift of a static atom is modified when a nearby planar body rotates rigidly about its normal while the atom is held at a fixed distance $a$. We derive a general formula for the shift in terms of the angularly Doppler-shifted reflection coefficients of the surface, valid for any axially symmetric planar material. Expanding the result to second order in the angular velocity $Ω$, we identify two independent contributions associated with the orbital and spin components of the electromagnetic angular momentum. The orbital contribution, proportional to $(Ωρ)^2$, reproduces locally the Lamb shift induced by a surface translating at the tangential velocity $Ωρ$, whereas the spin contribution, proportional to $(aΩ)^2$, originates from the rotational Doppler shift of the photon helicity and survives even on the rotation axis. We first illustrate the formalism using a graphene sheet and then apply it to finite-thickness Drude and plasma conductors and to doped semiconductors. Rotation enhances the Casimir-Polder interaction for graphene and metallic surfaces, whereas it weakens it for doped semiconductors, depending on whether the carrier plasma frequency reaches the near-field scale $1/a$. Above a threshold angular velocity, the atomic level also acquires a finite linewidth, providing a spectroscopic signature of quantum friction.

</details>


### [152] [False vacuum decay in a two-dimensional quantum spin system](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01994)

Abstract: False vacuum decay describes the relaxation of a metastable state through the nucleation and growth of bubbles of the stable phase. Testing its predictions is particularly important in two or more spatial dimensions, where bubble nucleation acquires its true geometrical nature. Here, we study false vacuum decay in the quantum Ising model in two dimensions. Through tree tensor network simulations we extract the decay rate, the effective interface tension and the critical bubble size. ### [153] [A Quantum-Walk Representation of Color-Ordered MHV Scattering Amplitudes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02456)
*Anirudh Verma,C. M. Chandrashekar*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于图论的框架，利用置换树上的量子游走（quantum walks）来表示量子色动力学（QCD）中颜色排序的最大螺旋性违反（MHV）散射振幅。该框架将置换树、量子游走与开放量子系统（open quantum systems）统一起来，为量子算法模拟量子场论中的散射过程提供了基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在为量子色动力学中颜色排序的MHV散射振幅建立一种统一的、基于图的表示框架，从而连接置换树、量子游走与开放量子系统，为量子算法模拟量子场论散射过程提供理论基础。

Method: 采用图论框架，在置换树（permutation trees）上定义涂色量子游走（coined quantum walks），其中每条根到终端路径对应外部胶子的一种颜色排序，局部转移振幅根据Parke–Taylor振幅的旋量积结构（spinor-product structure）分配。引入基于Kraus算符的量子信道（quantum-channel）形式描述扇区分辨贡献，并在公共参考节点处使用加权收集算符（weighted collection operator）相干组合终端扇区。最后在硬币空间（coin space）上应用量子傅里叶变换（quantum Fourier transform），将编码的贡献组合成对应的颜色分解振幅。

Result: 以低点胶子振幅为例的数值结果表明，所提出的表示方法能够忠实捕捉Parke–Taylor结构的特征，并与解析结果一致。

Conclusion: 该框架统一了置换树、量子游走与开放量子系统，为量子算法模拟量子场论中的散射过程提供了可行的理论工具。

Abstract: We introduce a graph-theoretic framework for representing color-ordered maximally helicity violating (MHV) scattering amplitudes in quantum chromodynamics using coined quantum walks on permutation trees. Each root-to-terminal path corresponds to a distinct color ordering of the external gluons, while local transition amplitudes are assigned according to the spinor-product structure of the Parke--Taylor amplitudes. The walk evolves in coherent superpositions over permutation sectors, giving a dynamical picture of the underlying combinatorics. A quantum-channel formulation based on Kraus operators is also introduced to describe sector-resolved contributions, while a weighted collection operator coherently combines the terminal sectors at a common reference node. A quantum Fourier transform on the coin space is then employed to combine the encoded contributions into the corresponding color-decomposed amplitude. Together, these constructions establish a unified graph-based framework connecting permutation trees, quantum walks, and open quantum systems providing a framework for quantum algorithms to simulate scattering processes in quantum field theory. As an example, numerical results for low-point gluon amplitudes demonstrate that the proposed representation faithfully captures the characteristic Parke--Taylor structure and is consistent with analytical results.

*Reza Pirmoradian,Soheir Rouhani,M. Reza Tanhayi*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过图论（graph theory）形式化方法，研究伊辛自旋网络（Ising spin networks）中的可积-混沌转变（integrability-to-chaos transition）与信息置乱（information scrambling），建立了网络拓扑与信息论、算符和谱学诊断之间的统一框架，表明长程耦合与异质性度分布显著加速量子信息传播，并揭示约化的Thouless时间强关联于加速的信息与算符置乱。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索量子多体系统中可积性到混沌的转变以及信息置乱机制，特别是网络拓扑结构（如路径图、Erdős–Rényi和Watts–Strogatz拓扑）如何影响量子信息的传播与混沌行为。

Method: 将自旋建模为顶点，相互作用通过邻接矩阵（adjacency matrix）描述；哈密顿量（Hamiltonian）包含局域与归一化非局域相互作用，通过调节非局域耦合与场异质性驱动可积性破缺；采用二分互信息（bipartite mutual information）和三方信息（tripartite information）、out-of-time-order correlators（OTOCs）、Krylov复杂度、能级间距统计以及谱形因子（spectral form factor, SFF）等多种诊断工具量化置乱与混沌。

Result: 长程耦合与异质性度分布加速量子信息传播；增大非局域相互作用使三方信息趋近大幅负值，标志深度信息置乱；OTOC呈指数早期增长，量子Lyapunov指数随混沌区参数系统性变化；Krylov复杂度在混沌相中快速增长，与OTOC和互信息动力学同步；谱统计从Poissonian过渡到Wigner–Dyson分布；SFF呈现斜率-下降-斜坡-平台（slope-dip-ramp-plateau）结构，可提取Thouless时间与Heisenberg时间；约化的Thouless时间强关联于加速的信息与算符置乱。

Conclusion: 建立了网络拓扑与信息论、算符及谱学诊断之间的统一分析框架，为理解量子多体系统中的热化（thermalization）与非平衡动力学提供了深刻见解。

Abstract: We investigate the integrability-to-chaos transition and information scrambling in Ising spin networks via a graph-theoretic formulation. Modeling spins as vertices and interactions via adjacency matrices across path, Erdős--Rényi, and Watts--Strogatz topologies, we demonstrate that long-range couplings and heterogeneous degree distributions drastically accelerate quantum information propagation. The Hamiltonian comprises local and normalized non-local interactions; tuning the non-local coupling and field heterogeneity drives integrability breaking. To quantify scrambling, we employ bipartite mutual and tripartite information. Increasing non-local interactions drives tripartite information to large negative values, signaling deep information scrambling. Out-of-time-order correlators (OTOCs) exhibit exponential early-time growth, yielding quantum Lyapunov exponents that scale systematically with parameters governing the chaotic regime. Complementing this, Krylov complexity reveals rapid operator growth in the chaotic phase, synchronizing with OTOC and mutual information dynamics. Spectrally, the transition manifests as a shift from Poissonian to Wigner--Dyson level spacing statistics. The spectral form factor (SFF) exhibits the characteristic slope-dip-ramp-plateau structure, enabling the extraction of Thouless and Heisenberg times. Crucially, a reduced Thouless time strongly correlates with accelerated informational and operator scrambling. Ultimately, this work establishes a unified framework bridging network topology with information-theoretic, operator, and spectral diagnostics, offering profound insights into thermalization and non-equilibrium dynamics in quantum many-body systems.

### [155] [One-Body Purity, Non-Gaussianity, and Entanglement in Interacting Integrable Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01326)
*Rafał Świętek,Maksymilian Kliczkowski,Lev Vidmar,Marcos Rigol*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出，可积系统（integrable systems）本征态的纠缠与熵性质由多项式多个高斯态（Gaussian states）的随机叠加描述，而非可积系统（nonintegrable systems）则由指数多个高斯态的随机叠加描述，并通过单粒子纯度（one-body purity）、非高斯性（non-Gaussianity）和纠缠熵（entanglement entropy）的分析与数值结果加以验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 可积多体晶格哈密顿量的典型中间谱本征态表现出与不可积系统不同的纠缠行为，且其本征态虽非高斯态，却展现出类似高斯态的纠缠特征。现有范式（Haar随机费米子高斯态与Haar随机纯态）分别适用于可积与不可积系统，但缺乏统一解释可积系统中非高斯性缺失与纠缠行为之间关系的框架。

Method: 本文提出“随机叠加”模型，将可积系统本征态建模为多项式多个高斯态的随机叠加，将不可积系统本征态建模为指数多个高斯态的随机叠加。通过计算单粒子纯度、非高斯性和纠缠熵三个量，对比随机叠加模型与哈密顿量本征态的解析与数值结果，验证模型的适用性。

Result: 可积系统的本征态可由多项式多个高斯态的随机叠加有效描述，而非可积系统本征态则需指数多个高斯态的随机叠加。这一区别同时解释了可积系统中纠缠熵的行为特征和缺乏高斯性的现象。

Conclusion: 随机叠加高斯态模型成功统一了可积系统中“非高斯本征态却呈现高斯态纠缠特征”的表观矛盾，并为区分可积与不可积系统的纠缠结构提供了新范式。

Abstract: When describing entanglement in typical midspectrum eigenstates of many-body lattice Hamiltonians, two paradigms have emerged that capture the behavior observed in integrable and nonintegrable systems, Haar-random fermionic Gaussian states and Haar-random pure states, respectively. Remarkably, the former capture the behavior of interacting integrable systems, whose eigenstates are non-Gaussian. We argue that the paradigm that captures both the entanglement properties and the lack of Gaussianity in integrable systems is that of random superpositions of polynomially many Gaussian states. In contrast, eigenstates of nonintegrable systems are consistent with being described by random superpositions of exponentially many Gaussian states. We gain this understanding by comparing analytical and numerical results for the one-body purity, the non-Gaussianity, and the entanglement entropy of the random superpositions and the Hamiltonian eigenstates.

### [156] [Controlling Waiting Time Statistics in Monitored Collective Spins: Mitigating Detector's Resolution Barrier in Measurement-Induced Phase Transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01332)
*Tanbir Islam,Fernando Iemini*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究集体耗散自旋系统中，通过初始态不均匀性（initial-state inhomogeneities）控制量子跳变（quantum jump）的等待时间统计，从而缓解探测器有限时间分辨率（finite temporal resolution）问题；发现测量诱导相变（measurement-induced phase transition）在非均匀条件下仍可存活，但需权衡探测器分辨率与后选择（postselection）开销。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 集体耗散自旋系统中，后选择屏障（postselection barrier）可被部分缓解，但探测器的有限时间分辨率可能构成进一步障碍；本文旨在探索如何通过初始态不均匀性控制量子跳变的等待时间统计，从而克服探测器分辨率问题。

Method: 研究一个具有边界时间晶相（boundary time-crystalline phase）的集体监测自旋模型，通过将系统划分为旋转角度θ的两个子系统来引入不均匀性，分析等待时间统计和纠缠标度行为。

Result: 测量诱导相变在非均匀条件下仍然存活，并展现出不同的纠缠标度（entanglement scaling）区域；等待时间随θ增加而增长，标度为1/N，但前置因子（prefactor）被显著增强数个量级；在反平行极限（θ=π）下等待时间保持有限，完全解决了分辨率屏障。

Conclusion: 缓解探测器分辨率问题需付出代价：纠缠饱和时间（entanglement saturation time）显著变长，部分重新引入后选择屏障；结果揭示了探测器分辨率与后选择开销之间的权衡（trade-off），对测量诱导现象的实验观测具有直接意义。

Abstract: In collective dissipative spin systems, the postselection barrier can be partially mitigated; however, a further obstacle may be posed by the finite temporal resolution of detectors. In this work, we investigate how initial-state inhomogeneities can control waiting-time statistics between quantum jumps, thereby mitigating the detector-resolution problem. We consider a collectively monitored spin model with a boundary time-crystalline phase, introducing inhomogeneity by partitioning the ensemble into two subsystems rotated by an angle $θ$. We find that the measurement-induced phase transition survives under inhomogeneities, with different entanglement scaling regimes. The waiting time increases with $θ$, scaling as $1/N$ but with a prefactor strongly enhanced by orders of magnitude, and in the anti-aligned limit $θ= π$ it remains finite, fully resolving the resolution barrier. This mitigation, however, comes at a cost: the entanglement saturation time becomes significantly longer, partially reintroducing the postselection barrier. Our results highlight a trade-off between detector resolution and postselection overhead, with direct implications for the experimental observation of measurement-induced phenomena.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于边界时间晶体模型，通过集体耗散通道将时间晶体序播种到其他静态自旋系综上，沿量子轨迹分析纠缠动力学的时域演化以及稳态性质。

Conclusion: 耗散播种是开放多体系统中控制量子关联的一种有效机制，且该模型在实验上具有直接相关性，无需后选择壁垒（postselection barrier）。

Abstract: We investigate the entanglement dynamics along quantum trajectories during the seeding of time-crystalline order in a boundary time crystal (BTC). Specifically, how entanglement spreads among different spin ensembles when a BTC attempts to seed its time-crystalline behavior onto otherwise static spin ensembles, through a collective dissipative channel. We analyse both the dynamical growth of entanglement in time and the steady-state properties of the system. Our results reveal two fundamentally distinct regimes. In the seeded BTC phase, the steady-state entanglement entropy between the ensembles grows with system size $N$, accompanied by macroscopic fluctuations along the trajectories. In contrast, in the non-seeded static phase, both the steady-state entanglement and its fluctuations decay exponentially with $N$. The model thus features a measurement-induced phase transition (MIPT) driven by the seeding mechanism. Furthermore, these findings establish dissipative seeding as a powerful mechanism for controlling quantum correlations in open many-body systems, with direct experimental relevance to this class of model without a postselection barrier.

### [158] [Mechanistic Interpretability and Causal Feature Steering of Neural Quantum States via Sparse Autoencoders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01336)
*Zihao Qi,Christopher Earls*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过稀疏自编码器（sparse autoencoder）分析神经量子态（Neural Quantum States, NQS）的内部激活，发现无监督提取的特征与物理可观测量（如序参量、交错磁化强度等）高度相关，且对单个特征进行干预可平滑、单调地控制对应可观测量，揭示了NQS内部存在可解释的物理表示。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用稀疏自编码器（sparse autoencoder）从NQS的残差流（residual stream）中提取特征，并在基态表示和实时动力学两种场景下，分析这些特征与物理可观测量（包括序参量、交错磁化强度、半链关联函数）之间的相关性。

Result: 无监督提取的特征与物理可观测量之间存在强相关性；对单个特征进行训练后干预（post-training intervention）可平滑、单调地控制对应的可观测量，同时变分能量（variational energy）几乎保持不变。

Conclusion: NQS不仅仅是一种函数逼近器，其内部编码了丰富且可解释的物理信息表示。该方法为NQS提供了诊断和干预工具，为推动基于机制可解释性（mechanistic interpretability）构建更可靠、更透明的NQS奠定了基础。

Abstract: Neural Quantum States (NQS) are a remarkably expressive class of variational ansätze for quantum many-body wavefunctions, yet little is understood about their internal mechanisms: trained on variational objectives alone, how do NQS accurately capture physical observables that they have never been explicitly optimized for? In this work, we present a systematic approach to analyze the internal activations of NQS using sparse autoencoders. We extract features from the residual stream and demonstrate that these features strongly correlate with physical observables such as order parameters, staggered magnetization, and half-chain correlators, across both ground state representation and real-time dynamics. Remarkably, the discovery of these features is entirely unsupervised, with no physical labels provided. We further establish that such features causally affect the corresponding observables predicted by NQS, by showing that targeted, post-training intervention on a \textit{single} feature smoothly and monotonically steers the corresponding observable, while leaving the variational energy nearly unchanged. These results demonstrate that NQS are not merely functional approximators, but encode rich, interpretable internal representations of physical information. Our approach provides both a diagnostic and an intervention tool for NQS, and serves as a foundation for using mechanistic interpretability towards more reliable, transparent NQS.

### [159] [Shallow Unitary Circuits for Kramers-Wannier Dualities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01624)
*Yanting Cheng,Shang Liu*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文构建了对数深度（logarithmic depth）的空间非局域幺正电路，实现了$\mathbb{Z}_2$和$\mathbb{Z}_n$量子Kramers-Wannier对偶性（quantum Kramers-Wannier duality），提供了短程纠缠（short-range entangled, SRE）态与长程纠缠（long-range entangled, LRE）态之间的高效纯幺正转换路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子Kramers-Wannier对偶性是从短程纠缠态映射到长程纠缠态的基本变换，但空间局域幺正电路实现该对偶需要与系统大小成线性比例的深度。非局域连通性下的纯幺正电路能否突破这一速度极限，是一个未解决的根本问题。

Method: 显式构造了空间非局域的幺正电路，在空间一维和二维中实现了精确的$\mathbb{Z}_2$ KW对偶，并推广至任意$\mathbb{Z}_n$ KW对偶。这些电路实现的是完整的对偶映射，而非针对特定目标态的算法。

Result: 所构造的电路深度呈对数增长（logarithmic depth），远低于局域电路所需的线性深度。在对称（电荷中性）扇区内，该对偶可精确地将任意非不动点的短程纠缠态变换为其对应的长程纠缠对偶态。

Conclusion: 该结果建立了一条高效且纯相干（purely coherent）的路径，可用于在现代量子平台上探索相变（phase transitions）和拓扑对偶性（topological dualities）。

Abstract: The quantum Kramers-Wannier (KW) duality is a fundamental transformation mapping short-range entangled (SRE) states to long-range entangled (LRE) states. While spatially local unitary circuits require linear-in-system-size depth to implement this duality, the ultimate speed limit for purely unitary circuits equipped with nonlocal connectivity remains an open question. Here, we explicitly construct logarithmic depth, spatially nonlocal unitary circuits that realize the exact $\mathbb{Z}_2$ KW dualities in both one and two spatial dimensions. We further generalize the construction to arbitrary $\mathbb{Z}_n$ KW dualities. Unlike algorithms tailored to prepare specific target states, our circuits implement complete duality maps. Within the symmetric (charge-neutral) sector, these dualities exactly transform arbitrary non-fixed-point SRE states into their corresponding LRE duals. Consequently, our results establish an efficient, purely coherent pathway for exploring phase transitions and topological dualities on modern quantum platforms.
