*Chun Hei Leung*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过Bethe ansatz（贝特拟设）基矢方法，研究了与集体自旋跳跃算符（collective spin jump operators）环境耦合的自旋-1/2海森堡链（Heisenberg chain）中的无阻尼行为。结果表明，对于任意链长 N >= 3，系统均存在无阻尼模（undamped modes），这些模对系统参数（如集体耗散形式和外场）保持鲁棒性，并在开放可积量子系统（open integrable quantum systems）中展现出长寿命的相干动力学。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索开放量子系统中是否存在无阻尼动力学行为，以及这些行为在可积系统（integrable systems）中能否保持稳定。

Method: 采用Bethe ansatz（贝特拟设）基矢方法分析自旋-1/2海森堡链与环境的集体耗散耦合。

Result: 对于任意链长 N >= 3，系统均存在无阻尼模；这些模对集体耗散的具体形式和外场变化保持鲁棒性；进一步表征了无阻尼模的数量及其振荡频率。

Conclusion: 在开放可积量子系统中存在长寿命的相干动力学，表现为无阻尼模的稳定存在。

Abstract: We investigate the undamped behaviors in a spin-1/2 Heisenberg chain coupled with an environment via collective spin jump operators. Using the Bethe ansatz basis, we show that undamped modes exist for any chain length N >= 3. These modes remain robust against variations in the system parameters, including the specific form of the collective dissipation, and the external field. Exploiting the Bethe ansatz solution, we further characterize the number of undamped modes and their oscillation frequencies, uncovering long-lived coherent dynamics in open integrable quantum systems.

</details>


### [161] [Thermodynamics of Quantum Reservoir Computing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02157)
*Lixiang Ding,Xingze Qiu*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过非平衡态热力学（non-equilibrium thermodynamics）框架，将驱动开放量子系统（driven open quantum systems）的宏观预测性能（predictive performance）与微观能量成本（energetic costs）联系起来，证明了量子临界区域（quantum critical region）的计算峰值源于能隙闭合（energy gap closing）引发的严格频谱共振（spectral resonance），并揭示了最优预测能力与最大信息耗散（informational dissipation）之间存在的根本性热力学权衡（thermodynamic trade-off）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子储层计算（quantum reservoir computing）在处理复杂时间序列数据方面具有潜力，但其基本的计算极限和能量极限（energetic limits）尚不明确，缺乏统一的理论框架来理解性能与能耗之间的关系。

Method: 建立非平衡态热力学框架，将Holevo容量（Holevo capacities）映射到Bogoliubov-Kubo-Mori几何流形（geometric manifold）上，通过解析证明建立频谱共振条件；引入量子信息耗散（quantum informational dissipation）概念量化非预测性历史数据的结构保留，并利用相干性分解（coherence decomposition）分析动态量子相干性（dynamic quantum coherences）的作用。

Result: 解析证明了量子临界区域的计算峰值来源于严格频谱共振（能隙闭合迫使储层跃迁频率与混沌驱动对齐）；推导出连续时间处理的广义Landauer界限（generalized Landauer bound）；发现临界共振在实现最优预测能力的同时最大化信息耗散和不可逆擦除功（irreversible work）；证明了动态量子相干性可严格增强预测能力而不需要额外的机械功。

Conclusion: 这些发现建立了量子学习器件的最终能量极限，为设计节能的量子神经形态硬件（energy-efficient quantum neuromorphic hardware）提供了理论原则。

Abstract: Quantum reservoir computing provides a framework for processing complex temporal data, yet its fundamental computational and energetic limits remain unresolved. Here, we establish a non-equilibrium thermodynamic framework that links the macroscopic predictive performance of driven open quantum systems to their microscopic energetic costs. By mapping the Holevo capacities onto the Bogoliubov-Kubo-Mori geometric manifold, we analytically prove that the computational peak within the quantum critical region originates from a strict spectral resonance: the closing of the energy gap forces the reservoir's transition frequencies to align with the chaotic drive. To evaluate the associated thermodynamic costs, we introduce quantum informational dissipation to quantify the non-predictive historical data structurally retained by the reservoir, deriving a generalized Landauer bound for continuous temporal processing. This reveals a fundamental thermodynamic trade-off: the critical resonance that unlocks optimal predictive capacity inherently maximizes informational dissipation and the irreversible work required for environmental erasure. Furthermore, coherence decomposition demonstrates that dynamic quantum coherences strictly amplify predictive capacity without demanding additional mechanical work. These findings establish the ultimate energetic limits of quantum learning devices, providing theoretical principles for designing energy-efficient quantum neuromorphic hardware.

</details>


### [162] [Computable measures of fermionic non-Gaussianity from the covariance matrix](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02242)
*Poetri Sonya Tarabunga,Bernhard Jobst,Raúl Morral-Yepes,Marc Langer,Barbara Kraus,Frank Pollmann,Sheng-Hsuan Lin*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过发展费米子非高斯性（fermionic non-Gaussianity）的凸资源理论（convex resource theory），提出了两类可计算的纯费米子态度量：占据数熵（occupation number entropies）和自然轨道参与熵（natural-orbital participation entropies），分别用于下界约束非高斯门数量和上界约束经典模拟成本，从而为量子信息、凝聚态物理和量子化学中的费米子复杂性研究建立了统一的资源理论框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 费米子非高斯性是理解费米子量子系统计算复杂性的关键资源，但目前缺乏既易于计算又在操作上有意义的量化方法。

Method: 基于协方差矩阵（covariance matrix）的Williamson标准型，提出两类可计算度量：第一类为占据数Tsallis-α熵，第二类为自然轨道基（natural-orbital basis）下态振幅平方的Rényi-α熵；并证明其中一族成员在高斯协议（Gaussian protocols）下具有单调性。

Result: 证明了一个占据数熵族成员是高斯协议下单调的凸资源单调量（convex resource monotone），从而下界约束态制备所需的非高斯门数量；自然轨道参与熵则上界约束正交高斯基下的经典模拟成本。两类度量在稳定子态（stabilizer state）和平移不变态（translation-invariant state）中简化并展现额外结构。通过随机SWAP掺杂匹配门电路（random SWAP-doped matchgate circuits）和键调制XXZ模型（bond-modulated XXZ model）等实例验证了非高斯性在多体现象中的作用。

Conclusion: 建立了统一的费米子非高斯性资源理论框架，将量子信息、凝聚态物理和量子化学中的相关概念联系起来，为研究量子多体系统的复杂性开辟了新方向，并为评估费米子态的经典可模拟性提供了实用工具。

Abstract: Fermionic non-Gaussianity, or fermionic magic, is a key resource underlying the computational complexity of fermionic quantum systems, yet tractable and operationally meaningful ways to quantify it remain limited. We address this challenge by developing a convex resource theory of fermionic non-Gaussianity and introducing two families of computable measures for pure fermionic states, both derived from the Williamson normal form of the covariance matrix. The first family, occupation number entropies, is defined as the Tsallis-$α$ entropy of the occupation numbers. We prove that one member of this family is monotonic under Gaussian protocols, establishing it as a computable convex resource monotone. It consequently lower bounds the number of non-Gaussian gates needed for state preparation. The second family, natural-orbital participation entropies, is given by the Rényi-$α$ entropy of the squared amplitudes of the state in the natural-orbital basis, defined by the eigenvectors of the covariance matrix. These measures quantify state compressibility in this basis and thus upper bound the classical simulation cost in an orthonormal Gaussian basis. We analyze both families for stabilizer and translation-invariant states, where they simplify and reveal additional structure. We further study representative examples, including random SWAP-doped matchgate circuits and the bond-modulated XXZ model, highlighting the role of non-Gaussianity in many-body phenomena. Our work establishes a resource-theoretic framework for computable fermionic non-Gaussianity that unifies notions arising across quantum information, condensed-matter physics, and quantum chemistry, opening new directions for studying the complexity of quantum many-body systems and providing practical tools to assess the classical simulability of fermionic states relevant for quantum advantage.

</details>


### [163] [A transition-metal qubit in diamond with all-optical control and millisecond quantum memory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02258)
*I. M. Morris,T. Alberth,L. Crooks,T. Lühmann,D. J. Twitchen,S. Pezzagna,J. Meijer,S. S. Nicley,J. N. Becker*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文展示了过渡金属缺陷（transition-metal defects）——镍空位（NiV⁻）中心——作为一种可在金刚石中实现自旋-光子界面的新型量子比特平台，其同时具备自旋-轨道保护（spin-orbit protected）的基态相干性、全光学控制（all-optical control）和近红外发射（near-infrared emission）特性，在1.65 K下实现超过1毫秒的相干时间，并通过全光动态解耦（all-optical dynamical decoupling）将相干时间从371 ns延长至1.27 ms。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子网络（quantum network）要求量子比特同时具备高效光学接入、相干控制和长寿命量子存储，但现有金刚石色心（diamond color center）平台在这三者之间存在权衡，尚未实现可扩展的统一解决方案。

Method: 采用单个镍空位（NiV⁻）中心作为自旋量子比特，在1.65 K温度下利用全光学手段实现Raman拉比振荡（Raman Rabi oscillations）和Ramsey干涉测量（Ramsey interferometry），并施加全光动态解耦序列延长相干时间。

Result: 实现了相干时间超过1毫秒的金刚石自旋量子比特；通过全光动态解耦将相干时间从T₂* = 371 ns提升至T₂^(CPMG-4) = 1.27 ms，提升了超过三个数量级。

Conclusion: NiV⁻中心被确立为一种可部署（deployable）的金刚石自旋-光子界面（spin-photon interface），为超越现有金刚石色心平台的量子网络应用提供了新的路径。

Abstract: Quantum networks require qubits that combine efficient optical access, coherent control, and long-lived quantum memory, but realizing all three in one scalable platform remains a central bottleneck. Diamond color centers are leading candidates, yet widely studied defects retain tradeoffs among these capabilities. Here, we show that transition-metal defects in diamond provide a distinct route beyond these platforms by combining spin-orbit protected ground-state coherence, all-optical control, and near-infrared emission. Using a single nickel-vacancy (NiV$^-$), we demonstrate an all-optically controlled diamond spin qubit with coherence exceeding one millisecond at 1.65 K, compatible with compact closed-cycle cryogenics. We implement Raman Rabi oscillations and Ramsey interferometry and use all-optical dynamical decoupling to extend coherence from $T_2^*$ = 371 ns to $T_2^{CPMG-4}$ = 1.27 ms, establishing NiV$^-$ as a deployable diamond spin-photon interface.

### [164] [Quantum mutual information as a robust probe of integrability in open quantum systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02462)
*Nirupam Sen,Keshav Das Agarwal,Aditi Sen De*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出基于Haar平均总关联和（aSTC）与平均真多体纠缠作为量子信息加扰（scrambling）的稳健探针，通过在长程量子XYZ自旋模型中的数值实验，证明aSTC的时间涨落能忠实且系统尺寸无关地标志可积与混沌动力学，并在非马尔可夫环境下保持区分能力，甚至在弱马尔可夫区域超越离时有序关联子（OTOC）的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子系统的动力学可反映哈密顿量是可积（integrable）还是混沌（chaotic）的特征，这通过量子信息加扰体现。现有加扰探针（如OTOC）存在局限性，因此需要发展更稳健且系统尺寸无关的信息论框架来区分可积与混沌动力学。

Method: 提出基于Haar平均总关联和（aSTC）与从初始完全可分态动态生成的平均真多体纠缠（genuine multipartite entanglement）作为量子信息加扰的探针。以长程量子XYZ自旋模型在横纵磁场中的动力学为例，其可积极限为近邻横场XY模型，考察aSTC与OTOC的长时平均和时域涨落。

Result: aSTC的时间涨落能忠实且系统尺寸无关地标志可积与混沌动力学，与OTOC效果类似。在马尔可夫（Markovian）热浴耦合下，仅在中间时间能区分可积与混沌；在非马尔可夫（non-Markovian）域，信息回流恢复加扰动力学，aSTC在长时间仍保持区分能力。在弱马尔可夫振幅阻尼与非马尔可夫退相位噪声下，aSTC的时域涨落能在OTOC失效时仍区分可积性与非可积性。

Conclusion: aSTC及其时域涨落是一种不依赖系统尺寸的、有效的量子信息加扰探针，能在多种噪声环境中（尤其是OTOC失效的情况下）区分可积与混沌动力学。

Abstract: The dynamics of a quantum system encode signatures of whether the underlying Hamiltonian is integrable or chaotic, giving rise to the concept of quantum information scrambling through the properties of the resulting dynamical states or operators. We introduce an information-theoretic framework based on the Haar-averaged sum of total correlations (aSTC), together with average genuine multipartite entanglement generated dynamically from initially fully separable states, as robust probes of quantum information scrambling. Using the long-range quantum XYZ spin model in transverse and longitudinal magnetic fields, whose integrable limit is the nearest-neighbor transverse XY model, we demonstrate that the long-time average and, more importantly, the temporal fluctuations of the aSTC provide a faithful and system-size-independent signature of integrable and chaotic dynamics, similar to the conventional measure of scrambling, out-of-time-ordered correlator (OTOC). When the system is in contact with the thermal reservoir and system-bath coupling follows Markovianity, we find that the fluctuations of the aSTC and OTOC continue to distinguish integrable and chaotic dynamics only at intermediate times. However, we observe that in the non-Markovian domain, information backflow restores the scrambling dynamics, enabling the aSTC to retain its distinguishing power even at long times. Interestingly, we exhibit that, under Markovian amplitude damping and non-Markovian dephasing noise, the temporal fluctuations of the aSTC can discriminate between integrability and non-integrability in the weak Markovian regime, even when OTOC fails to do so.

</details>

Result: 该方法在计算上具有显著效率，能以较低计算资源提取广泛的共形场论数据，并揭示了三维共形场论与非对易几何（noncommutative geometry）及量子霍尔效应（quantum Hall effect）之间的意外联系。

Abstract: This review discusses the recently proposed fuzzy sphere regularization for studying $2+1$D critical phenomena, particularly three-dimensional (3D) conformal field theory (CFT). We introduce the fundamental ideas of fuzzy sphere regularization, emphasizing its role in demonstrating the state-operator correspondence of 3D CFTs on the $S^2 \times \mathbb{R}$ geometry. ### [166] [First passage time for an underdamped harmonic oscillator and application to the power of an information engine](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01404)
*Aubin Archambault,Caroline Crauste-Thibierge,Alberto Imparato,Sergio Ciliberto,Ludovic Bellon*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过结合Kramers微分算子的特征值分析与短时Hamilton近似，推导了欠阻尼谐振子首次通过时间（first passage time）分布的解析表达式，并通过微悬臂梁实验验证了理论预测，进一步将该分布应用于信息引擎（information engines）功率的精确估计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 欠阻尼简谐振子（underdamped harmonic oscillator）中，位置x越过阈值x_B的首次通过时间t_fp的完整分布尚未被精确解析，而该分布对理解随机动力学（stochastic dynamics）及设计基于涨落的信息引擎具有重要意义。

Method: 采用三种方法的综合策略：在中长时间尺度上求解Kramers微分算子（Kramers differential operator）的本征值；在短时间尺度上使用Hamilton近似（Hamiltonian approximation）处理；最后将两种尺度的结果拼接，得到完整的首次通过时间分布。

Result: 理论计算得到的t_fp分布与欠阻尼微悬臂梁（micro-cantilever）实验的观测结果高度一致；同时，基于该分布实现了对信息引擎功率的精确估算，并通过实验验证。

Conclusion: 所建立的首次通过时间分布理论框架不仅与实验吻合，还为信息引擎等应用场景提供了精确的功率估计方法，展现了该方法在随机热力学（stochastic thermodynamics）中的实用价值。

Abstract: The distribution of the first passage time $t_{fp}$ for the position $x$ to overcome a threshold $x_B$ is calculated in an underdamped harmonic oscillator. The proof combines several approaches based on the determination of the eigenvalues of the Kramers differential operator for the intermediate and long time regimes and on a Hamiltonian approximation for the short times. The theoretical predictions are in excellent agreement with the results of an experiment on an underdamped micro-cantilever. The knowledge of the $t_{fp}$ distribution opens the way to several applications, among them the precise estimation of the power of information engines, which we have also experimentally checked.

### [167] [First passage time distribution in underdamped harmonic oscillators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.01405)
*Aubin Archambault,Caroline Crauste-Thibierge,Alberto Imparato,Sergio Ciliberto,Ludovic Bellon*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文推导了欠阻尼谐振子（underdamped harmonic oscillator）越过阈值x_B的首通时间（first passage time）分布，针对不同品质因子Q采用不同方法，并揭示了平均轨迹的特定形状。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 分析欠阻尼谐振子首通时间分布，特别是该分布对品质因子Q的依赖关系，以及不同Q区间所需的不同理论处理方法。

Method: 对于极高Q（Q≫100）的中长t_fp，采用能量扩散模型（energy diffusion model）；对于中等Q（Q∼10），基于Kramers线性微分算子在吸收边界条件下的特征值分析；对于所有Q下的短t_fp，采用哈密顿近似（Hamiltonian approximation）。

Result: 理论预测与直接数值模拟结果高度一致。此外，在t_fp时刻结束的轨迹均值呈现由特定噪声模式驱动的特殊形状。

Conclusion: 所提出的分段理论方法能够准确刻画不同Q区间下欠阻尼谐振子的首通时间分布，且轨迹均值存在由噪声模式决定的特殊形态。

Abstract: We derive the distribution of the first passage time $t_{fp}$ for the position $x$ of an underdamped harmonic oscillator to overcome a threshold $x_B$. As the $t_{fp}$ distribution depends on the oscillator quality factor $Q$ different approaches are used. At very large quality factor ($Q\gg 100$) and intermediate and long $t_{fp}$ the proof is based on an energy diffusion model, whereas at medium quality factor ($Q\sim 10$) the proof is based on the study of the eigenvalues of the Kramers linear differential operator with absorbing boundary conditions. For all $Q$ and short $t_{fp}$ we use a Hamiltonian approximation. The theoretical predictions are in excellent agreement with direct numerical simulations of underdamped oscillator dynamics. Finally we show that the mean of the trajectories ending at $t_{fp}$ presents a particular shape driven by a specific noise pattern.

</details>


### [168] [Sandpile Models on complex networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02023)
*Komlan Fiagbe,Jean-François de Kemmeter,Timoteo Carletti*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过建立包含耗散效应的分支过程（branching-process）框架，分析了复杂网络上的沙堆模型（sandpile model），揭示了耗散、聚类和稀疏连接如何根本性地重塑雪崩大小分布，并指出了经典分支近似的定量局限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典分支过程描述假设保守输运（conservative transport）和局域树状独立性（locally tree-like independence），忽略雪崩传播中的颗粒损失（grain-loss）效应。本文旨在引入耗散机制，研究其对复杂网络上雪崩动力学（avalanche dynamics）的定量影响。

Method: 在分支过程框架中显式引入耗散，将颗粒损失效应直接纳入子代分布（offspring distribution），构建耗散雪崩动力学的广义生成函数（generalized generating functions）。在稀疏随机网络和Holme-Kim聚类无标度网络（clustered scale-free networks）上进行数值模拟验证。

Result: 耗散使雪崩大小分布（avalanche-size distributions）呈现指数截断（exponential cutoffs），同时保留拓扑依赖的标度行为（topology-dependent scaling behavior）。在聚类无标度网络中，聚类系数增加会持续降低雪崩指数并增大大规模级联概率；树状网络上因低边密度和大量叶节点限制雪崩传播，也显著偏离幂律分布。

Conclusion: 耗散、聚类和稀疏连接从根本上改变了网络上沙堆模型的雪崩大小分布，建立了分支过程描述雪崩动力学的定量极限，表明短环（short cycles）产生的强相关性使经典独立分支近似失效。

Abstract: We investigate the sandpile model on complex networks by developing a branching-process framework that explicitly incorporates dissipation during avalanche propagation. Unlike classical branching descriptions, which assume conservative transport and locally tree-like independence, the present approach introduces grain-loss effects directly into the offspring distribution, yielding generalized generating functions for dissipative avalanche dynamics. In the dissipative regime, avalanche-size distributions acquire exponential cutoffs while preserving topology-dependent scaling behavior. Numerical simulations confirm the theoretical predictions on sparse random networks and reveal systematic deviations in highly structured topologies. In particular, by using Holme-Kim clustered scale-free networks, we show that increasing clustering continuously lowers the avalanche exponent and enhances the probability of large cascades, demonstrating that short cycles generate strong correlations that invalidate the classical independent-branch approx imation. Surprisingly, trees also exhibit substantial deviations from power-law because low edge density and the abundance of leaves constrain avalanche propagation. These results show that dissipation, clustering, and sparse connectivity fundamentally reshape avalanche size distribution of the sandpile model on networks and establish quantitative limits for branching-process descriptions of avalanche dynamics.

### [169] [Path-Measure Dynamics of Attention-Driven World Models: A Nonlocal Onsager--Machlup Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02154)
*Gunn Kim*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究注意力机制（attention）引入记忆后，潜变量动力学（latent dynamics）失去马尔可夫性（Markovian），对应的预测路径测度（predictive path measure）可投影为隐藏的线性马尔可夫增广（hidden linear Markov augmentation）。消除辅助场后得到非局域（nonlocal）Onsager-Machlup作用量，其记忆核完全单调（completely monotone），与有限弛豫谱（finite relaxation spectrum）的隐马尔可夫嵌入精确匹配。通过尺度分离参数展开，证明局域作用量是非局域理论的短记忆极限。

Result: 非局域作用量中的记忆核是完全单调的，与有限弛豫谱的隐马尔可夫嵌入精确匹配；否则动力学本质上是非局域的。尺度分离展开的首项恢复配套论文的局域作用量，建立局域性作为短记忆极限的地位。

Conclusion: 注意力引入的记忆使动力学在一般情况下是非局域的，但若记忆核满足完全单调性，则可等价嵌入隐马尔可夫过程；局域Onsager-Machlup理论是更一般非局域理论的短记忆近似。

Abstract: Attention enables a world model to condition on its entire history, providing long-term memory that facilitates long-range predictions. While the local Onsager--Machlup theory in our companion paper assumes a temporally local predictive action, we investigate the conditions under which this locality holds. We derive the predictive path measure for latent dynamics that become non-Markovian due to attention-induced memory, demonstrating that this measure is the projection of a hidden linear Markov augmentation. Eliminating the auxiliary field results in a nonlocal Onsager--Machlup action, where memory manifests as a nonlocal quadratic form rather than a force. These kernels are completely monotone and exactly match a hidden Markov embedding with a finite relaxation spectrum; otherwise, the dynamics remain fundamentally nonlocal. By expanding the action in terms of the scale-separation parameter $ε=τ_{\text{mem}}/τ_{\text{dyn}}$, we show that the leading order recovers the local action of the companion paper, establishing locality as the short-memory limit of a nonlocal theory. We verify the reversible sector of this expansion term by term against an exactly solvable vector linear model.

Abstract: We investigate homogeneous populations of smart active agents that exchange information with their neighbors to perform a decentralized learning process aimed at achieving a prescribed macroscopic state. Such agents may, for example, represent simple microrobots. The exchanged information comprises tunable parameters governing the agent dynamics, referred to as the individual policy, together with an internal memory encoding previously visited states. This memory is used to evaluate a reward that quantifies the success of a policy to achieve the prescribed state. We extend the kinetic-theory description of collective learning in spatially homogeneous systems [Phys. Rev. Lett. 134, 248302 (2025)] and derive formal evolution equations for the distribution of policies across the population. A central outcome of our theory is the emergence of an effective reward function that fully determines the evolution of the policy distribution and encapsulates the microscopic details of the agents physical and memory dynamics. We obtain closed equations for the policy mean and variance which admit explicit time-dependent solutions under the assumption of Gaussian-distributed memories and polices.
  To illustrate the framework, we present a series of minimal microscopic models, considering both perfect and partial separation of physical, memory and policy exchange time scales, as well as models with one- and two-dimensional policies. The obtained theoretical results compare well with agent-based numerical simulations. The theory captures key aspects of collective learning, including the influence of population diversity and reward fluctuations on learning performance. *Andrea Mazzolini,Leonardo Agasso,Filippo Valle,Michele Caselle,Marco Cosentino Lagomarsino,Matteo Osella*

TL;DR: 论文发现，复杂组件系统（如语言、基因组、乐高）的多样性增长普遍服从次线性标度律及其方差-均值平方关系，并证明这些宏观律可以从两种不同机制——创新驱动的增长模型与蕴含潜在异质性（latent heterogeneity）的统计模型——中推导出来，表明经验数据虽然能约束生成模型，但无法唯一识别底层机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管语言、技术制品、基因组和基因表达模式等多种复杂系统中，不同组件的数量随系统规模次线性增长，且方差大致正比于均值的平方，这些普遍规律被视为创新机制的标志，但支持这些规律涌现的基本条件仍不清楚，因此需要探究是否存在一般性约束或涌现原理来刻画具有不同组件数量的系统架构。

Method: 首先在一类增长模型（growth model）中推导出两种多样性定律联合涌现的解析条件，揭示创新概率（innovation probability）对多样性（diversity）和系统规模（system size）的特定渐近依赖关系；随后在另一类具有潜在异质性（latent heterogeneity）的模型中展示相同的宏观定律，利用总方差定律（law of total variance）证明二次波动标度的渐近涌现，无需显式假设创新机制或特定组装规则；最后将预测与语言、基因组、乐高构建以及大语言模型（large language model）生成文本的经验数据进行比较。

Result: 实证多样性标度律对生成模型施加了强约束，但无法唯一确定产生多样性的机制；创新驱动增长模型与潜在变量描述之间存在密切对应关系。

Conclusion: 经验多样性标度律虽然能约束可能的生成模型，但仅靠这些宏观规律不足以区分驱动多样性产生的具体机制，增长模型与潜在变量模型在宏观层面上具有等价性。

Abstract: Remarkably common statistical laws characterize the diversity scaling and its fluctuations across a wide range of complex "component systems". These regularities are often interpreted as signatures of an underlying innovation mechanism driving the growth of component diversity, but the basic ingredients necessary for their emergence remain poorly understood. In particular, from language and technological artifacts to genomes and gene expression patterns, the number of distinct components grows sublinearly with system size, while its variance scales approximately as the square of its mean. This behavior is consistent across diverse systems, raising the question of whether general constraints or emergent principles underlying diversity and innovation define the architectures of realizations with different numbers of components. To address this question, we derive analytical conditions for the joint emergence of these two diversity laws within a broad class of growth models, showing that they require a specific asymptotic dependence of the innovation probability on diversity and system size. We then demonstrate that the same macroscopic laws arise in a different class of models with latent heterogeneity, where quadratic fluctuation scaling always emerges asymptotically as a consequence of general statistical principles, essentially the law of total variance, without explicitly assuming an innovation mechanism or any specific rule for system assembly. We compare these predictions with empirical data from language, genomes, LEGO constructions, and texts generated by large language models. Our results show that empirical diversity scaling laws strongly constrain generative models but do not uniquely identify the mechanisms generating diversity, revealing a close correspondence between innovation-driven growth models and latent-variable descriptions.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 选择一个简单模型系统，其平均力势可用低阶多项式（low-order polynomial）良好近似；推导该模型的严格广义朗之万方程，并分析其中除线性记忆项之外的高阶记忆项对动力学的影响。

Result: 该模型系统的严格广义朗之万方程中包含除线性记忆项之外的额外记忆项。这些额外的高阶记忆项对动力学具有重要影响，不能忽略。

Conclusion: 如果意图正确模拟底层微观系统的核心动力学特征，非线性记忆项不可忽略。这意味着常用的三性质广义朗之万方程在描述系统核心动力学时存在本质局限。

Abstract: If a generalized Langevin equation contains a potential of mean force, it cannot at the same time contain a linear memory kernel and a fluctuating force that obeys a second fluctuation dissipation theorem in the sense of Kubo, and be exact. As modelers often prefer to use generalized Langevin equations that have the first three properties, one needs to ask how close the model dynamics is to the dynamics of the underlying microscopic system. To test this, we analyze a simple model system in which the potential of mean force can be well approximated by a polynomial of low order. The exact generalized Langevin equation of this model contains memory terms in addition to the linear one. We show that these additional terms, at least for the model system regarded in this article, are important for the dynamics and cannot be neglected if one intends to model core aspects of the underlying system correctly.

### [174] [Velocity and force autocorrelations in Brownian dynamics with a Lorentz force](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02282)
*Filippo Faedi,Abhinav Sharma*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文推导了外磁场中布朗粒子的速度自相关张量（VACT）与力自相关张量（FACT）之间的普适关系，并发现过阻尼极限下VACT中控制自扩散的部分与FACT的反对称部分耦合，耦合强度由回旋频率与热化率之比决定。通过可精确求解的带电粒子二聚体模型，验证了磁场可导致不同的扩散行为：要么是完全可恢复的瞬态抑制，要么是持续的振荡和长期自扩散抑制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究外磁场中布朗粒子的速度与力自相关张量之间的普适关系，探寻该关系是否依赖于相互作用势的具体细节，并理解磁场对自扩散行为的影响机制。

Method: 利用时间对称性（time-symmetry）论证，从完整的朗之万动力学（Langevin dynamics）出发，推导VACT与FACT之间的普遍关系。在热化与相互作用驱动运动的时间尺度分离假设下，将该关系简化为过阻尼（overdamped）极限形式。通过一个可精确求解的简谐束缚带电粒子二聚体模型进行验证。

Result: VACT仅依赖于FACT，与相互作用势的具体细节无关。过阻尼极限下，控制自扩散的VACT部分与FACT的反对称部分耦合，耦合强度为回旋频率（cyclotron frequency）与热化率（thermalization rate）之比。模型验证发现：电荷同号时，磁场产生可完全恢复的瞬态迁移率与扩散抑制；电荷异号时，出现持续的振荡力自相关、负迁移率区域以及长期自扩散抑制。

Conclusion: 建立了外磁场中布朗运动VACT与FACT之间的普适理论框架，揭示了磁场通过反对称力自相关影响自扩散的新机制，并展示了不同电荷符号组合下磁场对输运行为截然不同的调控效应。

Abstract: We derive a general relation between the velocity and force autocorrelation tensors (VACT and FACT) for a Brownian particle subject to an external magnetic field. Using time-symmetry arguments, we show that, for the full Langevin dynamics, the VACT depends only on the FACT, independently of the details of the interaction potential. Under the hypothesis of timescale separation between thermalization and interaction-driven motion, this relation simplifies considerably in the overdamped (Brownian) limit. A central feature of the overdamped result is that, unlike in the field-free case, the part of the VACT that controls the self-diffusion of the particle couples to the antisymmetric part of the FACT, with a coupling strength set by the ratio of the cyclotron frequency to the thermalization rate. We validate and illustrate the formalism on an exactly solvable model: a dimer of charged particles bound by a harmonic potential. Depending on the relative sign of the particle charges, the magnetic field is found to produce either a transient suppression of mobility and diffusion that is fully recovered at long times, or a persistent oscillatory force autocorrelation, regions of negative mobility, and a
  long-time suppression of self-diffusion.

### [175] [Contrarian Majority Dynamics: Violation of Detailed Balance and Nonequilibrium Steady States](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02358)
*Serge Galam*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文从统计力学视角重新审视带反对者（contrarian agents）的Galam多数模型（GMM），揭示了三个基本特征：构建了马尔可夫单粒子随机动力学；证明GMM的确定性演化方程并非平均场近似的结果，而是一种迭代平均场动力学；发现单粒子和同步更新均破坏细致平衡，但同步更新在科尔莫戈罗夫循环条件上更强烈地偏离平衡，证实平稳态为真正的非平衡稳态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建与GMM同步更新等价的单粒子随机动力学（single-agent stochastic dynamics），提供马尔可夫表示；推导常规平均场近似下的动力学方程并与GMM方程对比；利用细致平衡条件、科尔莫戈罗夫循环条件以及平稳态概率流计算分析动力学的热力学性质。

Result: 单粒子动力学与同步更新产生相同的演化方程；GMM的确定性方程并非平均场近似的结果，而是一种迭代平均场动力学；两种更新方式均破坏细致平衡，但同步更新还违背科尔莫戈罗夫循环条件，偏离平衡更强；平稳态概率流非零，确认不存在有效哈密顿量，平稳态为真正的非平衡稳态。

Conclusion: 反对者多数动力学本质上是一个非平衡过程，具有不同程度的不可逆性；反对者不应被视为热噪声，该模型不能归约为平衡态统计力学框架。

Abstract: I revisit the Galam Majority Model (GMM) with contrarian agents from a statistical-mechanics perspective, revealing three fundamental features. First, in addition to the GMM simultaneous-update of small discussion groups, I construct a related single-agent stochastic dynamics, providing a Markovian microscopic representation, which is found to yield the same evolution equation. Second, I show that, contrary to what is often stated in the literature, the GMM closed evolution equation for the opinion density is not the result of a mean-field approximation. Indeed, I derive the conventional mean-field dynamics associated with majority-rule interactions and show that it yields a distinct, probabilistic evolution equation contrary the deterministic GMM equation. I therefore identify the GMM as an iterated mean-field dynamics. Third, I investigate the thermodynamic nature of the dynamics obtained from both single-agent and simultaneous updates. Both are shown to violate detailed balance. However, while Kolmogorov's cycle condition is satisfied for single-agent updates, it is violated for simultaneous updates, making the departure from equilibrium stronger in the latter case. I then compute the probability flux in the stationary state and show that it is non-vanishing, confirming the absence of an effective Hamiltonian and establishing that the stationary state is a genuine nonequilibrium steady state.These results clarify the statistical-mechanical foundations of the GMM and establish contrarian majority dynamics as an intrinsically non-equilibrium process with distinct regimes of irreversibility. Contrarians are not thermal noise.

</details>


### [176] [Correlation and entanglement dynamics of free fermions in disguise](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02359)
*Dávid Szász-Schagrin,Pablo Bayona-Pena,Lorenzo Piroli,Eric Vernier*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究了一类可通过映射到“伪装自由费米子（free fermions in disguise）”求解的自旋链中的量子淬火（quantum quench）非平衡动力学。针对此类模型所有本征值指数简并的特性，作者发展了计算广义吉布斯系综（generalized Gibbs ensemble, GGE）准动量分布的解析方法，并提出了准粒子图像下纠缠增长公式的修正猜想。数值张量网络计算验证了局域可观测量预测的准确性，而纠缠动力学存在微小偏差，表明该猜想仅为近似正确。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此类自旋链模型的所有能量本征值均具有指数简并（exponential degeneracy），这一特性对现有可积系统非平衡动力学理论框架的有效性提出了根本性质疑。因此，需要检验并扩展该框架以涵盖这类伪装自由费米子系统。

Method: 首先，发展了一套解析方法计算描述广义吉布斯系综（GGE）的准动量分布函数（quasi-momentum distribution function），并导出对特殊可观测量期望值的解析公式。其次，基于准粒子图像（quasi-particle picture），考虑每个伪装自由费米子因能量本征值指数简并而携带额外熵，提出标准纠缠增长公式的修正猜想。最后，通过张量网络（tensor-network）数值计算对不同初态和哈密顿量参数下的理论预测进行检验。

Result: 对于局域可观测量（local observables），理论预测与数值结果吻合极好。对于纠缠动力学（entanglement dynamics），理论预测与数值结果存在微小偏差，表明所提出的修正猜想仅为近似正确。

Conclusion: 该工作是将可积系统非平衡动力学现有框架扩展到包含伪装自由费米子模型的第一步，为处理具有简并能谱的可积系统提供了新的解析工具和理论见解。

Abstract: We study the nonequilibrium dynamics following a quantum quench in spin chains that can be solved via a mapping to free fermions in disguise. These models feature an exponential degeneracy of all energy eigenvalues, raising the question of the validity of the established framework describing the properties of integrable systems out of equilibrium. We present two main results. First, we develop an analytic method to compute the quasi-momentum distribution function characterizing the generalized Gibbs ensemble, and derive an analytic formula to compute the corresponding expectation values for special observables. Second, we conjecture a modification of the standard formula for the entanglement growth based on the quasi-particle picture, taking into account that each fermion in disguise carries an additional amount of entropy due to the exponential degeneracy of the energy eigenvalues. We test our theoretical predictions against numerical tensor-network computations for different initial states and Hamiltonian parameters. For the local observables, we find excellent agreement. For the entanglement dynamics, we find small deviations suggesting that our conjecture is only approximately correct. Our results represent a first step towards the extension of the established framework of integrable systems out of equilibrium to models hosting free fermions in disguise.

</details>


### [177] [On the emergence of quantum many-body chaos for tunably-broken integrability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02506)
*Sounak Biswas,Sthitadhi Roy,Roderich Moessner*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过可调参数打破可积性，在自由费米子电路中掺杂可积性破缺门（integrability-breaking gates），建立了量子多体混沌（quantum many-body chaos）涌现的定量理论。利用时序外关联子（out-of-time-ordered correlators, OTOCs）揭示了从早期可积行为到晚期混沌的交叉微观机制，识别了特征时间尺度、长度尺度以及蝴蝶速度（butterfly velocity）等混沌OTOC特性对破缺参数的依赖关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解量子多体混沌如何随可积性破缺而涌现，并建立从可积到混沌交叉的微观定量理论。

Method: 在自由费米子（free fermions）电路模型中，通过可调密度掺杂可积性破缺门作为时空局域热点（hotspot），利用OTOC分析从可积到混沌的交叉过程。

Result: 可积性破缺门作为局域热点局域放大OTOC，其累积效应最终导致完全混沌；识别了控制交叉的特征时间尺度与长度尺度，并给出了蝴蝶速度和波前展宽（front broadening）对破缺参数的依赖关系。

Conclusion: 建立了可积性破缺驱动量子多体混沌涌现的定量理论，揭示了从可积到混沌交叉的微观机制与关键尺度。

Abstract: We develop a quantitative theory for the emergence of quantum many-body chaos as integrability is broken via a tunable parameter. In a circuit model of free fermions, 'doped' with a tunable density of integrability-breaking gates, we uncover the microscopic mechanisms underpinning the crossover from early-time integrable behaviour to late-time chaos through the lens of the out-of-time-ordered correlators (OTOCs). The integrability-breaking gates act as local, in spacetime, hotspots which locally amplify the OTOCs such that an accumulation of them eventually leads to fully-developed chaos. We identify the explicit characteristic time and length scales governing this crossover, as well as the dependence of the chaotic OTOC characteristics -- such as the butterfly velocity and front broadening -- on the integrability-breaking parameter.

</details>

### [178] [Unitriangular R-matrices of quantum affine algebras and Yangians via Theta series](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02287)
*Huafeng Zhang*

Main category: math.QA

TL;DR: 本文给出了量子仿射代数（quantum affine algebra）的单位三角R矩阵（unitriangular R-matrices）的共轭公式，将其与Frenkel-Hernandez的T级数（T-series）及先前引入的Theta级数（Theta series）联系起来，并将该公式推广到了Yangian情形。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子仿射代数的普适R矩阵（universal R-matrix）可分解为上单位三角、阿贝尔（abelian）和下单位三角三部分，但单位三角R矩阵的具体形式与表示之间的关系尚需简化。

Method: 通过共轭公式（conjugation formula）对单位三角R矩阵进行重新表达，其中一个张量因子在量子仿射代数的任意有限维表示（finite-dimensional representation）上求值；公式中利用了Frenkel-Hernandez的T级数和先前工作中引入的Theta级数。对于Yangian情形，进一步借助移位Yangian（shifted Yangians）的三重张量积表示的结合子（associators）实现推广。

Result: 得到了一个简洁的单位三角R矩阵共轭公式，并将该公式成功推广至Yangian情形。

Conclusion: 提供的共轭公式为理解量子仿射代数与Yangian的单位三角R矩阵结构提供了简洁的表达方式，为进一步研究相关可积系统（integrable systems）和表示论（representation theory）奠定了基础。

Abstract: The universal R-matrix of the quantum affine algebra associated to a finite-dimensional simple complex Lie algebra admits a Gauss decomposition into an uper unitriangular part, an abelian part, and a lower unitriangular part. In this paper, we provide a simple conjugation formula for the unitriangular R-matrices with one tensor factor evaluated at an arbitrary finite-dimensional representation of the quantum affine algebra. Our formula involves the T-series of Frenkel--Hernandez and the Theta series introduced in a previous work.
  We also extend our conjugation formula to the Yangian case, making use of associators for triple tensor product representations of shifted Yangians.

</details>

### [179] [Pressure-drop localization and momentum insulation in liquid-gas coexistence Poiseuille flow](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.02310)
*Naoko Nakagawa,Shin-ichi Sasa*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本文研究了液-气共存状态下单组分流体在绝热板间的压力驱动泊肃叶流，发现共存泊肃叶流中存在极小的无量纲参数（源于微观-宏观长度比的平方），导致压差集中于界面区域、粒子流大幅减小，并在等温储层条件下产生界面冷却效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 液-气共存体系中的压力驱动流动是理解界面传热与传质耦合机制的关键问题，但共存态下泊肃叶流（Poiseuille flow）的行为尚不明确，尤其是界面区域对压力梯度和粒子流的重新分配效应有待揭示。

Method: 基于体相区域中的泊肃叶流和傅里叶热传导（Fourier heat conduction），结合粒子守恒与能量守恒方程，推导出描述共存泊肃叶流的极小无量纲参数$A^\mathrm{L}$和$A^\mathrm{G}$，这些参数的小量性来自微观-宏观长度比的平方。

Result: 在弱驱动且液相与气相处于宏观尺度时，压力差集中于界面区域，常规的泊肃叶粒子流受到显著抑制；当储层温度相等时，残余的粒子流会导致界面冷却（interfacial cooling）。

Conclusion: 液-气共存显著改变了泊肃叶流的压力分布与粒子输运特性，界面区域成为压力降的主要承载部位，且残余流动会引发局域热效应，这对多相微流控系统和界面热管理具有潜在指导意义。

Abstract: We study pressure-driven Poiseuille flow of a one-component fluid between adiabatic plates in liquid-gas coexistence. The analysis uses Poiseuille flow and Fourier heat conduction in the bulk regions together with particle and energy conservation. From these bulk equations, we identify extremely small dimensionless parameters $A^\mathrm{L}$ and $A^\mathrm{G}$ describing coexistence Poiseuille flow, whose smallness comes from squared microscopic-to-macroscopic length ratios. In weak driving with macroscopic liquid and gas regions, the pressure difference is concentrated across the interfacial region, and the ordinary Poiseuille particle current is strongly reduced. For equal-temperature reservoirs, this residual particle current produces interfacial cooling.

</details>
